⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

           ♦ SURAH YUSUF ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1587)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

الۤرۚ تِلۡكَ ءَایَـٰتُ ٱلۡكِتَـٰبِ ٱلۡمُبِینِ * إِنَّاۤ أَنزَلۡنَـٰهُ قُرۡءَ ٰ⁠ نًا عَرَبِیࣰّا لَّعَلَّكُمۡ تَعۡقِلُونَ.

"Alim, Laam, Raa! Ye Kitab e Mubeen (Clear Book) ki Ayaat (Signs) hain. Hamne ise Qur'an bana kar Arabi Zabaan mein nazil kiya hai, taake tum ise achhi tarah se samajh sako."

(Surah Yusuf: 1 - 2)

https://youtu.be/rpymJzfL6x4

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Allah Ta'ala ne Surah Yunus mein Qur'an Majeed ko 'Qur'an e Hakeem' ke Alfaaz se yaad kiya aur Surah Yusuf mein is 'Kitab e Mubeen' ke Naam se yaad kiya hai. Iske wujuhaat ye hain:

(1) Qur'an e Majeed Muhammad Mustafa (saww) ki Nabuwwat ka zabardast Mo'jaza hai isliye ye 'Mubeen' hai. Qur'an mein Mo'ajza ko 'Bayyanah' ke alfaaz se zikr kiya hai.

(2) Is Kitab mein Rushd o Hidayat (Guidance) ki nishadahi ki gayi hai aur Halaal o Haraam ki Tafseel bayan ki gayi hai. Bayan means clear explanation.

(3) Qur'an mein Awwalin (earlier) ke waqeaat bayan kiye gaye hain aur unke halaat ki tafseel bayan ki gayi hai.

(Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Imam Mohd Baqir (as):

"Chand cheezen Aurton ke liye na-Munasib hain. Aurton par Azaan nahi hai aur unhe Surah Yusuf nahi padhna chahiye. Is Surah mein Allah Ta'ala ne ye bayan kiya hai ke jo Insaan Khuloos e Dil ke saath Baargah e Khuda Wandi mein jhuk jaye to Allah Ta'ala us par khusoosi Shafqat karta hai aur qadam qadam par uski Rahnumai karta hai. Zahiri halaat khwah kitne hi na-muafiq hon aur hawadis e zamana uski zillat o halakat ke darpay hon, magar Allah Ta'ala us Oje Kamaal par pahuncha deta hai aur tamam mukhalifon ki mukhalifaten aur Hasedeen ka Hasad uska kuchh bhi nahi bigad sakta. Is haqeeqat ke amali izhaar ke liye Allah Ta'ala ne Hazrat Yusuf (as) ka haseen Qissa bayan kiya."

Qur'an Kareem mein agarche bahut se Anbiya ke waqeaat bayan kiye gaye hain lekin jis tafseel ke saath ek hi jagah par Hazrat Yusuf (as) ka Qissa bayan kiya gaya hai us tarah se kisi Nabi ka Qissa bayan nahi kiya gaya.

Is Qisse mein Allah Ta'ala ne bataya ke Yusuf (as) Uska Mukhlis Banda tha. Allah ne use Izzat ata ki thi jabke zahiri halaat uske na-muafiq the magar Khuda ne use har Musibat se rihai ata ki aur akheri Natija ye nikla ke woh bhai Jinhone Aap (as) par Zulm o Sitam ke Pahad tode the woh Aap (as) maangne par majboor ho gaye aur Zulekha aur doosri Misri Aurton ko Aap (as) ki Ismat ki Gawahi deni padi aur jis Mulk ke Qaidkhane mein Aap (as) ki Zindagi ka ek taweel arsa guzra tha us Mulk ki hukumat Aap (as) ke haath mein aa gayi."

Algharz ye Surah is haqeeqat ki Shaahid hai ke Izzat o Zillat Khuda ke haath mein hai aur Khuda Apne Mukhlis Bandon ko kabhi besahara nahi chhodta.

🤲🏻

اَلسَّلَامُ عَلٰى يُوْسُفَ الَّذِيْ نَجَّاهُ اللهُ مِنَ الْجُبِّ بِعَظَمَتِهٖ،......

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

   8th December 2020, Tuesday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

           ♦ SURAH YUSUF ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1588)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

نَحۡنُ نَقُصُّ عَلَیۡكَ أَحۡسَنَ ٱلۡقَصَصِ بِمَاۤ أَوۡحَیۡنَاۤ إِلَیۡكَ هَـٰذَا ٱلۡقُرۡءَانَ وَإِن كُنتَ مِن قَبۡلِهِۦ لَمِنَ ٱلۡغَـٰفِلِینَ.

"Paighambaron! Ham Aapke saamne ek Haseen tareen Qissa bayan kar rahe hain, jiski Wahy Hamne is Qur'an ke zariye Aap tak ki hai, warna isse pehle to (in cheezon se) Aap bilkul hi bekhabar the."

(Surah Yusuf: 3)

https://youtu.be/rpymJzfL6x4

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Jab Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne apni Qaum ko Qur'an ko sunaya to unhone kaha ke Aap hamen koi Qissa sunate to kya hi behtar hota. Iske jawab mein Allah ne Surah Yusuf nazil ki.

Qissa Yusuf (as) ko 'Ahsanul Qasas' isliye kaha gaya ke is mein Ibrat ke bahut se samaan maujood hain. Is Sureh mein is haqeeqat ko wazeh kiya gaya hai ke Allah ki Taqdeer wuqu pazeer hone se koi nahi rok sakta aur agar Khuda kisi ko izzat o iqtedar dena chahe to koi bhi use Usse door nahi rakh sakta.

(Noorus Saqlain)

🍁

Imam Sadiq (as) se manqool hai ke Qur'an "Ahsanul Hadees" aur "Ahsanul Qasas" hai.

Ameerul Mo'meneen Ali (as) ne ek Khutbe mein farmaya: "Qur'an Kitab e Khuda, Ahsanul Qasas, Baleegh Tareen Maueza aur faydemand Nasihat (Lesson) hai."

(Al Kaafi, Rauza e Kaafi, Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim, Noorus Saqlain)

☘️

Imam Baqir (as):

"Wahy ke Nuzool ki 5 Kaifiyaat hain:

Baaz Anbiya ko Zanjeer ki Awaaz ki tarah se awaaz sunayi deti thin aur woh uska mafhoom samajh lete the.

Baaz Anbiya ko Khwab mein Hidayat milti thin jaisa  ke Hazrat Ibrahim (as) ne apne farzand ki Qurbani ka Hukm Khwab mein paya aur Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne apne Iqtedar ki Bashaarat Khwab se hi haasil ki thi.

Kuchh Anbiya aise the jo Malaika ko dekhte the.

Kuchh woh the jinke Quloob par Ilqa' (Inspiration) hota tha.

Aur kuchh woh the jinhe Kaanon se Hukm e Khuda Wandi sunayi deti thi."

(Tafseer Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Imam Baqir (as):

"Baaz auqaat mein apne kuchh bachchon ko bila istehqaq pyaar karta hun aur unhe apni gaud mein bithata hun jabke mujhe ye bhi Ilm hota hai ke ye itne pyaar ke qabil nahi hain. Mein ye sab kuchh isliye karta hun ke woh Ehsaas e Mehroomi ka shikar na hon aur apne Ahle bhai se Hasad na karen. Allah Ta'ala ne Surah Yusuf ke zariye se ye Sabaq diya hai ke aise halaat paida na kiye jayen ke bhai ek doosre se Hasad karne lag jayen."

(Tafseer Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)

✒️

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Arabi Zabaan seekho. Ye Khuda ka wo Kalam hai jisse Allah ne Bandon se khitaab kiya hai."

(Kitabul Khisaal, Noorus Saqlain)

🤲🏻

اَلسَّلَامُ عَلٰى يُوْسُفَ الَّذِيْ نَجَّاهُ اللهُ مِنَ الْجُبِّ بِعَظَمَتِهٖ،......

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

9th December 2020, Wednesday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

     ♦ HAZRAT YUSUF (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1589)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

إِذۡ قَالَ یُوسُفُ لِأَبِیهِ یَـٰۤأَبَتِ إِنِّی رَأَیۡتُ أَحَدَ عَشَرَ كَوۡكَبࣰا وَٱلشَّمۡسَ وَٱلۡقَمَرَ رَأَیۡتُهُمۡ لِی سَـٰجِدِینَ *  قَالَ یَـٰبُنَیَّ لَا تَقۡصُصۡ رُءۡیَاكَ عَلَىٰۤ إِخۡوَتِكَ فَیَكِیدُوا۟ لَكَ كَیۡدًاۖ إِنَّ ٱلشَّیۡطَـٰنَ لِلۡإِنسَـٰنِ عَدُوࣱّ مُّبِینࣱ.

"Jab Yusuf (as) ne apne Waalid se kaha ke Abba Jaan! Meine 11 Sitaron, Suraj aur Chaand ko dekha hai ke wo mujhe Sajdah kar rahe hain. Unke Waalid ne kaha: Beta! Apna Khwab Bhaiyyon ko mat bayan karna warna woh tumhare khilaf saazishen karenge. Yaqeenan Shaitan Insaan ka khullam khulla Dushman hai."

(Surah Yusuf: 4 - 5)

https://youtu.be/rpymJzfL6x4

📚📖 💫⭐

👉 Tafseer:

Imam Baqir (as):

"Hazrat Yusuf (as) ke Khwab ki ta'beer ye thi ke woh Mulke Misr (Egypt) ki hukumat par faaez honge aur unke daure iqtedar mein unke Waaledain aur Bhai unke paas aayenge. "Suraj" se Hazrat Yusuf (as) ki Waledah "Raheel" aur Chaand se unke Waalid Hazrat Yaqoob (as) murad the aur 11 Sitaron se unke 11 Bhai murad the. Jab Hazrat Yaqoob (as) apne Kunbe ko le kar Misr mein dakhil hue the aur unhone Yusuf (as) ki Baadshahat dekhi to unhone Allah ka Shukr ada karte hue khaalis Allah ka hi Sajdah kiya tha."

(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi, Noorus Saqlain)

💫⭐

Imam Baqir (as):

"Hazrat Yusuf (as) ke 11 Bhai the. Binyamin unka saga Bhai tha. Hazrat Yaqoob (as) ka Laqab Israel hai jiske maani hain: "Allah ka khaalis Banda." Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne 9 Baras ki Umr mein ye Khwab dekha tha. Jab unhone ye Khwab apne Waalid ke saamne bayan kiya to unhone Yusuf (as) se kaha tha: "Beta! Ye Khwab apne Bhaiyyon se bayan na karna warna woh tere khilaf chaalen chalenge. Yaqeenan Shaitan Insaano ka khullam khulla Dushman hai."

(Noorus Saqlain)

💫⭐

Rasoole Khuda (saww):

"Un Sitaron ke Naam Jinhone Hazrat Yusuf (as) ko Sajdah kiya:

(1) Khubaan (2) Tariq (3) Zyal (4) Zulkatfani (5) Qabis (6) Wasaab (7) Amuraan (8) Filaq (9) Subeeh (10) Sadoo'  (11) Zulquroo'. In 11 Sitaron ke alawa Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne Suraj aur Chaand ko Sajdah karte hue dekha tha."

(Kitabul Khisaal, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Jo Surah Yusuf ki har roz ya har shab tilawat karega to Allah Ta'ala Qayamat wale Din use Hazrat Yusuf (as) ke Jamaal ki maanind Khubsoorati mein uthayega aur Qayamat wale Din use koi khauf na hoga aur wo Khuda ke Saleh bando'n mein se hoga…"

(Sawaabul Aamaal o Iqaabul Aaamal, p227)

🤲🏻

اَلسَّلَامُ عَلٰى يُوْسُفَ الَّذِيْ نَجَّاهُ اللهُ مِنَ الْجُبِّ بِعَظَمَتِهٖ،......

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

     ♦ HAZRAT YUSUF (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1590)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

إِذۡ قَالَ یُوسُفُ لِأَبِیهِ یَـٰۤأَبَتِ إِنِّی رَأَیۡتُ أَحَدَ عَشَرَ كَوۡكَبࣰا وَٱلشَّمۡسَ وَٱلۡقَمَرَ رَأَیۡتُهُمۡ لِی سَـٰجِدِینَ *  قَالَ یَـٰبُنَیَّ لَا تَقۡصُصۡ رُءۡیَاكَ عَلَىٰۤ إِخۡوَتِكَ فَیَكِیدُوا۟ لَكَ كَیۡدًاۖ إِنَّ ٱلشَّیۡطَـٰنَ لِلۡإِنسَـٰنِ عَدُوࣱّ مُّبِینࣱ.

"Jab Yusuf (as) ne apne Waalid se kaha ke Abba Jaan! Meine 11 Sitaron, Suraj aur Chaand ko dekha hai ke wo mujhe Sajdah kar rahe hain. Unke Waalid ne kaha: Beta! Apna *Khwab* Bhaiyyon ko mat bayan karna warna woh tumhare khilaf saazishen karenge. Yaqeenan Shaitan Insaan ka khullam khulla Dushman hai."

(Surah Yusuf: 4 - 5)

https://youtu.be/rpymJzfL6x4

📚📖 💫⭐

👉 Tafseer: 💭

*Khwab ki Ibteda kab hui?*

Imam Musa Kazim (as):

"Ibteda mein Insaan Khwab nahi dekha karte the. Khwab baad mein shuru hue.

Baat ye hai ke Allah ne ek Rasool bheja. Usne logon ko Allah ki Ita'at o Ibaadat ki dawat di. Logon ne usse kaha: 'Achha batao agar ham tumhara kehna maan len to hamen kya milega?' Aap hamse zyada Daulatmand bhi nahi hain aur Qaum Qabile ke aitbar se hamse zyada Sahibe Quwwat bhi to nahi hain. Phir ham Aapki pairavi karen to kyon karen? Us Nabi ne jawab diya: "Agar tumne meri pairavi ki to Allah tumhe Jannat mein dakhil karega aur agar tumne meri Nafarmani ki to Khuda tumhe Dozakh bhejega."

Unhone kaha: 'Jannat kiya cheez hain? Nabi ne kaha:"Jannat Ne'mato'n ka Ghar hai aur Dozakh Azaab ka Ghar hai." Unhone kaha: 'Ye Jannat o Jahannum hamen kab milegi?' Nabi ne kaha 'marne ke baad.' Phir un logon ne Nabi zyada mukhalifat shuru kar di. Allah Ta'ala ne us waqt Khwabon ka silsila shuru kar diya. Jab un logon ne Khwab dekhe to hairaan ho kar Nabi ke paas aaye. Nabi ne unse kaha: "Allah ne is zariye se tum par Hujjat tamam ki hai. Jab tum mar jaoge to tumhare Badan gal sadh jayenge, lekin tumhari Arwaah (Souls) baqi honge. Khuda unhe Azaab dega aur ye silsila Qayamat tak qaem rahega."

(Rauza e Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)

💭 🌜

What is the Reality of Dreams? click for Ans:

https://www.al-islam.org/180-questions-enquiries-about-islam-volume-two-various-issues/18-what-reality-dreams

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Riwayat:

"Janabe Hamza aur Janabe Jafare Tayyar ne Rasoole Khuda (saww) ko *Khwab* mein bataya "Hum ne Aap par Salwaat bhejne, pyase ko paani pilane aur Mohabbat e Ali (as) ko sabse behtar Amal paya hai."

(Fazaail e Salwaat Aur Mushkilaat ka Hal)

🤲🏻

"Mere Malik Tere aise bhi Dost hain Shab mein jo Khwabe Ghaflat mein hain unke liye Dua karte hain: Mere Malik garche Terr kuchh Bande Mahv e Khwab hain, kuchh aise hain jo bedaar reh jar Girya o buka ki haalat mein hain."

(Munajat e Ameerul Mo'meneen Ali (as)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

     ♦ HAZRAT YUSUF (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1591)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَكَذَ ٰ⁠لِكَ یَجۡتَبِیكَ رَبُّكَ وَیُعَلِّمُكَ مِن تَأۡوِیلِ ٱلۡأَحَادِیثِ وَیُتِمُّ نِعۡمَتَهُۥ عَلَیۡكَ وَعَلَىٰۤ ءَالِ یَعۡقُوبَ كَمَاۤ أَتَمَّهَا عَلَىٰۤ أَبَوَیۡكَ مِن قَبۡلُ إِبۡرَ ٰ⁠هِیمَ وَإِسۡحَـٰقَۚ إِنَّ رَبَّكَ عَلِیمٌ حَكِیمࣱ.

"Aur is tarah se tera Rab tujhe muntakhib karega aur tujhe baaton ki teh tak pahunchna sikhayega aur tujh par aur Aale Yaqoob (as) par apni Ne'mat usi tarah poori karega jis tarah isse pehle Woh tere Buzurgon Ibrahim (as) wa Ishaaq (as) par chuka hai. Yaqeenan tera Rab Sahibe Ilm aur Sahibe Hikmat hai."

(Surah Yusuf: 6)

https://youtu.be/rpymJzfL6x4

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Azmayish ki Ibteda kab hui?

Poore Qisse ka pase manzar ye hai:

🕌 🍪🍵

Imam Zainul Abedin (as) ne apni Kaneez se kaha jo bhi Saael darwaaze par aaye use Khaana zaroor khilana. Aaj Jume ka Din hai.

Raavi ne sawal kiya: 'Har Saael to Mustaheq nahi hota?

Aap (as) ne farmaya:

"Mein darta hun ke kahin koi Mustaheq Saael mehroom na ho jaye aur uski wajah se ham par wo Azmaish na aa jaye jo Hazrat Yaqoob (as) ke Gharane par nazil hui thi lehaza unhe Khaana khilao, unhe Khaana khilao."

Yaqoob (as) ka dastoor tha ke Aap (as) rozana apne Khandan ke liye ek Dunba zabah karte the. Aap (as) ka Khandan bhi uska Gosht khata aur Sawal karne walon ko bhi Khaana khilate the.

Us zamane mein ek Sachcha Momin rehta tha jiska naam "Zamyaal" tha. Khuda ki nazar mein use Maqam hasil tha. Woh Din ko Roza rakhta tha aur Raat ko Ibaadat kiya karta tha. Ek bar Shabe Juma ko woh Hazrat Yaqoob (as) ke darwaze par aaya aur usne sada di: 'Gharwalo! Ek Musafir Ghareeb ko Khuda ke naam par Khaana do.' Usne kayi bar ye sada di lekin kisi ne us par tawajjah na di. Jab woh mayoos hua to usne Kalma e Istisreja padha aur Khuda ke Huzoor apni bhook ki shikayat ki aur usne bhook ki haalat mein Raat guzari. Subah hui to usne Roza rakh liya. Woh bechara saari Raat bhook se bilakta raha ke Aale Yaqoob shikam ser ho kar sote rahe.

Allah Ta'ala ne Subah ke waqt Yaqoob (as) ko ye Wahy farmayi:

"Yaqoob (as)! Tu ne Mere Bandon ki Tauheen ki hai, jiski wajah se Tu Mere Ghazab ka Haqdar qarar paya hai. Mein tujh par aur teri Aulad par sakhti nazil karunga. Mere Anbiya mein se mujhe woh Nabi zyada pyara hai jo Mere Miskeen Bandon par Rahem kare aur unhe apne qareeb bithaye aur unhe Khaana khilaye aur Mere Miskeen Bandon ke liye Malja o Mawa ho."

"Yaqoob (as)!........ aur tumhe maloom hona chahiye ke Mein Apne Dushmano par jaldi se Azmayish (Test) nazil nahi karta jabke apne Doston par jaldi se Azmayish nazil karta hun. Lehaza ab tum Azmayish ke liye amada ho jao aur Masaeb par Sabr karo."

Jis Raat Zamyaal bhooka raha tha usi waqt Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne ye Khwab dekha. Subah hui to unhone ye Khwab apne Waalid se bayan kiya, jo ke ye sun kar pareshan hue aur unhe yaqeen ho gaya ke ab un par Azmayish aane waali hai. Isiliye Aap (as) ne apne Farzand se kaha: 'Beta! Ye Khwab Bhaiyyon se bayan na karna...'

(Kitab Ilalush Sharaye, Noorus Saqlain)

🤲🏻

اَللّٰهُمَّ اغفِرلِىَ الذُّنُوبَ الَّتِى تُنزِلُ البَلَاء.

"Khudaya! Un Gunahon ko bakhsh de jo nuzoole Balaa ka sabab hote hain."

(Dua-e-Kumail)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

  12th December 2020, Saturday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

     ♦ HAZRAT YUSUF (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1592)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

لَّقَدۡ كَانَ فِی یُوسُفَ وَإِخۡوَتِهِۦۤ ءَایَـٰتࣱ لِّلسَّاۤىِٕلِینَ *  إِذۡ قَالُوا۟ لَیُوسُفُ وَأَخُوهُ أَحَبُّ إِلَىٰۤ أَبِینَا مِنَّا وَنَحۡنُ عُصۡبَةٌ إِنَّ أَبَانَا لَفِی ضَلَـٰلࣲ مُّبِینٍ *  ٱقۡتُلُوا۟ یُوسُفَ أَوِ ٱطۡرَحُوهُ أَرۡضࣰا یَخۡلُ لَكُمۡ وَجۡهُ أَبِیكُمۡ وَتَكُونُوا۟ مِنۢ بَعۡدِهِۦ قَوۡمࣰا صَـٰلِحِینَ.

"Yaqeenan, Yusuf (as) aur uske Bhaiyyon ke Qisse mein Sawal karne walon ke liye bahut si Nishaniyan hain. Jab unhone kaha ke Yusuf (as) aur uska Bhai hamare Waalid ko hamse zyada pyare hain, halanke ham ek poora jatha hain. Yaqeenan hamara Waalid sareeh Gumrahi mein mubtila hai. Tum Yusuf (as) ko qatl kar do ya use kisi Zameen par phenk aao taake tumhare Waalid ki tawajjoh tumhari taraf ho jaye, phir uske baad Nek ban jana."

(Surah Yusuf: 7 - 9)

https://youtu.be/rpymJzfL6x4

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 📚📖 💫⭐

👉 Tafseer:

Waqea: (Riwayat Cont'd)

Imam Zainul Abedin (as):

........

Is tanbeeh ke bawajood Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne Bhaiyyon se apna Khwab bayan kiya. Jab unhone ye Khwab suna to unhone isse Hasad kiya aur unke khilaf sazishen karne lage. Iske Natije mein ye waqea pesh aaya aur jab Yusuf (as) ke bhai unhe saath le kar Jungle ki taraf rawana hue. Abhi thodi der hi chale the ke Yaqoob (as) apni Muhabbat ke haathon majboor ho kar daudte hue Beton ke paas aaye aur Yusuf (as) ko seene se lagaya aur ji bhar kar pyar kiya. Phir use Bhaiyyon ke hawale kar diya.

Hazrat Yusuf (as) ke Bhaiyyon ne socha ke kahin Hazrat Yaqoob (as) par Pidari Shafqat ghalib na aa jaye aur woh Yusuf (as) ko apne paas na bula len isliye unhone jaldi safar shuru kar diya. Jab woh Yusuf (as) ko Baap se door ek Jungle mein le aaye to darakhton ke ek jhund ke neeche baith kar kehne lage ke ham Yusuf (as) ko yahan zabah karen aur iski Laash yahan phenk den jaise hi Raat hogi to Jungli darinde aa kar ise khaa jayenge.

(To be Cont'd.........)

(Kitab Ilalush Sharaye, Noorus Saqlain, Raavi: Abu Hamza Somali)

🤲🏻

Imam Sadiq (as):

Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne Kuwen mein ye Dua padhi:

اَللّٰهُمَّ إنِّى اَسئَلُكَ بِاَنَّ لَكَ الحَمدُ لَا إلٰهَ إلَّا أنتَ المَنَّانُ بَدِيعُ السَّمٰوٰاتِ وَ الأرضِ ذُوالجَلَالِ وَ الأِكرَامِ اَن تُصَلِّى عَلَى مُحَمَّدٍ وَ آلِ مُحَمَّدٍ وَ اَن تَجعَل لِى مِمَّا اَنَا فِيهِ فَرَجًا وَ مَخرَجًا.

(Usoole Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)

     ♦ HAZRAT YUSUF (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1593)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

قَالَ قَاۤىِٕلࣱ مِّنۡهُمۡ لَا تَقۡتُلُوا۟ یُوسُفَ وَأَلۡقُوهُ فِی غَیَـٰبَتِ ٱلۡجُبِّ یَلۡتَقِطۡهُ بَعۡضُ ٱلسَّیَّارَةِ إِن كُنتُمۡ فَـٰعِلِینَ *  قَالُوا۟ یَـٰۤأَبَانَا مَا لَكَ لَا تَأۡمَ۬نَّا عَلَىٰ یُوسُفَ وَإِنَّا لَهُۥ لَنَـٰصِحُونَ *  أَرۡسِلۡهُ مَعَنَا غَدࣰا یَرۡتَعۡ وَیَلۡعَبۡ وَإِنَّا لَهُۥ لَحَـٰفِظُونَ.

"Un mein se ek kehne wale ne kaha: ke Yusuf (as) ko qatl na karo aur agar tumhe kuchh karna hi hai to use andhe Kuwen mein dal do aur koi aanewala Qafila use nikal le jayega. Unhone apne Baap se kaha: 'Abba Jaan! Kya wajah hai ke Aap Yusuf (as) ke mutalliq ham par etemad nahi karte, jabke ham to uske Khair khwah (Wellwisher) hain. Aap kal use hamare saath rawana karen, kuchh kha pi lega aur khel kood lega aur ham uski muhafizat karte rahenge."

(Surah Yusuf: 10 - 12)

https://youtu.be/rpymJzfL6x4

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 📚📖 💫⭐

👉 Tafseer:

Waqea: (Riwayat Cont'd)

Imam Zainul Abedin (as):

........

Shaam ke waqt woh Khoon aaloodah Kurta le kar Baap ke paas rote hue aaye aur kehne lage: 'Abba Jaan! Ham daudne mein masroof the. Yusuf (as) hamare Maan ke paas baitha hua tha ke itne mein ek Bhedya aaya jo use khaa gaya.' Hazrat Yaqoob (as) ne jab ye suna to unhe yaqeen ho gaya ke Parwardigar ki taraf se unki Azmayish shuru ho chuki hai. Aap (as) ne apne Beton se farmaya: "Tumne ye baat apni taraf se bana li hai, jab tak Yusuf (as) ko uski Khwab ki ta'beer na mil jaye us waqt tak us par Maut nahi aa sakti."

(Imam (as) ne yahan guftugu khatm ki, baqi hissa agle din bayan kiya.)

(To be Cont'd.........)

(Kitab Ilalush Sharaye, Noorus Saqlain, Raavi: Abu Hamza Somali)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

     ♦ HAZRAT YUSUF (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1594)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

قَالَ إِنِّی لَیَحۡزُنُنِیۤ أَن تَذۡهَبُوا۟ بِهِۦ وَأَخَافُ أَن یَأۡكُلَهُ ٱلذِّئۡبُ وَأَنتُمۡ عَنۡهُ غَـٰفِلُونَ *  قَالُوا۟ لَىِٕنۡ أَكَلَهُ ٱلذِّئۡبُ وَنَحۡنُ عُصۡبَةٌ إِنَّاۤ إِذࣰا لَّخَـٰسِرُونَ.

"Yaqoob (as) ne kaha: 'Mujhe ye baat shaaq guzarti hai ke tum use le jao aur mujhe andesha hai ke koi Bhediya use na khaa jaye aur tum usse ghaafil rah jao.' Unhone kaha: 'Bhala hamara is jathe ki maujoodgi mein use Bhediya kaise kha lega. Agar aisa hoga to phir ham nuqsaan uthane wale qarar payenge."

(Surah Yusuf: 13 - 14)

https://youtu.be/rpymJzfL6x4

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Jab Hazrat Yaqoob (as) ke Beton ne unse bahar jaane ki ijazat talab ki thi to Yaqoob (as) ne unse kaha tha ke mein darta hun ke Yusuf (as) ko kahin Bhediya hi na kha jaye aur tum isse ghafil raho. Agar Hazrat Yaqoob (as) Bhediye ki baat na karte to Bete bhi Bhediye ka jhoota afsaana na tarashte.

(Kitab Ilalush Sharaye, Noorus)

🐺

Rasoole Khuda (saww):

"Logon ko jhoote bahane mat sikhao warna tumse wohi jhoote bahane banane lag jayenge. Yaqoob (as) ke Beton ko maloom nahi tha ke Bhediya Insaan ko kha jata hai. Jab Yaqoob (as) ne Bhediye ka andesha zahir kiya to Beton ne bhi Bhediye ka hi bahana tarash liya."

(Majmaul Bayan, Noorus Saqlain)

👕

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Qissa e Yusuf (as) ki Jaan Yusuf (as) ki Qameez par hai. Ek martaba Qameez par Khoon laga. Zulekha ke haathon Qameez phati. Isi Qameez se Hazrat Yaqoob (as) ko binayi mili."

(Kitabul Khisaal, Noorus Saqlain)

🤲🏻

Imam Sadiq (as):

Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne Kuwen mein ye Dua padhi:

اَللّٰهُمَّ اِن كَانَتَ الخَطَايَا وَ الذَّنُوبَ قَد وَجهِى عِندَكَ فَلَن تَرفَع لِى الَيكَ صَوتًا وَ لَن تَستَجِيبَ لِى دَعوَةٌ فَاِنِّى اَسئَلُكَ بِحَقِّ الشَّيخ يَعقُوبَ فَارحَم ضَعفَه وَاجمَع بَينِى وَ بَينَهٗ فَقَد عَلِمتَ رِقَّتَهٗ عَلَىَّ وَ شَوقِى اِلَيهِ.

(Amali Sudooq, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

     ♦ HAZRAT YUSUF (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1595)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

فَلَمَّا ذَهَبُوا۟ بِهِۦ وَأَجۡمَعُوۤا۟ أَن یَجۡعَلُوهُ فِی غَیَـٰبَتِ ٱلۡجُبِّۚ وَأَوۡحَیۡنَاۤ إِلَیۡهِ لَتُنَبِّئَنَّهُم بِأَمۡرِهِمۡ هَـٰذَا وَهُمۡ لَا یَشۡعُرُونَ *  وَجَاۤءُوۤ أَبَاهُمۡ عِشَاۤءࣰ یَبۡكُونَ *  قَالُوا۟ یَـٰۤأَبَانَاۤ إِنَّا ذَهَبۡنَا نَسۡتَبِقُ وَتَرَكۡنَا یُوسُفَ عِندَ مَتَـٰعِنَا فَأَكَلَهُ ٱلذِّئۡبُۖ وَمَاۤ أَنتَ بِمُؤۡمِنࣲ لَّنَا وَلَوۡ كُنَّا صَـٰدِقِینَ *  وَجَاۤءُو عَلَىٰ قَمِیصِهِۦ بِدَمࣲ كَذِبࣲۚ....

"Jab woh use le kar gaye aur unhone Ijma (agreed) kar liya tha ke woh use Andhe Kuwen mein phenkenge aur Hamne Yusuf (as) ki taraf Wahy ki ke ek waqt aayega jab tu un logon ko unki ye harkat jatayega. Us waqt unhe khabar na hogi."

"Shaam ke waqt woh rote hue apne Baap ke paas aaye. Unhone kaha: 'Abba Jaan! Ham daudne ke muqabile (racing) mein masroof the aur hamne Yusuf (as) ko apne samaan ke paas bithaya hua tha. Is asna mein ek Bhediya use kha gaya. Ham khwah kitne hi sachche kyon na hon Aap (as) phir bhi ham par etemad nahi karenge. Woh Yusuf (as) ke Qamees par jhoota Khoon laga kar aaye the."

(Surah Yusuf: 15 - 18)

https://youtu.be/rpymJzfL6x4

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 📚📖

👉 Tafseer: 🐺

Imam Zainul Abedin (as):

(Riwayat Cont'd...)

Jab Bradarane Yusuf (as) apne Bhai ko Kuwen mein dal chuke to unhone kaha: 'Ab ham ek Dumba zabah karte hain aur uska Khoon Yusuf (as) ki Qameez par laga kar apne Waalid se kahenge ke Aapke Yusuf (as) ko Bhediya kha gaya. Us waqt Yusuf (as) ke ek bhai "Laavi" ne kaha:

"Bhaiyyon! Kya ham Yaqoob (as) Nabi ke bete nahi hain aur kya hamara Dada Ishaaq (as) Nabi na tha aur kya hamara pardada Ibrahim (as) Khalilullah nahi tha?"

Sabne kaha kyon nahi. Sab ke sab Nabi the.

Laavi ne kaha: "To tum kya samajhte ho ke tum jhoot bol kar azaad ho jaoge? Kya Khuda Wahy ke zariye hamare Waalid ko is waqae ke mutalliq kuchh nahi batayega?"

Bhaiyyon ne kaha: haan!

Laavi ne kaha: _"Iska bas yehi hal hai ke ham sab Ghusl karen aur ba-Jamat Namaz padh kar Khuda se darkhwast karen ke Woh hamare Waalid ko asl Haqeeqat se agah na kare."

Millat e Ibrahim (as) ka Qanoon tha ke 11 afraad ke baghair Jamat nahi hoti thi. Lekin Aulad e Yaqoob (as) ki majboori ye thi ke unki tadaad 11 se kam thi. Laavi ne kaha: 'Koi baat nahi ham Allah ko apna Imam bana lete hain. Chunanche unhone waisa hi kiya aur ro ro ka Dua ki. Phir Shaam ko apne Waalid ke paas pahunche. Hazrat Yaqoob (as) ne Qameez dekh kar farmaya: "Maloom hota hai Bhediya bada Meherban tha. Usne Yusuf (as) ko to kha liya lekin uski Qameez ko kahin se nahi phada.'"

(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi, Noorus Saqlain)

(To be Cont'd.....)

🤲🏻

Imam Sadiq (as):

Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne Kuwen mein ye Dua padhi:

اَللّٰهُمَّ اِن كَانَتَ الخَطَايَا وَ الذَّنُوبَ قَد وَجهِى عِندَكَ فَلَن تَرفَع لِى الَيكَ صَوتًا وَ لَن تَستَجِيبَ لِى دَعوَةٌ فَاِنِّى اَسئَلُكَ بِحَقِّ الشَّيخ يَعقُوبَ فَارحَم ضَعفَه وَاجمَع بَينِى وَ بَينَهٗ فَقَد عَلِمتَ رِقَّتَهٗ عَلَىَّ وَ شَوقِى اِلَيهِ.

(Amali Sudooq, Noorus Saqlain)

16th December 2020, Wednesday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

     ♦ HAZRAT YUSUF (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1595)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَجَاۤءُو عَلَىٰ قَمِیصِهِۦ بِدَمࣲ كَذِبࣲۚ قَالَ بَلۡ سَوَّلَتۡ لَكُمۡ أَنفُسُكُمۡ أَمۡرࣰاۖ فَصَبۡرࣱ جَمِیلࣱۖ وَٱللَّهُ ٱلۡمُسۡتَعَانُ عَلَىٰ مَا تَصِفُونَ *  وَجَاۤءَتۡ سَیَّارَةࣱ فَأَرۡسَلُوا۟ وَارِدَهُمۡ فَأَدۡلَىٰ دَلۡوَهُۥۖ قَالَ یَـٰبُشۡرَىٰ هَـٰذَا غُلَـٰمࣱۚ وَأَسَرُّوهُ بِضَـٰعَةࣰۚ وَٱللَّهُ عَلِیمُۢ بِمَا یَعۡمَلُونَ.

"Unke Waalid ne kaha: Tumhare Nafs ne ek bade kaam ko tere liye asaan bana diya hai. Ab Sabr hi achhi cheez hai. Jo baat tum bana rahe ho us par Khuda se hi Madad maangi ja sakti hai."

"Ek Qafila aaya. Unhone apne Paani bharne wale ko Paani lene ke liye bheja. Usne Kuwen mein Dol dala. Usne kaha: 'Khushkhabari ho, ye ek ladka hai.' Un logon ne use Maale Tijarat samajh kar chhupa liya, halanke woh jo kuchh kar rahe the Khuda ko iski sab Khabar thi."

(Surah Yusuf: 18 - 19)

https://youtu.be/rpymJzfL6x4

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 📚📖

👉 Tafseer: 🐺

Imam Zainul Abedin (as):

(Riwayat Cont'd...)

Imam Sajjad (as):

"Us Raat Bradrane Yusuf (as) ne apne ghar guzari. Subah hui to unhone ek doosre se kaha: Aao chal kar Yusuf (as) ka haal maloom karen aur ye pata chalayen ke woh mar gaya hai ya zinda hai. Allah ne wahan ek Qafila bheja tha. Ahle Qafila ne Paani laane wale ko us Kuwen se Paani laane ke liye kaha. Usne Kuwen mein Dol dala to Yusuf (as) uske Dol se chimat gaye. Jab usne masoom bachche ko dekha to usne khushi se kaha: 'Lo Mubarak ho, ye ladka Kuwen se mila hai. Ahle Qafila ne Yusuf (as) ko Samaane Tijart samajh kar apne paas bitha liya.

(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi, Noorus Saqlain)

(To be Cont'd.....)

🤲🏻

Imam Sadiq (as):

Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne Kuwen mein ye Dua padhi:

اَللّٰهُمَّ اِن كَانَتَ الخَطَايَا وَ الذَّنُوبَ قَد وَجهِى عِندَكَ فَلَن تَرفَع لِى الَيكَ صَوتًا وَ لَن تَستَجِيبَ لِى دَعوَةٌ فَاِنِّى اَسئَلُكَ بِحَقِّ الشَّيخ يَعقُوبَ فَارحَم ضَعفَه وَاجمَع بَينِى وَ بَينَهٗ فَقَد عَلِمتَ رِقَّتَهٗ عَلَىَّ وَ شَوقِى اِلَيهِ.

(Amali Sudooq, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

     ♦ HAZRAT YUSUF (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1598)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَشَرَوۡهُ بِثَمَنِۭ بَخۡسࣲ دَرَ ٰ⁠هِمَ مَعۡدُودَةࣲ وَكَانُوا۟ فِیهِ مِنَ ٱلزَّ ٰ⁠هِدِینَ.

"Unhone use thodi si Qeemat par chand Dirhamon ke badle bech diya aur woh uski Qeemat se bezaar the."

(Surah Yusuf: 20)

https://youtu.be/rpymJzfL6x4

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Imam Zainul Abedin (as):

(Riwayat Cont'd...)

"Bradrane Yusuf (as) wahan pahunche to unhone ek Qafile ko wahan maujood paya. Unhone wahan apne Bhai Yusuf (as) ko bhi dekh liya. Iske baad woh Salaare Qafila ke paas aaye aur usse kaha: 'Ye hamara Ghulam hai. Kal ye is Kuwen mein gir pada tha ab ham isko nikalne ke liye yaha aaye hain.

Ye keh kar unhone Yusuf (as) ko Ahle Qafila se chhin liya aur use door le ja kar kaha:' Ab Tumhare saamne do hi raaste hain ya to unke saamne iqraar karo ke tum hamare Ghulam ho. Agar tumne iqraar kar liya to ham tujhe unke haathon forokht (sell) kar denge. Is tarah tumhari zindagi bach jayegi aur agar tum iska iqraar nahi karte to ham tujhe aa le ja kar qatl kar denge.

Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne kaha: "Mujhe qatl na karo. Tum mujhe forokht kar do." Iske baad woh use Qafile walon ke paas le aaye aur unse kaha: 'Kya tum mein se koi is Ghulam ko khareedna chahta hai?' Ek Tajir ne use 20 Dirham ke ewaz khareed liya aur Bhai waise bhi uski Qeemat se be raghbat the."

(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi, Noorus Saqlain)

(To be Cont'd.....)

💰

Imam Reza (as):

"Bhaiyyon ne Yusuf (as) ko 20 Dirhamon ke ewaz forokht (sell) kiya tha jab ke ye Raqam (value) itni haqeer hai ke agar kisi ke haathon se Shikari Kutta qatl ho jaye to ewaz mein 20 Dirham ada kiye jate hain."

(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi, Noorus Saqlain)

💰

Imam Sajjad (as):

"Bhaiyyon ne Yusuf (as) ko 20 Dirhamon mein forokht kiya tha aur 10 Bhaiyyon ne 2-2 Dirham hasil kiye the."

(Majmaul Bayan, Noorus Saqlain)

🕳️

Imam Reza (as):

"Dirham o Dinar ke Sikke (Coin) sab se pehle Nimrod bin Kan'an ne raaej kiye the."

(Uyoonul Akhbar, Noorus Saqlain)

🤲🏻

Imam Sadiq (as):

Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne Kuwen mein ye Dua padhi:

اَللّٰهُمَّ اِن كَانَتَ الخَطَايَا وَ الذَّنُوبَ قَد وَجهِى عِندَكَ فَلَن تَرفَع لِى الَيكَ صَوتًا وَ لَن تَستَجِيبَ لِى دَعوَةٌ فَاِنِّى اَسئَلُكَ بِحَقِّ الشَّيخ يَعقُوبَ فَارحَم ضَعفَه وَاجمَع بَينِى وَ بَينَهٗ فَقَد عَلِمتَ رِقَّتَهٗ عَلَىَّ وَ شَوقِى اِلَيهِ.

(Amali Sudooq, Noorus Saqlain)

     ♦ HAZRAT YUSUF (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1597)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَقَالَ ٱلَّذِی ٱشۡتَرَىٰهُ مِن مِّصۡرَ لِٱمۡرَأَتِهِۦۤ أَكۡرِمِی مَثۡوَىٰهُ عَسَىٰۤ أَن یَنفَعَنَاۤ أَوۡ نَتَّخِذَهُۥ وَلَدࣰاۚ وَكَذَ ٰ⁠لِكَ مَكَّنَّا لِیُوسُفَ فِی ٱلۡأَرۡضِ وَلِنُعَلِّمَهُۥ مِن تَأۡوِیلِ ٱلۡأَحَادِیثِۚ وَٱللَّهُ غَالِبٌ عَلَىٰۤ أَمۡرِهِۦ وَلَـٰكِنَّ أَكۡثَرَ ٱلنَّاسِ لَا یَعۡلَمُونَ

"Aur Misr ke jis shakhs ne use khareeda, usne apni Biwi se kaha: "Isko achhi tarah se rakhna, mumkin hai ke ye hame fayda pahunchaye ya ham ise Beta bana len. Is tarah se Hamne Yusuf (as) ke liye us Zameen par qadam jamane ki sabeel paida ki taake Ham ise Batoon ki teh tak pahunchne (Taveel) ki Taleem de. Allah Apne Maamle mein Ghalib hai, lekin logon ki aksariyat ko Ilm nahi hai."

(Surah Yusuf: 21)

https://youtu.be/rpymJzfL6x4

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 📚📖

👉 Tafseer: 

Imam Zainul Abedin (as):

(Riwayat Cont'd...)

"Jis Tajir ne Yusuf (as) ko khareeda tha, woh use apne saath le kar Misr (Egypt) le aaya aur Misr pahunch kar usne Yusuf (as) ko giran Qeemat ke ewaz "Aziz e Misr" ke haathon forokht kar diya.

Aziz e Misr Hazrat Yusuf (as) ko le kar apne ghar pahuncha aur usne apni Biwi se kaha ke use achhi tarah se rakhna mumkin hai ke ye bada ho kar hamen fayda pahunchaye aur ye bhi hi sakta hai ke ham ise apna Beta bana len."

(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi, Noorus Saqlain)

(To be Cont'd.....)

💕😞👑

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Yusuf (as) ki Zindagi bhi badi ajeeb thi. Bachpane mein Baap ki Aankh ka Taara the, phir bik kar Ghulam bane, phir kuchh arse baad Misr ke Haakim  bane."

(Tafseer Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)

🤲🏻

Imam Sadiq (as):

Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne Kuwen mein ye Dua padhi:

اَللّٰهُمَّ اِن كَانَتَ الخَطَايَا وَ الذَّنُوبَ قَد وَجهِى عِندَكَ فَلَن تَرفَع لِى الَيكَ صَوتًا وَ لَن تَستَجِيبَ لِى دَعوَةٌ فَاِنِّى اَسئَلُكَ بِحَقِّ الشَّيخ يَعقُوبَ فَارحَم ضَعفَه وَاجمَع بَينِى وَ بَينَهٗ فَقَد عَلِمتَ رِقَّتَهٗ عَلَىَّ وَ شَوقِى اِلَيهِ.

(Amali Sudooq, Noorus Saqlain)

     ♦ HAZRAT YUSUF (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1598)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَلَمَّا بَلَغَ أَشُدَّهُۥۤ ءَاتَیۡنَـٰهُ حُكۡمࣰا وَعِلۡمࣰاۚ وَكَذَ ٰ⁠لِكَ نَجۡزِی ٱلۡمُحۡسِنِینَ.

"Aur jab woh apni Jawani ko pahuncha to Hamne usi ko Quwwat e Faisla aur Ilm ata kiya aur Nekokar afraad ko Ham isi tarah se Badla diya karte hain."

(Surah Yusuf: 22)

https://youtu.be/rpymJzfL6x4

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Imam Zainul Abedin (as):

(Riwayat Cont'd...)

"Jab Hazrat Yusuf (as) ko Kuwen mein giraya us waqt Aapki Umr 9 Saal ki thi. Hazrat Yaqoob (as) ke Ghar se Misr tak 12 Dino ka faasla tha. Hazrat Yusuf (as) apne daur ke Haseen tareen fard the. Jab Aap (as) Jawani ko pahunche to Aziz e Misr ki Biwi ki Niyyat kharab ho gayi aur usne darwaze band kiye aur Hazrat Yusuf (as) ko Gunah ki dawat di.

Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne kaha: "Khuda ki Panah, mera talluq us Khandan se hai jo Zina se mehfooz hai.

Aziz e Misr ki Biwi Aap (as) par girne lagi to Aap (as) wahan se bhage. Woh Aap (as) ko pakadne ke liye Aap (as) ke peechhe daudi. Darwaze khulte gaye aur Yusuf (as) bahar aate rahe. Jab akhiri Darwaze par pahunche to Aurat ne peechhe se unki Qameez ko pakda jisse wo Qameez peechhe se phat gayi. Abhi ye kashmakash jaari thi ke Aziz e Misr Darwaze par aa gaya. Aurat ne cheekh kar apne Shauhar se kaha jo shakhs aapki gharwali ki Namoos tabah karna chahe aap usko kya Saza denge? Meri nazar mein to iski Saza ye hai ke ise Zindan bhej diya jaye ya ise sakht Azaab diya jaye."

(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi, Noorus Saqlain)

(To be Cont'd.....)

🤲🏻

Imam Sadiq (as):

Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne Kuwen mein ye Dua padhi:

اَللّٰهُمَّ اِن كَانَتَ الخَطَايَا وَ الذَّنُوبَ قَد وَجهِى عِندَكَ فَلَن تَرفَع لِى الَيكَ صَوتًا وَ لَن تَستَجِيبَ لِى دَعوَةٌ فَاِنِّى اَسئَلُكَ بِحَقِّ الشَّيخ يَعقُوبَ فَارحَم ضَعفَه وَاجمَع بَينِى وَ بَينَهٗ فَقَد عَلِمتَ رِقَّتَهٗ عَلَىَّ وَ شَوقِى اِلَيهِ.

(Amali Sudooq, Noorus Saqlain)

     ♦ HAZRAT YUSUF (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1599)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَرَ ٰ⁠وَدَتۡهُ ٱلَّتِی هُوَ فِی بَیۡتِهَا عَن نَّفۡسِهِۦ وَغَلَّقَتِ ٱلۡأَبۡوَ ٰ⁠بَ وَقَالَتۡ هَیۡتَ لَكَۚ قَالَ مَعَاذَ ٱللَّهِۖ إِنَّهُۥ رَبِّیۤ أَحۡسَنَ مَثۡوَایَۖ إِنَّهُۥ لَا یُفۡلِحُ ٱلظَّـٰلِمُونَ.

"Jis Aurat ke Ghar mein Yusuf (as) qayam pazeer the, woh us par Ishq ka Jaal phenkne lagi aur usne Darwaze band kar diye aur kehne lagi ke aa ja. Yusuf (as) ne kaha: Khuda ki Panah! Mere Rab ne to mujhe achhi Manzelat Bakhshi hai aur Zulm karnewale kabhi kamyab nahi hote."

(Surah Yusuf: 23)

https://youtu.be/rpymJzfL6x4

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Imam Zainul Abedin (as):

(Riwayat Cont'd...)

"Jab Aziz e Misr ne ye suna to use ghussa aaya. Usne iraada kiya ke Yusuf (as) ko sakht Saza de. Us waqt Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne usse kaha: "Mujhe Yaqoob (as) ke Ma'bood ki Qasam! Meine teri Biwi se Burayi ka koi iraada nahi kiya tha. Usne hi pahel ki thi. Agar tum ye maloom karna chahte ho ke ham mein se zyadti kiski taraf se hui hai to tum is Masoom Bachche se poochh lo. Us Bachche ka talluq Zulekha ke Khandan se tha. Us Bachche ki Maa use milne ke liye wahan aayi hui thi. Allah Ta'ala ne Bachche ko bolne ki quwwat ata kar di.

Usne kaha: Badshah! Yusuf (as) ki Qameez ko dekho agar wo saamne se phati hui ho to khata Yusuf (as) ki hai aur teri Biwi be-gunah hai aur agar Yusuf (as) ki Qameez peechhe se phati hui ho to khata teri Biwi ki hai aur Yusuf (as) bequsoor hai.

Jab Badshah ne ek Masoom Bachche ki ye Gawahi suni to woh ghabra gaya. Phir usne Yusuf (as) ki Qameez ko dekha to wo peechhe se phati hui thi. Qameez ko dekh kar use Yusuf (as) ki begunahi ka yaqeen ho gaya. Usne apni Biwi se kaha: 'Ye sab kuchh tumhara kara dhara hai, tum Aurton ki chaalen bahut sakht hoti hain. Phir usne Hazrat Yusuf (as) se kaha: "Aye Yusuf (as)! Is baat ko jaane do. Kisi ko Kaano Kaan iski khabar nahi honi chahiye. Lekin Yusuf (as) ne is khabar ko makhfi na rakha aur yun baat mohallat mein pahunchi aur Aurton ne ek doosre se kaha ke Aziz ki Biwi apne ghulam par Dil haar baithi hai aur yaqeenan woh sakht gumrahi mein hai."

(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi, Noorus Saqlain)

(To be Cont'd.....)

🤲🏻

Imam Sadiq (as):

Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne Kuwen mein ye Dua padhi:

اَللّٰهُمَّ اِن كَانَتَ الخَطَايَا وَ الذَّنُوبَ قَد وَجهِى عِندَكَ فَلَن تَرفَع لِى الَيكَ صَوتًا وَ لَن تَستَجِيبَ لِى دَعوَةٌ فَاِنِّى اَسئَلُكَ بِحَقِّ الشَّيخ يَعقُوبَ فَارحَم ضَعفَه وَاجمَع بَينِى وَ بَينَهٗ فَقَد عَلِمتَ رِقَّتَهٗ عَلَىَّ وَ شَوقِى اِلَيهِ.

(Amali Sudooq, Noorus Saqlain)

     ♦ HAZRAT YUSUF (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1600)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَلَقَدۡ هَمَّتۡ بِهِۦۖ وَهَمَّ بِهَا لَوۡلَاۤ أَن رَّءَا بُرۡهَـٰنَ رَبِّهِۦۚ كَذَ ٰ⁠لِكَ لِنَصۡرِفَ عَنۡهُ ٱلسُّوۤءَ وَٱلۡفَحۡشَاۤءَۚ إِنَّهُۥ مِنۡ عِبَادِنَا ٱلۡمُخۡلَصِینَ.

"Zulekha Yusuf (as) se Burayi ka iraada kar chuki thi aur Yusuf (as) agar apne Rab ki Burhan na dekh chuka hota to woh bhi usse Burayi ka iraada kar hi leta, taake Ham usse Badi aur Burayi ko door karen. Yaqeenan woh Hamare Chune hue Bandon mein se tha."

(Surah Yusuf: 24)

https://youtu.be/rpymJzfL6x4

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Ismat e Yusuf (as):

وَلَقَدۡ هَمَّتۡ بِهِۦۖ وَهَمَّ بِهَا

Imam Reza (as) ne is Ayat ke zel mein farmaya:

"Is Ayat ka mafhoom ye hai ke Zulekha ne jab Hazrat Yusuf (as) se Jinsi Taskeen (Sex) haasil karne ka iraada kiya tha to iske jawab mein Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne ye iraada kar liya tha ke agar usne zyada majboor kiya to woh use qatl kar denge. Allah Ta'ala ne farmaya ke Hamne Yusuf (as) ko Zina aur Qatl se mehfooz rakha tha."

(Uyoonul Akhbar, Noorus Saqlain)

💕

Imam Reza (as) ne Mamoon ko Yusuf (as) ki Ismat ke bare mein yun jawab diya:

"Agar Yusuf (as) pehle se apne Rab ka Burhan na dekh chuke hote to woh bhi Zulekha ki tarah se Burayi ka iraada kar lete. Lekin woh Parwardigar ki Burhan dekh chuke the aur Masoom the aur Masoom kabhi bhi Badkari ka iraada nahi kar sakta."

"Mere Jadd Imam Sadiq (as) farmate the ke Zulekha Jinsi Taskeen ka iraada kar chuki thi aur Yusuf (as) Badfe'li na karne ka iraada kar chuke the."

(Uyoonul Akhbar, Noorus Saqlain)

Imam Zainul Abedin (as):

"Jab Zulekha ne Behayai ka iraada kiya to usne ghar mein rakhe hue But par kapda dala. Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne Malka se kaha ke ye kya kar rahi ho? Malka ne jawab diya ke ab ham Badkari karenge isliye mein chahti hun ke mera Ma'bood hame Burayi karte hue na dekhe isliye meine uske chehre par kapda dal diya hai, taake ye hamen na dekh sake."

"Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne farmaya: _'Aye Malka! Kuchh to socho! Tum to ek But ka saamna karne se ghabra rahi ho jo na to dekh sakta hai aur na sun sakta hai to kya mein us Khuda ka Haya na karun jo Dekh bhi raha hai, Sun bhi raha hai aur Jo har jagah Haazir o Naazir hai.'_ Is cheez ko Allah Ta'ala ne' Burhan' se tabeer kiya hai."

(Noorus Saqlain)

(To be Cont'd.....)

🤲🏻

Imam Sadiq (as):

Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne Kuwen mein ye Dua padhi:

اَللّٰهُمَّ اِن كَانَتَ الخَطَايَا وَ الذَّنُوبَ قَد وَجهِى عِندَكَ فَلَن تَرفَع لِى الَيكَ صَوتًا وَ لَن تَستَجِيبَ لِى دَعوَةٌ فَاِنِّى اَسئَلُكَ بِحَقِّ الشَّيخ يَعقُوبَ فَارحَم ضَعفَه وَاجمَع بَينِى وَ بَينَهٗ فَقَد عَلِمتَ رِقَّتَهٗ عَلَىَّ وَ شَوقِى اِلَيهِ.

(Amali Sudooq, Noorus Saqlain)

     ♦ HAZRAT YUSUF (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1603)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَٱسۡتَبَقَا ٱلۡبَابَ وَقَدَّتۡ قَمِیصَهُۥ مِن دُبُرࣲ وَأَلۡفَیَا سَیِّدَهَا لَدَا ٱلۡبَابِۚ قَالَتۡ مَا جَزَاۤءُ مَنۡ أَرَادَ بِأَهۡلِكَ سُوۤءًا إِلَّاۤ أَن یُسۡجَنَ أَوۡ عَذَابٌ أَلِیمࣱ.

"Woh dono Darwaze ki taraf daude. Usne peechhe se Yusuf (as) ki Qameez phad di. Darwaze par dono ne uske Shauhar ko maujood paya. Kehne lagi ke us shakhs ki kya Saza honi chahiye jo teri gharwali se Burayi ka iraada kare? Aise shakhs ki iske alawa aur kya Saza ho sakti hai ke use Zindan (Jail) mein dal diya jaye ya use sakht Azaab diya jaye."

(Surah Yusuf: 25)

https://youtu.be/rpymJzfL6x4

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

*Ismat e Yusuf (as):*

وَلَقَدۡ هَمَّتۡ بِهِۦۖ وَهَمَّ بِهَا

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Logon ko raazi rakhna namumkin hai aur logon ki Zabaano ko khamosh rakhna usse bhi zyada mushkil hai. Logon ki Zaban se to Anbiya (as) mehfooz nahi rahe. Logon ne to Hazrat Yusuf (as) par bhi Zina ka ilzaam aaed kiya tha."

(Amaali Sudooq, Noorus Saqlain)

💕

Hazrat Yusuf (as) ke Ismat ki 7 Shakhsiyat Gawah hain:

1. Khud Hazrat Yusuf (as):

Qur'an ne unke qaul naql kiya hai: "Malka ne mujhe apni jaanib raaghib karna chaha."  aur jab unhone Dua ki: "Parwardigar! In Aurton ki Dawate Gunah qabool karne se mujhe Zindan jana zyada pasand hai."  (12:33)

2. Zulekha ne kaha:  "Meine hi use apni jaanib maael karna chaha lekin woh bach nikla."

3. Aziz e Misr ne bhi Hazrat Yusuf (as) ki begunahi ka ailaan kiya. (12:28)

4. Misr ki Aurton ne kaha: "Khuda ki Panah! Hamne is mein koi Burayi nahi dekhi thi." (12:30)

إِنَّا لَنَرَىٰهَا فِی ضَلَـٰلࣲ مُّبِینࣲ.

5. Hazrat Yusuf (as) ki Qameez ka peechhe se phata hona. (12:25)

6. Allah Ta'ala ne Gawahi di:

كَذَ ٰ⁠لِكَ لِنَصۡرِفَ عَنۡهُ ٱلسُّوۤءَ وَٱلۡفَحۡشَاۤءَۚ.

 "Is tarah se Ham usse Burayi aur Behayai door kar rahe the."

7. Iblees: Isne Allah Ta'ala se kaha tha ke mein sab ko gumrah karunga siwae Tere Muskhlis Bando ke. (Saad:83)

إِلَّا عِبَادَكَ مِنۡهُمُ ٱلۡمُخۡلَصِینَ.

Allah Ta'ala ne farmaya:

إِنَّهُۥ مِنۡ عِبَادِنَا ٱلۡمُخۡلَصِینَ.

 "Yaqeenan! Yusuf (as) hamare Mukhlis Bando mein se the."

In Saat Qur'ani Gawahon se sabit hai ke Hazrat Yusuf (as) Masoom the.

(Tafseer e Safi, Noorus Saqlain)

(To be Cont'd.....)

🤲🏻

Imam Sadiq (as):

Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne Kuwen mein ye Dua padhi:

اَللّٰهُمَّ اِن كَانَتَ الخَطَايَا وَ الذَّنُوبَ قَد وَجهِى عِندَكَ فَلَن تَرفَع لِى الَيكَ صَوتًا وَ لَن تَستَجِيبَ لِى دَعوَةٌ فَاِنِّى اَسئَلُكَ بِحَقِّ الشَّيخ يَعقُوبَ فَارحَم ضَعفَه وَاجمَع بَينِى وَ بَينَهٗ فَقَد عَلِمتَ رِقَّتَهٗ عَلَىَّ وَ شَوقِى اِلَيهِ.

(Amali Sudooq, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

     ♦ HAZRAT YUSUF (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1604)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

قَالَ هِیَ رَ ٰ⁠وَدَتۡنِی عَن نَّفۡسِیۚ وَشَهِدَ شَاهِدࣱ مِّنۡ أَهۡلِهَاۤ إِن كَانَ قَمِیصُهُۥ قُدَّ مِن قُبُلࣲ فَصَدَقَتۡ وَهُوَ مِنَ ٱلۡكَـٰذِبِینَ * وَإِن كَانَ قَمِیصُهُۥ قُدَّ مِن دُبُرࣲ فَكَذَبَتۡ وَهُوَ مِنَ ٱلصَّـٰدِقِینَ * فَلَمَّا رَءَا قَمِیصَهُۥ قُدَّ مِن دُبُرࣲ قَالَ إِنَّهُۥ مِن كَیۡدِكُنَّۖ إِنَّ كَیۡدَكُنَّ عَظِیمࣱ * یُوسُفُ أَعۡرِضۡ عَنۡ هَـٰذَاۚ وَٱسۡتَغۡفِرِی لِذَنۢبِكِۖ إِنَّكِ كُنتِ مِنَ ٱلۡخَاطِـِٔینَ.

"Yusuf (as) ne kaha: Yehi Aurat mujhe phansane ki koshish mein thi. Us Aurat ke Khandan mein se ek Gawah ne ye Gawahi di ke uski Qameez aage se phati ho to Aurat Sachchi hai aur ye Jhoota hai. Aur agar uski Qameez peechhe se phati hui ho to Aurat Jhooti hai aur woh Sachcha hai."

"Jab Shauhar ne dekha ke Yusuf (as) ki Qameez peechhe se phati hui hai to usne kaha: Ye tum Aurton ki chalakiyan hain aur yaqeenan tumhari chaalen bahut sakht hoti hain. Yusuf (as)! Is baat ko rehne do aur Aye Aurat! Tu apne Gunah ki maafi maang, tu hi Khatakaron mein se hai."

(Surah Yusuf: 26 - 29)

https://youtu.be/rpymJzfL6x4

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

وَلَقَدۡ هَمَّتۡ بِهِۦۖ وَهَمَّ بِهَا 💕

Muhabbat (Love) hi Wabaal e Jaan bani.

Imam Reza (as):

"Jab Hazrat Yusuf (as) Qaid Khaane mein the to ek Din Zindaanban (Jailor) ne Aap (as) se farmaya: 'Aye Yusuf (as)! Mujhe tum se Muhabbat hai. Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne farmaya: "Khayal rakhna, Zindagi mein mujh par jo bhi Musibaten aayin hain sab "Muhabbat" ki wajah se aayin hain. Meri Khaala ko mujh se Muhabbat thi to usne mujhe chor bana diya tha. Mere Waalid ne Muhabbat ki to unki Muhabbat dekh kar mere Bhaiyyon ne mujh se Hasad kiya. Aziz e Misr ki Biwi ne mujh se Muhabbat ki to mujhe Zindaan (Jail) mein aana pada."

(Khuda jaane ab teri Muhabbat kya gul khilayegi?)

(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi, Noorus Saqlain)

💕

Rasule Khuda (saww):

"Allah Ta'ala saheb e Haya aur Iffat (Modesty) wale shakhs se Muhabbat karta hai aur Fohosh (Ashleel) bakne aur Gaaliya'n dene wale aur bure Saayil se bugz rakhta hai."

(Amaali - Shaikh Toosi, v1, p110)

🌍

Imam Ali (as):

"Duniya ki Mohabbat Waba e Nafs (Infection of the Soul) hai."

(Sharh Dua e Kumail)

💕

Imam Ali (as):

"Jis tarah Suraj aur Raat ikattha nahi ho sakte, isi tarah Allah ki Mohabbat aur Duniya ki mohabbat bhi ek saath nahi ho sakte."

(Tajalliyat e Hikmat, Duniya)

🐍

Imam Ali (as):

"Duniya saa'np (snake) jaisi hai ke uska chhoona to narm o mulayam hai magar uske andar zeher mila hai. Be-khabar nadaan uska aashiq ho jaata hai, magar hosh-mand aaqil oos se darta hai."

(Guftaar e Dil Nasheen, p69)

(To be Cont'd.....)

🤲🏻

Imam Sadiq (as):

Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne Kuwen mein ye Dua padhi:

اَللّٰهُمَّ اِن كَانَتَ الخَطَايَا وَ الذَّنُوبَ قَد وَجهِى عِندَكَ فَلَن تَرفَع لِى الَيكَ صَوتًا وَ لَن تَستَجِيبَ لِى دَعوَةٌ فَاِنِّى اَسئَلُكَ بِحَقِّ الشَّيخ يَعقُوبَ فَارحَم ضَعفَه وَاجمَع بَينِى وَ بَينَهٗ فَقَد عَلِمتَ رِقَّتَهٗ عَلَىَّ وَ شَوقِى اِلَيهِ.

(Amali Sudooq, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

     ♦ HAZRAT YUSUF (as)♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1605)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَقَالَ نِسۡوَةࣱ فِی ٱلۡمَدِینَةِ ٱمۡرَأَتُ ٱلۡعَزِیزِ تُرَ ٰ⁠وِدُ فَتَىٰهَا عَن نَّفۡسِهِۦۖ قَدۡ شَغَفَهَا حُبًّاۖ إِنَّا لَنَرَىٰهَا فِی ضَلَـٰلࣲ مُّبِینࣲ. * فَلَمَّا سَمِعَتۡ بِمَكۡرِهِنَّ أَرۡسَلَتۡ إِلَیۡهِنَّ وَأَعۡتَدَتۡ لَهُنَّ مُتَّكَـࣰٔا وَءَاتَتۡ كُلَّ وَ ٰ⁠حِدَةࣲ مِّنۡهُنَّ سِكِّینࣰا وَقَالَتِ ٱخۡرُجۡ عَلَیۡهِنَّۖ فَلَمَّا رَأَیۡنَهُۥۤ أَكۡبَرۡنَهُۥ وَقَطَّعۡنَ أَیۡدِیَهُنَّ وَقُلۡنَ حَـٰشَ لِلَّهِ مَا هَـٰذَا بَشَرًا إِنۡ هَـٰذَاۤ إِلَّا مَلَكࣱ كَرِیمࣱ.

"Shaher ki Aurton ne kehna shuru kar diya ke Aziz ki Biwi apne Ghulam ke peechhe padi hui hai, use Muhabbat ne beqabu kar diya. Hamari nazar mein woh sareeh Ghalti ka irtekaab kar rahi hai. Jab usne unki Makr par mabni baaten suni to unko Dawat di aur unke liye Takiyadar Mehfil araasta ki aur har ek ke haath mein Chhuri pakda di (jab woh sab phal kaat rahi thin) aur usne Yusuf (as) se kaha ke unke saamne nikal aayen. Jab Aurton ne use dekha to woh dang reh gayin aur apne haath kaat baithi aur kehne lagin: Khuda Panah! Ye Insaan nahi hai, ye koi Buzurg Farishta hai."

(Surah Yusuf: 30 - 31)

https://youtu.be/rpymJzfL6x4

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Imam Zainul Abedin (as):

(Riwayat Cont'd...)

"Aziz e Misr ne apni Biwi se kaha: 'Ye sab kuchh tumhara kara dhara hai, tum Aurton ki chaalen bahut sakht hoti hain. Phir usne Hazrat Yusuf (as) se kaha: "Aye Yusuf (as)! Is baat ko jaane do. Kisi ko Kaano Kaan iski khabar nahi honi chahiye. Lekin Yusuf (as) ne is khabar ko makhfi na rakha aur yun baat mohallat mein pahunchi aur Aurton ne ek doosre se kaha ke Aziz ki Biwi apne ghulam par Dil haar baithi hai aur yaqeenan woh sakht gumrahi mein hai.

Jab Aziz e Misr ki Biwi ne Aurton ki baaten suni to usne unhe apne haan aane ki dawat di aur unke liye ek mehfil araasta ki aur unke liye khaane ka intezaam karaya aur har Aurat ko ek ek Narangi (Orange or Lemon) pakdayi aur sabke haath mein chhuriyan de di. Ye intezaam kar ke woh Yusuf (as) ke paas aayi aur unse kaha: Aap (as) ek dafa un Aurton ke saamne se guzren. Hazrat Yusuf (as) jab Aurton ke saamne se guzre to Auraton ne unka Husn o Shabab dekha to woh mabhoot ho gayin aur kehne lagin: "Khuda ki panah ye Insaan nahi hai ye to mohtaram Farishta hai. Isi asna mein unhone ne Narangi kaati to Naarangi ki bajaye apne haath kaat baithin."

(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi, Noorus Saqlain)

(To be Cont'd.....)

🤲🏻

Imam Sadiq (as):

Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne Kuwen mein ye Dua padhi:

اَللّٰهُمَّ اِن كَانَتَ الخَطَايَا وَ الذَّنُوبَ قَد وَجهِى عِندَكَ فَلَن تَرفَع لِى الَيكَ صَوتًا وَ لَن تَستَجِيبَ لِى دَعوَةٌ فَاِنِّى اَسئَلُكَ بِحَقِّ الشَّيخ يَعقُوبَ فَارحَم ضَعفَه وَاجمَع بَينِى وَ بَينَهٗ فَقَد عَلِمتَ رِقَّتَهٗ عَلَىَّ وَ شَوقِى اِلَيهِ.

(Amali Sudooq, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

     ♦ HAZRAT YUSUF (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1606)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

قَالَتۡ فَذَ ٰ⁠لِكُنَّ ٱلَّذِی لُمۡتُنَّنِی فِیهِۖ وَلَقَدۡ رَ ٰ⁠وَدتُّهُۥ عَن نَّفۡسِهِۦ فَٱسۡتَعۡصَمَۖ وَلَىِٕن لَّمۡ یَفۡعَلۡ مَاۤ ءَامُرُهُۥ لَیُسۡجَنَنَّ وَلَیَكُونࣰا مِّنَ ٱلصَّـٰغِرِینَ *  قَالَ رَبِّ ٱلسِّجۡنُ أَحَبُّ إِلَیَّ مِمَّا یَدۡعُونَنِیۤ إِلَیۡهِۖ وَإِلَّا تَصۡرِفۡ عَنِّی كَیۡدَهُنَّ أَصۡبُ إِلَیۡهِنَّ وَأَكُن مِّنَ ٱلۡجَـٰهِلِینَ *  فَٱسۡتَجَابَ لَهُۥ رَبُّهُۥ فَصَرَفَ عَنۡهُ كَیۡدَهُنَّۚ إِنَّهُۥ هُوَ ٱلسَّمِیعُ ٱلۡعَلِیمُ.

"Us Aurat ne kaha: "Ye hai woh Shakhs jiske mutalliq tumne mujhe malamat ki hai. Beshak meine use apne daman mein phansne ki koshish ki thi magar ye bach nikla aur agar usne mere hukm par amal ba kiya to use Qaid kar liya jayega aur ye zaleel o khwar ho jayega."

"Yusuf (as) ne kaha: "Aye mere Rab! Ye Aurten jis Gunah ki mujhe dawat de rahi hain us Burayi ki be-nisbat mujhe Zindaan (Jail) jana kahin zyada mehboob hai. Aur agar Tu ne mujhe se inki chaalon ko dooe na kiya to mein bhi unki taraf maael ho jaonga aur Jaahilon mein shamil ho jaonga."

"Uske Rab ne uski Dua Manzoor ki aur Aurton ki Chaalen usse hata din. Beshak Woh Sunnewala, Ilmwala hai."

(Surah Yusuf: 32 - 34)

https://youtu.be/rpymJzfL6x4

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

وَلَقَدۡ رَ ٰ⁠وَدتُّهُۥ عَن نَّفۡسِهِۦ فَٱسۡتَعۡصَمَۖ 💕

*Muhabbat (Love) hi Wabaal e Jaan bani.*

Imam Reza (as): (Riwayat Cont'd)

"Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne Bargahe Ahdiyyat mein arz kiya:

"Parwardigar! Mujhe kis Jurm mein Zindaan bheja gaya?"

Allah Ta'ala ne Farmaya:

"Tu ne khud hi Mujh se Zindaan jaane ki khwahish ki thi aur kaha tha ke in Aurton ki dawat qubool karne se to mujhe Zindaan jaana zyada pasand hai. Aur agar iske bajaye tu ye kehta ke unki dawat qubool karne se mujhe Aafiyat ata farma to Mein tujhe kabhi bhi Zindaan na bhejta."

(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi, Noorus Saqlain)

⛓️⛓️

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Hazrat Yusuf (as) firaaq e Yaqoob (as) mein itna roye ke Qaidi tang aa gaye aur unhone Aap (as) se kaha: 'Agar Aap (as) din ko royen to ham Raat ko araam karenge aur agar Raat ko royen to ham din ko araam karenge. Akhirkar Aap (as) ko rone ke liye ek waqt muqarrar karna pad gaya."

(Kitabul Khisaal, Noorus Saqlain)

⛓️⛓️

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Hazrat Yusuf (as) apne Waalid ke firaaq mein Qaidkhane mein itna roye ke Qaidi tang aa gaye. Aap (as) ne un se is baat par musalehat ki ke ek din royenge aur ek din khamosh rahenge."

(Tafseer Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)

(To be Cont'd.....)

🤲🏻

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Hazrat Jibrael (as) Qaid Khaane mein Hazrat Yusuf (as) ke paas aaye aur un se kaha ke har Namaz ke baad ye Dua padho:  (Khuda tumhe Rihai dega)

اَللّٰهُمَّ اجعَل لِى فَرَجًا وَ مَخرَجًا وَ ارزُقنِي مِن حَيثُ احتَسِب وَ مَن حَيثُ لَا احتَسِب.

(Usoole Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)

    27th December 2020, Sunday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

     ♦ HAZRAT YUSUF (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1607)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

ثُمَّ بَدَا لَهُم مِّنۢ بَعۡدِ مَا رَأَوُا۟ ٱلۡـَٔایَـٰتِ لَیَسۡجُنُنَّهُۥ حَتَّىٰ حِینࣲ *  وَدَخَلَ مَعَهُ ٱلسِّجۡنَ فَتَیَانِۖ قَالَ أَحَدُهُمَاۤ إِنِّیۤ أَرَىٰنِیۤ أَعۡصِرُ خَمۡرࣰاۖ وَقَالَ ٱلۡـَٔاخَرُ إِنِّیۤ أَرَىٰنِیۤ أَحۡمِلُ فَوۡقَ رَأۡسِی خُبۡزࣰا تَأۡكُلُ ٱلطَّیۡرُ مِنۡهُۖ نَبِّئۡنَا بِتَأۡوِیلِهِۦۤۖ إِنَّا نَرَىٰكَ مِنَ ٱلۡمُحۡسِنِینَ.

"Phir un logon ko ye Tadbeer soojhi ke ek arse ke liye use Qaid kar den, halanke woh uski Paak-damani ki sareeh Nishaniyan dekh chuke the. Qaidkhane mein do aur Jawan uske saath dakhil hue. Un mein se ek ne kaha: 'meine Khwab mein apne aap ko Sharab nichodte hue dekh hai.' Aur doosre ne kaha: 'meine apne aap ko dekha hai ke mein apne Sar par Roti uthate hue hun jise Parinde kha rahe hain. Aap hame inki Ta'beer batayen, ham Aapko Nek logon mein se samajhte hain."

(Surah Yusuf: 35 - 36)

https://youtu.be/rpymJzfL6x4

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 📚📖 ⛓️⛓️

👉 Tafseer:

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Jab Badshah ke hukm se Yusuf (as) Qaidkhane (Jail) gaye to Allah ne unhe Ta'beer e Khwab ka Ilm Ilhaam (inspire) kiye. Aap (as) Qaidiyon ko unke Khwab ki Ta'beer bataya karte the. Badshah ke do Naukar Qaid ho kar aaye aur unhe Aap (as) ke saath thehraya gaya. Zindaan mein unhone ek Raat guzari to Subah ke waqt un mein se ek Qaidi ne Hazrat Yusuf (as) se kaha ke meine Khwab dekha hai ke mein Sharab nichod raha hun. Doosre ne kaha ke meine Khwab mein dekha hai ke mere Sar par Rotiyan hain aur Parinde unhe noch rahe hain. Hamare in Khwabon ki Ta'beer batayen."

"Aap (as) ne pehle se farmaya ke tum riha ho jaoge aur Badshah ko Sharab pilaoge. Doosre se farmaya ke tumhe Saleeb par latkaya jayega (Crucified), Parinde tumhara Damagh noch noch kar khayenge. Aap (as) ne jo Ta'beer di thi wo harf ba harf sachchi sabit hui."

(Tafseer Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)

🕌

إِنَّا نَرَىٰكَ مِنَ ٱلۡمُحۡسِنِینَ.

Iska ek mafhoom ye bhi hai ke Qaidiyon ne dekha ke Hazrat Yusuf (as) Sahih Ta'beer batate hain. Isse pata chalta hai Khwabon ka Silsila Pichhli Ummaton mein bhi tha aur hadis ke mutabiq Khwab Nabuwwat ka Chheyaliswan (46th) hissa hai. Iski wajah ye hai ke Anbiya (as) bhi aanewale halaat batate hain aur Khwab mein bhi Mustaqbil (future) ki jhalak dikhayi deti hai.

Imam Ali (as):

"Har Insaan ki Qeemat wo Hunar hai jise woh achhe andaaz se anjaam de sakta hai."

Ek Qaidi ne Aap (as) se kaha tha ke meine Angoor ke Teen Khoshe dekhe hain, jinhe meine Badshah ke Jam mein nichoda aur uske baad pilaya hai. Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne farmaya: 'Tum Teen Din ke baad riha ho jaoge aur Badshah ke Saaqi banoge.'

Ek Riwayat mein hai ke doosre Qaidi ne Rotiyon wala Khwab khud ghada tha. Jab Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne uski Ta'beer di to wo Khuda ki Taqdeer ban gayi.

(Hazrat Ali (as) ko test karne ke liye ek Aurat ne Aap (as) ko apne zinda Bete ki Namaz e Janaza padhane ke liye kaha. Aap (as) ne padha bhi di. Baad mein sab ne uske Bete ko sahih mein Murda paya. - waqea sabko pata hoga)

(Majmaul Bayan, Noorus Saqlain)

⛓️⛓️

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Yusuf (as) Zindaan mein Bimar Qaidiyon ki timardari karte the aur Hajatmandon ki madad karte the aur dil khol kar Qaidiyon ki madad kiya karte the. Aap (as) ke inhi Ausaaf ki wajah se Qaidiyon ne Aap (as) se kaha:  "Ham Aapko Nekokaron mein se khayal karte hain."

(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi, Noorus Saqlain)

(To be Cont'd.....)

----------------------------------------------

🤲🏻

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Hazrat Jibrael (as) Qaid Khaane mein Hazrat Yusuf (as) ke paas aaye aur un se kaha ke har Namaz ke baad ye Dua padho: (Khuda tumhe Rihai dega)

اَللّٰهُمَّ اجعَل لِى فَرَجًا وَ مَخرَجًا وَ ارزُقنِي مِن حَيثُ احتَسِب وَ مَن حَيثُ لَا احتَسِب.

(Usoole Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)

    28th December 2020, Monday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

     ♦ HAZRAT YUSUF (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1608)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِ*

*قَالَ لَا یَأۡتِیكُمَا طَعَامࣱ تُرۡزَقَانِهِۦۤ إِلَّا نَبَّأۡتُكُمَا بِتَأۡوِیلِهِۦ قَبۡلَ أَن یَأۡتِیَكُمَاۚ ذَ ٰ⁠لِكُمَا مِمَّا عَلَّمَنِی رَبِّیۤۚ إِنِّی تَرَكۡتُ مِلَّةَ قَوۡمࣲ لَّا یُؤۡمِنُونَ بِٱللَّهِ وَهُم بِٱلۡـَٔاخِرَةِ هُمۡ كَـٰفِرُونَ * وَٱتَّبَعۡتُ مِلَّةَ ءَابَاۤءِیۤ إِبۡرَ ٰ⁠هِیمَ وَإِسۡحَـٰقَ وَیَعۡقُوبَۚ مَا كَانَ لَنَاۤ أَن نُّشۡرِكَ بِٱللَّهِ مِن شَیۡءࣲۚ ذَ ٰ⁠لِكَ مِن فَضۡلِ ٱللَّهِ عَلَیۡنَا وَعَلَى ٱلنَّاسِ وَلَـٰكِنَّ أَكۡثَرَ ٱلنَّاسِ لَا یَشۡكُرُونَ * یَـٰصَـٰحِبَیِ ٱلسِّجۡنِ ءَأَرۡبَابࣱ مُّتَفَرِّقُونَ خَیۡرٌ أَمِ ٱللَّهُ ٱلۡوَ ٰ⁠حِدُ ٱلۡقَهَّارُ * مَا تَعۡبُدُونَ مِن دُونِهِۦۤ إِلَّاۤ أَسۡمَاۤءࣰ سَمَّیۡتُمُوهَاۤ أَنتُمۡ وَءَابَاۤؤُكُم مَّاۤ أَنزَلَ ٱللَّهُ بِهَا مِن سُلۡطَـٰنٍۚ إِنِ ٱلۡحُكۡمُ إِلَّا لِلَّهِ أَمَرَ أَلَّا تَعۡبُدُوۤا۟ إِلَّاۤ إِیَّاهُۚ ذَ ٰ⁠لِكَ ٱلدِّینُ ٱلۡقَیِّمُ وَلَـٰكِنَّ أَكۡثَرَ ٱلنَّاسِ لَا یَعۡلَمُونَ.*

"Yusuf (as) ne kaha: 'Tumhe yahan jo Khana diya jata hai wo Khana aane se pehle mein tumhe iski Ta'beer bata dunga. Iska talluq un Uloom se hai jo mere Rab ne mujhe taleem diye hain. Jo log Allah par Imaan nahi rakhte aur jo Akherat ke Munkir hain, meine un logon ka raasta chhod diya hai."

"Aur meine apne Buzurgon Ibrahim (as), Ishaaq (as) aur Yaqoob (as) ki Millat ki Pairavi ki hai. Hamara ye kaam nahi hai ke Allah ke saath kisi ko Sharik thehrayen. Ye ham par aur tamam Insaano par Allah ka Karam hai, lekin lohon ki aksariyat Shukr ada nahi karti."

"Aye Zindan ke mere do saathiyon! Tum zara socho to sahi ke bahut se mutafarriq alag alag Rab behtar hain ya EK ALLAH jo sab Ghalib hai. Unko chhod kar tum jinki Ibaadat kar rahe ho wo to bas kuchh naam hain jo tumne aur tumhare Aaba o Ajdaad ne rakh liye hain. Allah ne inke liye koi Sanad (Certificate) nazil nahi kiya. Farmabardari ka Haq bas Allah ke liye makhsoos hai. Usne Hukm diya hai ke tum Uske alawa kisi aur ki Ibaadat na karo. Yehi Seedha Deen hai lekin logon ki aksariyat jaanti hi nahi."

(Surah Yusuf: 37 - 40)

https://youtu.be/rpymJzfL6x4

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 📚📖 ⛓️⛓️

👉 Tafseer:

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Jab Yusuf (as) ne ek Qaidi se apni Shifarish ke liye kaha to Jibrael (as) nazil hue aur unhone kaha:

"Aye Yusuf (as)! Rabbul Aalamin tujhe Salam kehta hai aur Salam baad ke baad tujh se kehta hai ke tujhe apni Makhlooq mein Haseen o Jameel kisne banaya? Yusuf (as) ne kaha: Khudaya! Tu ne hi mujhe Haseen banaya. Jibrael (as) ne keh raha hai tere bade Bhaiyyon ki maujoodgi mein tujhe tere Baap ka Manzoor e Nazar kisne banaya? Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne apna Rukhsar Zameen par rakha aur arz kiya: 'Khudaya! Tu ne hi aisa kiya hai. Jibrael (as) ne kaha Allah Farmata hai: 'Tujhe Kuwen se Kisne Najaat di hai?' Yusuf (as) ki cheekh nikal gayi aur kaha: Khudaya! Tu ne hi mujhe Kuwen se Najaat di thi. Hazrat Jibrael (as) ne kaha ke tu ne Khuda ko chhod kar bande se madad talab ki hai. Ab teri saza ye hai ke ab kuchh aur Baras tak tujhe Zindaan mein rehna padega."

🤲🏻

"Jab Mi'aad (Time) puri ho gayi aur Allah ne Aap (as) ko rihai ki Dua maangne ki ijazat di to Aap (as) ne apna Rukhsar Zameen par rakha aur ye Dua maangi:"

*اَللّٰهُمَّ إن كَانَت ذُنُوبِى قَد اَخلَقَت وَجهِى عِندَكَ فَاِنِّى اَتَوَجَّهُ بِوَجهِ اٰبَائِى الصَّالِحِينَ اِبرَاهِيمَ وَ اِسمَاعِيلَ وَ اِسحَاقَ وَ يَعقُوبَ.*

"Allah Ta'ala ne is Dua ki Barkat se Yusuf (as) ko Zindaan se Nijaat di."

(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi, Noorus Saqlain)

     ♦ KHWAB - DREAMS ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1609)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

یَـٰصَـٰحِبَیِ ٱلسِّجۡنِ أَمَّاۤ أَحَدُكُمَا فَیَسۡقِی رَبَّهُۥ خَمۡرࣰاۖ وَأَمَّا ٱلۡـَٔاخَرُ فَیُصۡلَبُ فَتَأۡكُلُ ٱلطَّیۡرُ مِن رَّأۡسِهِۦۚ قُضِیَ ٱلۡأَمۡرُ ٱلَّذِی فِیهِ تَسۡتَفۡتِیَانِ.

"Aye Qaidkhane ke mere do saathiyon! Tum mein se ek apne Rab (Shahe Misr) ko Sharab pilayega aur raha doosra, to use Sooli par chadhaya jayega (Phansi), Parinde uska Sar noch noch kar khayenge. Jo baat tum dono poochh rahe the uska faisla ho gaya hai."

(Surah Yusuf: 41)

https://youtu.be/rpymJzfL6x4

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 📚📖 ⛓️⛓️

👉 Tafseer:  💭

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Khwab 3 qism ke hote hain:

1. Kuchh Khwab Khuda ki taraf se Momin ke liye Bashaarat hote hain.

2. Kuchh Khwab Iblees ki taraf se Insaan ko khaufzada karne ke liye hote hain.

3. Kuchh Khwab Pareshan hote hain.

(Rauza e Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)

💭🌜

Imam Sadiq (as) se sawal kiya gaya:

"Baaz auqat Insaan Khwab dekhta hai to uski Ta'beer uske Khwab ke ain mutabiq hoti hai aur kabhi Insaan Khwab dekhta hai to kuchh bhi wuqu pazeer nahi hota?"

Aap (as) ne farmaya:

"Jab Momin so jata hai to uski Rooh se ek harkat baramad hoti hai jo Aasmaan ki taraf chali jati hai aur wahan Maqam e Taqdeer o Tadbeer par pahunch kar woh kuchh dekhti hai wo Haq hota hai aur jo kuchh woh Zameen par dekhta hai to wo Khwab Pareshan hote hain."

(Amaali e Sudooq, Noorus Saqlain)

🌜💭

Hazrat Ali (as) ne Rasoole Khuda (saww) se poochha ke kya wajah hai ke kabhi Insaan ko Sachche Khwab dikhayi dete hain to kabhi Jhoote Khwab?

Aap (saww) ne farmaya:

"Jab Insaan so jata hai to uski Rooh ko Rabbul Aalamin ke Huzoor mein pesh kiya jata hai. Rooh jo kuchh Rabbul Aalamin ke paas dekhti hai wo Haq hota hai. Phir jab Allah Ta'ala ki taraf se us Rooh ko Jism mein palatne ka Hukm sadir hota hai aur Rooh wapsi ke safar mein Aasmaan o Zameen ke darmiyan hoti hai aur wahan jo kuchh dekhti hai wo Pareshan Khwab hote hain."

(Noorus Saqlain)

Watch on Dreams:

(1) https://youtu.be/AcX21FpMCYg

(2) https://youtu.be/q9aweOAzwCc

🤲🏻

Imam Sadiq (as) se Raavi ne arz kiya: "Aye Farzande Rasool (as)! Kya Mushkelat ke waqt ham bhi ye Dua padh sakte hain jo Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne padhi thi?"

Aap (as) ne farmaya: "Tum ye Dua na padho albatta us jaisi ye Dua padho:"

اَللّٰهُمَّ إنْ كَانَتْ ذُنُوبِىْ قَدْ اَخْلَقَتْ وَجْهِىْ عِنْدَكَ فَاِنِّىْ اَتَوَجَّهُ اِلَيْكَ بِنَبِيِّكَ نَبِيِّ الرَّحْمَةِ مُحَمَّدٍ وَ عَلِىٍّ وَ فَاطِمَةَ وَالْحَسَنِ وَالْحُسَيْنِ وَالْاَئِمَّةِ عَلَيْهِمُ السَّلَامُ.

(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi, Noorus Saqlain)

(To be Cont'd.....)

     14th Jamadi ul Awwal 1442

30th December 2020, Wednesday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

     ♦ KHWAB - DREAMS♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1610)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَقَالَ لِلَّذِی ظَنَّ أَنَّهُۥ نَاجࣲ مِّنۡهُمَا ٱذۡكُرۡنِی عِندَ رَبِّكَ فَأَنسَىٰهُ ٱلشَّیۡطَـٰنُ ذِكۡرَ رَبِّهِۦ فَلَبِثَ فِی ٱلسِّجۡنِ بِضۡعَ سِنِینَ *  وَقَالَ ٱلۡمَلِكُ إِنِّیۤ أَرَىٰ سَبۡعَ بَقَرَ ٰ⁠تࣲ سِمَانࣲ یَأۡكُلُهُنَّ سَبۡعٌ عِجَافࣱ وَسَبۡعَ سُنۢبُلَـٰتٍ خُضۡرࣲ وَأُخَرَ یَابِسَـٰتࣲۖ یَـٰۤأَیُّهَا ٱلۡمَلَأُ أَفۡتُونِی فِی رُءۡیَـٰیَ إِن كُنتُمۡ لِلرُّءۡیَا تَعۡبُرُونَ *  قَالُوۤا۟ أَضۡغَـٰثُ أَحۡلَـٰمࣲۖ وَمَا نَحۡنُ بِتَأۡوِیلِ ٱلۡأَحۡلَـٰمِ بِعَـٰلِمِینَ.

"Phir un mein se jiske mutalliq use khayal tha ke woh Azad ho jayega, usse Yusuf (as) ne kaha ke apne Rab (Shahe Misr) se mera zikr karna, magar Shaitan ne use ghafil kiya ke woh apne Rab (Shahe Misr) se iska zikr karna bhool gaya. Chunanche Yusuf (as) kai Saalon tak mazeed Zindaan mein pada raha."

"Badshah ne kaha ke mein Khwab mein dekh raha hun ke Saat Moti Gayen mein jinko Saat Dubli Gayen kha rahi hain aur Anaaj ke Saat khoshe hare hain aur doosre Khushk (dry) hain."

"Ahle Darbar ne kaha: Pareshan kun Khwab hain aur ham Khwabon ki Ta'beer nahi jaante."

(Surah Yusuf: 42 - 44)

https://youtu.be/rpymJzfL6x4

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 📚📖 ⛓️⛓️

👉 Tafseer:  💭

Hazrat Yusuf (as) ki rehai mein der hone ki wajah pehle ham zikr kar chuke hain. Aap (as) Qaidkhane mein 7 Saal tangi wa sakhti faramosh shuda Insaan ki tarah rahe. Qaidkhane mein woh Insaani Khudsaazi, Rushd o Hidayat, Bimaron ki Ayadat mein masroof rahe.

Shahe Misr jiska naam Walid bin Rayaan tha Aziz e Misr uska Wazir tha. (Tafseer Namoona) Usne Khwab dekha jisse woh pareshan ho gaya aur apne Waziron, Ta'beer batane walon ko jama kiya aur unke saamne apna Khwab sunaya. Uske darbar mein har ek ne apne mutabiq jawab diya. Unki Ta'beer sirf Badshah ki khushamad karne ke liye hua karti thi. Lekin unki Ta'beer sun kar Badshah ko taskeen nahi hui, isliye zaroorat mehsoos hui ke usko shakhs ko hazir kiya jaye jisko Khwab ki Ta'beer mein mahir ho.

🌜💭

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Ek bar Hazrat Fatema Zehra (sa) ne Khwab dekha goya Hasan (as), Husain (as) zabah kar diye gaye hain ya qatl kar diye gaye hain. Ye Khwab dekh kar Aap (sa) ghamgeen huin aur Aap (sa) ne ye Khwab apne Waalid Majid Rasoole Khuda (saww) se bayan kiya.

AanHazrat (saww) ne ye Khwab sun kar awaaz di ke aye Ro'ya ( رؤيا )! Saamne aa. Ro'ya mujassam ho kar (Physical form) Aap (saww) ke saamne aa gaya. Aap (saww) ne usse farmaya: Kya Tu ne meri Beti ko ye manzar dikhaya hai? Usne kaha: 'Nahi ya Rasoolullah (saww)! Phir Aap (saww) ne awaaz de kar farmaya: 'Asghaas ( اصغاث )! Saamne aa. Asghaas mujassam ho kar saamne aaya to Aap (saww) ne farmaya: 'Kya Tu ne meri Beti ko ye manzar dikhaya hai? Usne kaha: Ji haan! Aap (saww) ne farmaya: 'Tu ne aisa kyon kiya?" Usne kaha: "Mein unhe Ghamgeen karna chahta hun." AanHazrat (saww) ne apni Sahebzadi (sa) se farmaya ke sun lo ye kuchh bhi nahi hai."

(Tafseer Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)

Watch on Dreams:

(1) https://youtu.be/AcX21FpMCYg

(2) https://youtu.be/q9aweOAzwCc.

----------------------------------------------

🤲🏻

Imam Sadiq (as) se Raavi ne arz kiya: "Aye Farzande Rasool (as)! Kya Mushkelat ke waqt ham bhi ye Dua padh sakte hain jo Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne padhi thi?"

Aap (as) ne farmaya: "Tum ye Dua na padho albatta us jaisi ye Dua padho:"

اَللّٰهُمَّ إنْ كَانَتْ ذُنُوبِىْ قَدْ اَخْلَقَتْ وَجْهِىْ عِنْدَكَ فَاِنِّىْ اَتَوَجَّهُ اِلَيْكَ بِنَبِيِّكَ نَبِيِّ الرَّحْمَةِ مُحَمَّدٍ وَ عَلِىٍّ وَ فَاطِمَةَ وَالْحَسَنِ وَالْحُسَيْنِ وَالْاَئِمَّةِ عَلَيْهِمُ السَّلَامُ.

(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi, Noorus Saqlain)

(To be Cont'd.....)

   17th Jamadi ul Awwal 1442

   2nd January 2021, Saturday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

     ♦ KHWAB - DREAMS ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1611)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

 قَالُوۤا۟ أَضۡغَـٰثُ أَحۡلَـٰمࣲۖ وَمَا نَحۡنُ بِتَأۡوِیلِ ٱلۡأَحۡلَـٰمِ بِعَـٰلِمِینَ.

"Ahle Darbar ne kaha: *Pareshan kun Khwab* hain aur ham Khwabon ki Ta'beer nahi jaante."

(Surah Yusuf: 44)

https://youtu.be/rpymJzfL6x4

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 📚📖 ⛓️⛓️

👉 Tafseer: 💭

Raavi ne Imam Reza (as) se Arz kiya ke maine Khwab dekha ke ek Pinjre mein 17 Shishyan (Bottles) hain. Woh Pinjra zameen par gira aur us mein maujood Shishyan toot gayin. Is Khwab ki Ta'beer kiya hai?

Aap (as) ne farmaya:

"Agar tu ne sach kaha hai to iski Ta'beer ye hai ke mere Khandan mein se ek shakhs khurooj karega jo sirf 17 Din Hukumat karega, phir mar jayega." Chunanche Mohd bin Ibrahim ne Abis Saraya ke saath khurooj kiya aur 17 Din zinda rehne ke baad mar gaya.

(Rauza e Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)

🌜💭

Ek shakhs ne Imam Sadiq (as) se is Khwab ki Ta'beer maloom ki: 'Ke mein Kufa Shaher se nikal kar aisa jagah jata hun jise mein pehchanta hun aur mein ye dekhta hun ke lakdi ki Shabeeh ya lakdi se hue ek shakhs ki mujhe Shabeeh dikhayi deti hai jo lakdi ke Ghode par sawar hai aur uske haath mein chamakti hui Talwar hai aur mein ye manzar dekh kar ghabra jata hun.'

Aap (as) ne farmaya:

"Tu ek shakhs ko Maali taur par nuqsan pahuchna chahta hai. Lehaza us Khuda ka khauf kha Jisne tujhe paida kiya hai, phir tujhe Maut dega aur us shakhs ko Nuqsaan pahuchne se baaz aa ja."

Us shakhs apne majra sunaya jo ke Imam (as) ke Ta'beer ke ain mutabiq tha.

Imam (as) ne usse farmaya:

"Achha batao kya woh shakhs hamse Muhabbat rakhta hai aur hamare Dushmanon se Bezaari ka izhaar karta hai?"

Usne kaha: "Ji haan, meine jo iraada kiya tha usse Tauba karta hun. Lekin Maula ye bataye, agar woh shakhs Nasibi hota to kya mere liye usko exploit karna jaiz tha?"

Imam (as) ne farmaya:

"Jo tumhe Ameen (Amanatdar-Trustworthy) banaye, uski Amanat uske sipurd kar do, aur jo tum se Khair khwahi ka talabgar ho usse Khair khwahi (Goodness) karo, chahe woh Imam Husain (as) ka Qatil hi kyon na ho."

(Noorus Saqlain)

🌜💭

Nabi Akram (saww):

"Mujhe Yusuf (as) aur uske Karam o Sabr par tajjub hota hai. Jab unse Saat Moti aur Saat Kamzor Gayon ke Khwab ki Ta'beer poochhi gayi to unhone fauran kaise bayan kar di, agar bil farz mein unki jagah hota to mein pehle apni rihai ki shart rakhta phir rihai ke baad Ta'beer batata."

(Majmaul Bayan, Tafseer Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)

(1) https://youtu.be/AcX21FpMCYg

(2) https://youtu.be/q9aweOAzwCc.

Imam Sadiq (as) se Raavi ne arz kiya: "Aye Farzande Rasool (as)! Kya Mushkelat ke waqt ham bhi ye Dua padh sakte hain jo Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne padhi thi?"

Aap (as) ne farmaya: "Tum ye Dua na padho albatta us jaisi ye Dua padho:"

اَللّٰهُمَّ إنْ كَانَتْ ذُنُوبِىْ قَدْ اَخْلَقَتْ وَجْهِىْ عِنْدَكَ فَاِنِّىْ اَتَوَجَّهُ اِلَيْكَ بِنَبِيِّكَ نَبِيِّ الرَّحْمَةِ مُحَمَّدٍ وَ عَلِىٍّ وَ فَاطِمَةَ وَالْحَسَنِ وَالْحُسَيْنِ وَالْاَئِمَّةِ عَلَيْهِمُ السَّلَامُ.

(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi, Noorus Saqlain)

   18th Jamadi ul Awwal 1442

     3rd January 2021, Sunday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

     ♦ KHWAB - DREAMS ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1612)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

 وَقَالَ ٱلَّذِی نَجَا مِنۡهُمَا وَٱدَّكَرَ بَعۡدَ أُمَّةٍ أَنَا۠ أُنَبِّئُكُم بِتَأۡوِیلِهِۦ فَأَرۡسِلُونِ *  یُوسُفُ أَیُّهَا ٱلصِّدِّیقُ أَفۡتِنَا فِی سَبۡعِ بَقَرَ ٰ⁠تࣲ سِمَانࣲ یَأۡكُلُهُنَّ سَبۡعٌ عِجَافࣱ وَسَبۡعِ سُنۢبُلَـٰتٍ خُضۡرࣲ وَأُخَرَ یَابِسَـٰتࣲ لَّعَلِّیۤ أَرۡجِعُ إِلَى ٱلنَّاسِ لَعَلَّهُمۡ یَعۡلَمُونَ.

"Un dono Qaidiyon mein se jo Shakhs bach gaya tha use ek arse ke baad baat yaad aayi. Usne kaha: 'Mein tum logon ko is Khwab ki Ta'beer batata hun, mujhe Qaidkhane mein Yusuf (as) ke paas jaane do."

"(Usne kaha:) Yusuf (as)! Aye Siddiq! Aap hame batayen ke 7 Moti Gayen hain jinhe Kamzor Gayen kha rahi hain aur 7 hare bhare Anaaj ke Baliyan (khoshe) hain aur baqi Khushk (dry) hain, taake mein logon ke paas jaon aur is tarah se woh inki Ta'beer jaan saken."

(Surah Yusuf: 45 - 46)

https://youtu.be/rpymJzfL6x4

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 📚📖 ⛓️⛓️

👉 Tafseer:  💭

Jab Badshah ke Saaqi ne Badshah ko uske Khwab ki Ta'beer sunayi to Badshah ko woh Ta'beer bahut pasand aayi aur usne kaha: 'Use Zindan se riha karke mere paas le aao. Chunanche Shahi Messenger Aap (as) ke paas aaya aur kaha ke ab Aap (as) ki Qais khatm ho chuki hai, lehaza Aap (as) Badshah ke paas chalen.

Is waqae se maloom hota hai ke Ilm wo Azeem Daulat hai jisne Yusuf (as) ko Zindaan se rihai dilayi thi. Ilm sirf Duniya mein karamad nahi hota balke Uqba (Akherat, Hereafter) ki pareshaniyon se bhi Insaan ki Najaat ka sabab banta hai. Jab Yusuf (as) ne Badshah ka bulawa suna to Aap (as) ne kaha: 'Mein is shart par Zindaan se bahar aaonga ke pehle Badshah mere Kirdar ke mutalliq Azaadana Tehqeeq kare aur ja ye sabit ho jaye ke mera damam Gunah se Paak hai to phir mein bahar aa jaunga.'

🌜💭

Hazrat Yusuf (as) ki baat mein kayi Hikmaten hain:

1. Agar aisi shart na lagate to Aapke Kirdar par hamesha ye dhabba baqi reh jata.

2. Koi aur hota to jaldi nikal bhagta, lekin ye Aap (as) ki Sabit Qadami ko zahir karta hai.

3. Aap (as) ne mutaleba kiya ke jitni Aurton ne apni Ungliyan kaati thi unke unhe bula kar unke Kirdar ke bare mein tehqeeq ki jaye. Lekin ye nahi kaha ke Badshah ki Biwi ki bhi Gawahi li jaye, kyonki Aap (as) nahi chahte the ke usko badnaam kiya jaye.

(Noorus Saqlain)

(To be Cont'd.....)

Watch on Dreams:

(1) https://youtu.be/AcX21FpMCYg

(2) https://youtu.be/q9aweOAzwCc.

🤲🏻

Imam Sadiq (as) se Raavi ne arz kiya: "Aye Farzande Rasool (as)! Kya Mushkelat ke waqt ham bhi ye Dua padh sakte hain jo Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne padhi thi?"

Aap (as) ne farmaya: "Tum ye Dua na padho albatta us jaisi ye Dua padho:"

اَللّٰهُمَّ إنْ كَانَتْ ذُنُوبِىْ قَدْ اَخْلَقَتْ وَجْهِىْ عِنْدَكَ فَاِنِّىْ اَتَوَجَّهُ اِلَيْكَ بِنَبِيِّكَ نَبِيِّ الرَّحْمَةِ مُحَمَّدٍ وَ عَلِىٍّ وَ فَاطِمَةَ وَالْحَسَنِ وَالْحُسَيْنِ وَالْاَئِمَّةِ عَلَيْهِمُ السَّلَامُ.

(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi, Noorus Saqlain)

    4th January 2021, Monday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

    ♦ QAIDKHANA - PRISON ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1613)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

 قَالَ تَزۡرَعُونَ سَبۡعَ سِنِینَ دَأَبࣰا فَمَا حَصَدتُّمۡ فَذَرُوهُ فِی سُنۢبُلِهِۦۤ إِلَّا قَلِیلࣰا مِّمَّا تَأۡكُلُونَ *  ثُمَّ یَأۡتِی مِنۢ بَعۡدِ ذَ ٰ⁠لِكَ سَبۡعࣱ شِدَادࣱ یَأۡكُلۡنَ مَا قَدَّمۡتُمۡ لَهُنَّ إِلَّا قَلِیلࣰا مِّمَّا تُحۡصِنُونَ *  ثُمَّ یَأۡتِی مِنۢ بَعۡدِ ذَ ٰ⁠لِكَ عَامࣱ فِیهِ یُغَاثُ ٱلنَّاسُ وَفِیهِ یَعۡصِرُونَ *  وَقَالَ ٱلۡمَلِكُ ٱئۡتُونِی بِهِۦۖ فَلَمَّا جَاۤءَهُ ٱلرَّسُولُ قَالَ ٱرۡجِعۡ إِلَىٰ رَبِّكَ فَسۡـَٔلۡهُ مَا بَالُ ٱلنِّسۡوَةِ ٱلَّـٰتِی قَطَّعۡنَ أَیۡدِیَهُنَّۚ إِنَّ رَبِّی بِكَیۡدِهِنَّ عَلِیمࣱ.

"Yusuf (as) ne kaha: 'Tum 7 Saal tak musalsal Zara'at (Kheti, Farming) karte rahoge. Is arse mein jo Faslen kaatoge un mein se apni Khuraak ke barabar hisse Khoshon (Baliyon) se nikal lo baqi Anaaj Baliyon mein hi rehne do. Phir sakht 7 Saal aayenge. Is dauran wo sab Ghalla (Grain) kha liya jayega jo tumne us waqt ke liye jama kiya hoga. Uske baad phir ek Saal aayega jis mein logon ke liye Baarishen barsayi jayengi aur log Phalon ka Ras nichodenge."

"Aur Badshah ne kaha: 'Use mere paas le aao. Lekin jab Shahi Elchi (Qasid, Messenger) uske paas aaya, usne kaha ke: 'Apne Maalik ke paas wapas chale jao aur usse poochho un Aurton ka kya mamla hai, jinhone apne haath kaat dale the? Yaqeenan mera Maalik unki chaalon se Khoob Waqif hai."

(Surah Yusuf: 47 - 50)

https://youtu.be/rpymJzfL6x4

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 📚📖 ⛓️⛓️

👉 Tafseer:

Baaz riwayat mein hai:

"Hazrat Yusuf (as) Qaid se riha hue aur Badshah e Misr se unki mulaqat hui. Jab Badshah ne unki Hikmat Amez guftugu suni to woh Aap (as) se bahut mutassir hua aur usne kaha: 'Aaj se Aap (as) hamare haan ba waqar andaz mein Sahib e Ikhtiyar ban kar rahenge aur hame Aap (as) ki Amanat par bharosa hai.'

Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne farmaya: 'Agar tum mujhe Iqtedar mein sharik karne ke khwahishmand ho to Zameen ke Khazanon ka mujhe Incharge muqarrar karo, kyonki mein Hifazat karnewala hun. Yani Sarkari Khazane mein Khayanat nahi karunga aur mein mutalliqa umoor se agaahi bhi rakhta hun.'

👉🏻

Is waqea se ye baat sabit hoti hai ke awaamun ki bhalayi ke liye Kafir Hukumat mein shamuliyat jaez hai, kyonki Shahe Misr Kafir tha aur Hazrat Yusuf (as) Allah ke muntakhib Bande the.

🤲🏻 ⛓️⛓️

Hazrat Yusuf (as) Qaid se riha hue to Aap (as) ne Qaidiyon ke haq mein Dua di aur kaha:

"Khudaya! Nek logon ke Dilon par Meherbani Farma aur unhe halaat se bekhabar na rakh."

Chunanche yehi wajah hai ke Qaidiyon ko aam afraad ki ba nisbat halaat e hazra ki zyada khabar hoti hai.

Phir Yusuf (as) ne Zindaan ke Darwaze par ye ibarat kunda karayi thi:

هَذَا قُبُورُ الْأحْيَاءِ وَ بَيْتُ الْأحْزَانِ وَ تَجَرِبَةُ الْأصْدِقَاءِ وَ شَمَاتَةُ الْأعْدَاءِ.

"Ye Ghar Zinda Afraad ke liye Qabr hai aur Ghamon ka Ghar hai. Doston ke Tajarbe ka Maqam hai aur Dushmanon ke Khush hone ka Zariya hai."

(Majmaul Bayan, Noorus Saqlain)

(To be Cont'd.....)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi

    20th Jamadi ul Awwal 1442

     5th January 2021, Tuesday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

    ♦ QAIDKHANA - PRISON ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1614)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

 قَالَ مَا خَطۡبُكُنَّ إِذۡ رَ ٰ⁠وَدتُّنَّ یُوسُفَ عَن نَّفۡسِهِۦۚ قُلۡنَ حَـٰشَ لِلَّهِ مَا عَلِمۡنَا عَلَیۡهِ مِن سُوۤءࣲۚ قَالَتِ ٱمۡرَأَتُ ٱلۡعَزِیزِ ٱلۡـَٔـٰنَ حَصۡحَصَ ٱلۡحَقُّ أَنَا۠ رَ ٰ⁠وَدتُّهُۥ عَن نَّفۡسِهِۦ وَإِنَّهُۥ لَمِنَ ٱلصَّـٰدِقِینَ *  ذَ ٰ⁠لِكَ لِیَعۡلَمَ أَنِّی لَمۡ أَخُنۡهُ بِٱلۡغَیۡبِ وَأَنَّ ٱللَّهَ لَا یَهۡدِی كَیۡدَ ٱلۡخَاۤىِٕنِینَ.

"Badshah ne un Aurton se kaha ke tumhara us waqt kya mamla tha jab tumne Yusuf (as) ko rijhane ki koshish ki thi? Auton ne kaha: 'Hasha Lillah! (Nauzobillah) Hamne us mein koi burayi nahi dekhi thi.' Aziz e Misr ki Biwi ne kaha: 'Ab Haq khul kar saamne aa chuka hai. Meine hi use phuslane ki koshish ki thi jabke woh Sachchon mein se hai. (Yusuf (as) ne kaha:) 'Is Tehqeeq se mera maqsad sirf ye tha ke use ye maloom ho sake ke meine dar pardah usse koi Khayanat nahi ki thi aur Allah Khayanat karnewalon ki chaalon ko kabhi kamyabi se hamkinar nahi karta."

(Surah Yusuf: 51 - 52)

https://youtu.be/rpymJzfL6x4

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 📚📖 ⛓️⛓️

👉 Tafseer:

Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne Shahi Messenger se kaha ke Badshah se kaho ke woh Aurton se poochhe jinhone apne haath kaate the. Aap (as) ne Haath kaatne wali Aurton ka tazkara kiya lekin Aap (as) ne ye nahi kaha ke Aziz e Misr ki Biwi ko bula kar Tehqeeq ki jaye jabke Hazrat (as) ki Badnaami mein usne markazi kirdar ada kiya tha.

Aap (as) ne Malka e Misr ka zikr na kar ke apni Namak halali ka Haq ada kiya tha, kyonki Hazrat (as) nahi chahte the ke jis Khatoon ne kai baras tak unki khidmat ki hai use Adalat ke Kathare mein khada kiya jaye. Baherhal jab Badshah ne Aurton ko bula kar poochha ke us waqt tumhara kiya mamla tha? Sab ne ek zaban ho kar kaha: 'Khuda Gawah hai ke hamne to us mein koi burayi dikhayi nahi di thi. Jab Aziz e Misr ki Biwi ne Aurton ki ye Gawahi suni to usne Akhlaqi jura'at se kaam lete hue apne Gunah ka sare aam aitraf kiya aur kaha ke ab Haq wazeh ho chuka hai, sara kiya dhara mera hi tha. Jab sab ne iqrar kar liya tab Yusuf (as) ne apna maqsad bayan kiya.

(Noorus Saqlain)

🤲🏻 ⛓️⛓️

Hazrat Yusuf (as) Qaid se riha hue to Aap (as) ne Qaidiyon ke haq mein Dua di aur kaha:

"Khudaya! Nek logon ke Dilon par Meherbani Farma aur unhe halaat se bekhabar na rakh."

Chunanche yehi wajah hai ke Qaidiyon ko aam afraad ki ba nisbat halaat e hazra ki zyada khabar hoti hai.

Phir Yusuf (as) ne Zindaan ke Darwaze par ye ibarat kunda karayi thi:

هَذَا قُبُورُ الْأحْيَاءِ وَ بَيْتُ الْأحْزَانِ وَ تَجَرِبَةُ الْأصْدِقَاءِ وَ شَمَاتَةُ الْأعْدَاءِ.

"Ye Ghar Zinda Afraad ke liye Qabr hai aur Ghamon ka Ghar hai. Doston ke Tajarbe ka Maqam hai aur Dushmanon ke Khush hone ka Zariya hai."

(Majmaul Bayan, Noorus Saqlain)

(To be Cont'd.....)
