    21st Jamadi ul Awwal 1442

  6th January 2021, Wednesday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

                 ♦ NAFS ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1615)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَمَاۤ أُبَرِّئُ نَفۡسِیۤۚ إِنَّ ٱلنَّفۡسَ لَأَمَّارَةُۢ بِٱلسُّوۤءِ إِلَّا مَا رَحِمَ رَبِّیۤۚ إِنَّ رَبِّی غَفُورࣱ رَّحِیمࣱ.

"Mein apne *Nafs* ko bhi Begunah qarar nahi deta. *Nafs* to Burayi par uksata hai, haan jis par mere Rab ki Rehmat ho jaye to woh isse mustasna (exception) hota hai. Beshak mera Rab bahut Bakhshnewala, Meherban hai."

(Surah Yusuf: 53)

https://youtu.be/rpymJzfL6x4

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 📚📖 ⛓️⛓️

👉 Tafseer:

Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne 'Nafs e Ammara' ka zikr kiya ke agar Allah ka Rahem na hota wo unko Burayi ki taraf khech leti.

Jab Insaan Duniya ki chakachond mein ghoomta hai to uske andar ke Nafson mein kashmaksh hoti hai, jo Nafs haavi ho jati hai Insaan woh fe'l anjaam deta hai.

Ulama e Akhlaaq ne Nafs ko 3 hisson mein taqseen kiya hai jiska Qur'an mein bhi ishaara hua hai, jis par jo haavi/overpower ho jata hai woh waise hi amal karta hai. :

 1. Nafs e Ammara :

إِنَّ ٱلنَّفۡسَ لَأَمَّارَةُۢ بِٱلسُّوۤءِ

Ye Insaan ko Gunah ki taraf targheeb (attract) deta hai. Use har taraf kheechta hai isliye Ammara kehte hain. Is mein dekha jata hai ke Insaan ka Aql o Imaan kitna mazboot hai.

 2. Nafs e Lawwama:

Qur'an mein Allah ne is Nafs ki Qasam khayi hai:

وَلَااُقْسِمُ بِالنَّفْسِ اللَّوَّامَةِ

Ye Nafs Insaan ko Neki ki taraf khinchta hai. Jab Ammara fail ho jata hai to Lawwamah apni taraf khenchta hai. Insaan apni ghaltiyon se pasheman hota hai, malamat karta hai aur Tauba ki taraf rukh karta hai. Yehi woh Nafs hai jo Insaan ko Gunah se bachaye rakhta hai. Is marhale ko par karne ke liye use Jihaad e Akbar ki zaroorat hoti hai.

3. Nafs e Mutmainnah:

Qur'an mein Allah isko Apni taraf bulata hai:

یَااٴَیَّتُھَا النَّفْسُ الْمُطْمَئِنَّةُ، ارْجِعِی إِلَی رَبِّکِ رَاضِیَةً مَرْضِیَّةً....

Insaan pehle do marhale par kar ke is manzil par pahunch jata. Jahan Sarkash Nafs apne hatiyar dal deta hai, aur Nafs Lawwamah ko tay karte hue Sukoon o Itminan ki Manzil par pahunchta hai jaha Khuda usse Raazi aur woh Usse raazi ho jata hai.

Imam Husain (as) ko Allah ne isi tarah mukhtib kiya tha.

🕌

Imam Ali (as):

"Duniya ki Mohabbat *Waba e Nafs* (Infection of the Soul) hai."

(Sharh Dua e Kumail)

🕌

Imam Ali (as):

"Jab Aa'nkhein *Nafs* ki pasandida cheezein dekhne lagein to Dil anjaam se Andha ho jaata hai."

(Aqwaal e Masoomeen (as), p193)

🕌

Rasule Khuda (saww):

"Afzal Jihad khwaishaat ke khilaaf *Nafs ki Jihad* hai aur Dunyavi Lazzato'n ko chhodna (Jihad) hai."

(Meezan ul Hikmah, v2)

🕌

Rasule Khuda (saww):

"Achche kaamo'n ko zabardasti karne ki koshish karo aur apne *Nafs* par inko apnane ke liye sakhti karo, kyunki burayi to insaan ki Fitrat mein shamil hi hai."

(Meezan ul Hikmah, v5)

🕌

Imam Baqir (as):

"Apna khwaab sirf us Momin se bayan karo jiska dil Hasad aur Adawat se khaali ho aur *Nafs e Lawwama* (sarkash) ka taabedar na ho."

(Tehzeeb ul Islam, p197)

🤲🏻

Bare Ilaha! Hamari Madad farma ke ham Teri Qur'an ki Noorani Ayaat ke zere Saaya 'Nafs e Ammara' se 'Nafs e Lawwama' aur 'Nafs e Mutmainna' ki taraf irteqa (moving up) kar rahe hain. Aur ek Mutmain aur Sukoon Rooh paida karen.

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

    22nd Jamadi ul Awwal 1442

    7th January 2021, Thursday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

     ♦ HAZRAT YUSUF (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1616)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَقَالَ ٱلۡمَلِكُ ٱئۡتُونِی بِهِۦۤ أَسۡتَخۡلِصۡهُ لِنَفۡسِیۖ فَلَمَّا كَلَّمَهُۥ قَالَ إِنَّكَ ٱلۡیَوۡمَ لَدَیۡنَا مَكِینٌ أَمِینࣱ *  قَالَ ٱجۡعَلۡنِی عَلَىٰ خَزَاۤىِٕنِ ٱلۡأَرۡضِۖ إِنِّی حَفِیظٌ عَلِیمࣱ.

"Badshah ne kaha: 'Use mere paas le aao taake mein use apne liye Makhsoos kar lun. Jab Yusuf (as) ne Badshah se guftugu ki to usne kaha:' Aaj se Aap (as) hamare haan qadr o manzelat rakhne wale hain aur hamen Aap (as) ki Amanat par bharosa hai. Yusuf (as) ne kaha: 'Mujhe Zameen ke Khazanon par muqarrar kar do, mein hifazat karnewala aur Ilm rakhnewala hun."

(Surah Yusuf: 54 - 55)

https://youtu.be/rpymJzfL6x4

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 📚📖 💰

👉 Tafseer:  

Imam Reza (as) se ek shakhs ne arz kiya: 'Hame tajjub hai Aap (as) Zalim Hukmuran Mamoon ki Wali Ahdi kaise qubool ki?'

Aap (as) ne farmaya:

"To phir sun lo! Badshah e Misr Mushrik tha aur Hazrat Yusuf (as) Nabi the, iske bawajood unhone usse kaha tha ke mujhe Zameen ke Khazanon ka Incharge bana do, mein hifazat karnewala aur Ilm rakhnewala shakhs hun. Mujhe to Mamoon ne Wali Ahdi qubool karne par majboor kar diya tha, agar mein ye mansab qubool na karta to woh mujhe qatl kara deta. Agar Yusuf (as) ne mansab qubool karke ghalti nahi ki thi to meine ye mansab qubool kar ke kaun si khata ki hai?"

(Uyoonul Akhbar, Noorus Saqlain)

👉🏻

Yahi jawab unke liye hai jo sawal karte hain ke Hazrat Ali (as) ne Shekhain ki madad kyon ki jabke maloom tha ke woh Ghasib hain. Hazrat Ali (as) ne unki madad nahi ki balke Islam ki madad ki. Unhone wahi support kiya jahan Islam ka maslah aaya. Iska matlab ye bilkul nahi nikalta ke unko qubool kar liya.

☺️🙌🏻

Imam Sadiq (as) se sawal hua ke Insaan apni tareef kar sakta hai?

Aap (as) ne farmaya ke kar sakta hai jaise Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne kaha ke 'mein Hafeez aur Ameen hun.' Hazrat Saleh (as) ne kaha ke 'mein tumhara Khair khwah hun.'

(Tafseer Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)

🕌

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Jo log 'Tark e Duniya' ko hi apne liye Sa'adat samajhte hain aur doosron ko bhi iski dawat dete hain unhe zara Hazrat Sulaiman (as) aur Hazrat Yusuf (as) ki misalon par bhi ghaur karna chahiye."

(Al Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)

👉🏻

Yahan Imam (as) ne Sufiyat ki taraf ishaara kiya hai. Imam (as) ki bahut si riwayaat hain jaha Aap (as) ne Sufiyat ki mazammat (Condemn) kiya hai.

🤲🏻

Dua-e-Hafeza: Har Namaaz ke baad padhe:

Rasoole Khuda (saww) & Ali (as):

سُبْحَانَ مَنْ لَايَعْتَدِىْ عَلٰى اَهْلِ مَمْلَكَتِهِ سُبْحَانَ مَنْ لَا يَاْخُذُ اَهْلَ الْاَرْضِ بِاَلْوَانِ الْعَذَابِ سُبْحَانَ الرَّؤُفِ الرَّحِيْمِ اَللّٰهُمَّ اجْعَلْ لِىْ فِىْ قَلْبِىْ نُوْرًا وَ بَصَرًا وَ فَهْمًا وَ عِلْمًا اِنَّكَ عَلٰى كُلِّشَىْ ءٍ قَدِيْرٌ ۔

(Jibrael (as) is Dua ko Hazrat Yusuf (as) taleem di thi jab woh Qaidkhane mein the. - Mafateeh)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

   23rd Jamadi ul Awwal 1442

      8th January 2021, Friday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

     ♦ HAZRAT YUSUF (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1617)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَقَالَ ٱلۡمَلِكُ ٱئۡتُونِی بِهِۦۤ أَسۡتَخۡلِصۡهُ لِنَفۡسِیۖ فَلَمَّا كَلَّمَهُۥ قَالَ إِنَّكَ ٱلۡیَوۡمَ لَدَیۡنَا مَكِینٌ أَمِینࣱ *  قَالَ ٱجۡعَلۡنِی عَلَىٰ خَزَاۤىِٕنِ ٱلۡأَرۡضِۖ إِنِّی حَفِیظٌ عَلِیمࣱ.

"Badshah ne kaha: 'Use mere paas le aao taake mein use apne liye Makhsoos kar lun. Jab Yusuf (as) ne Badshah se guftugu ki to usne kaha:' Aaj se Aap (as) hamare haan qadr o manzelat rakhne wale hain aur hamen Aap (as) ki Amanat par bharosa hai. Yusuf (as) ne kaha: 'Mujhe Zameen ke Khazanon par muqarrar kar do, mein hifazat karnewala aur Ilm rakhnewala hun."

(Surah Yusuf: 54 - 55)

https://youtu.be/rpymJzfL6x4

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 📚📖 💰

👉 Tafseer:  

Imam Reza (as):

"Hazrat Yusuf (as) jab Paidawar ke Vazir (Agriculture Minister) muqarrar hue to 7 Saal Baarish hoti rahi aur khub Ghalla (Anaaj) paida hua. Aap (as) ne in Saalon mein ye ehtiyat barti ke logon ko unki zaroorat ke barabar Dana nikalne ki ijazat di aur zaroorat se zyada Fasal Baliyon sameet khareedte rahe aur use bade bade Godowns mein mehfooz karate rahe. Phir jab Khushk (dry) Saali shuru hui to Aap (as) ne Khushk Saali ke pehle Saal Dirhamon Dinar ke ewaz forokht (sell) kiya yahan tak ke logon ke gharon mein jitne bhi Dirhamon Dinar the wo khatm ho gaye aur tamam Dirhamon Dinar Yusuf (as) ke khazane mein jama ho gaye."

"Phir doosra Saal shuru hua to Aap (as) ne Zewraat o Jawaher ke ewaz logon ko Ghalla faraham kiya, yahan tak ke poore Misr mein kisi ke paas Zewar tak na raha. Tamam Zewar Yusuf (as) ke Khazane mein jama ho gaye. Phir 3rd Dry year shuru hua to Aap (as) ne Janwar aur Maveshiyon (Animals) ke ewaz logon ko Ghalla faraham kiya aur Misr mein kisi ke paas Jaanwar na rahe. Sab ke sab Janwar Yusuf (as) ki Sarkari tehveel mein chale gaye. Phir Chautha Saal shuru hua to Aap (as) ne logon ko unke Ghulamon aur Kaneezon ke ewaz Ghalla faraham kiya, yahan tak ke poore Misr mein kisi ke paas Ghulam aur Kaneez baqi na rahe. Tamam Ghulam aur Kaneezen Hazrat (as) ki tehveel mein aa gayin.

Phir Khushk Saali ka Paanchva Saal shuru hua to Aap (as) ne logon ko unke Zameenon aur Gharon ke ewaz Ghalla faraham kiya, yahan tak ke poore Misr ki Zameenen aur Makanat Hazrat Yusuf (as) ki milkiyat mein chale gaye. Phir Khushk Saali ka Chhata Saal shuru hua to Aap (as) ne un ki Anhaar aur Kisano ke ewaz Ghalla faraham kiya, yahan tak ke Misr ki tamam Nehren aur Rajbahen Hazrat Yusuf (as) ki milkiyat mein chali gayin."

"Phir Khushk Saali ka Saatwan (7th) Saal shuru hua to logon ke paas Ghalla khareedne ke liye kuchh bhi nahi tha. Unhone apne aapko Hazrat Yusuf (as) ka Ghulam bana liya aur Ghalla hasil kiya. Chunanche is Saal poore Misr ke log Hazrat Yusuf (as) ki Ghulami mein aa gaye. Log ye kehne lage aaj tak Khuda ne kisi ko Hazrat Yusuf (as) se zyada Ilm o Hikmat ata nahi ki. Woh hamari Raqam se le kar hamari Jaanon tak ke Malik ban gaya hai."

(Hadis to be Cont'd......)

🤲🏻

"Aye Aziz e Misr! Ham aur hamare Ahlo Ayaal Musibat mein giraftar ho chuke hain aur ham kuchh mamooli si poonji laye hain. Aap (as) hame bhar poor Ghalla enayat karen aur hame Khairat karen. Beshak Allah Khairat karne walon ko Jaza deta hai." (12:88)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

    24th Jamadi ul Awwal 1442

    9th January 2021, Saturday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

     ♦ HAZRAT YUSUF (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1618)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَكَذَ ٰ⁠لِكَ مَكَّنَّا لِیُوسُفَ فِی ٱلۡأَرۡضِ یَتَبَوَّأُ مِنۡهَا حَیۡثُ یَشَاۤءُۚ نُصِیبُ بِرَحۡمَتِنَا مَن نَّشَاۤءُۖ وَلَا نُضِیعُ أَجۡرَ ٱلۡمُحۡسِنِینَ *  وَلَأَجۡرُ ٱلۡـَٔاخِرَةِ خَیۡرࣱ لِّلَّذِینَ ءَامَنُوا۟ وَكَانُوا۟ یَتَّقُونَ.

"Is tarah se Hamne Yusuf (as) ke liye is Sarzameen ke Iqtedar ki rah hamwar ki, woh Mukhtar tha, jahan chahe apni jagah banaye. Ham Apni Rehmat se jise chahen nawaz dete hain aur Ham Nekokaron ke Ajr ko zaye nahi karte. Aur Yaqeenan Akherat ka Ajr un logon ke liye zyada behtar hai jo Imaan laye aur Parhezgari ke taqazon par amal paira rahe."

(Surah Yusuf: 56 - 57)

https://youtu.be/rpymJzfL6x4

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 📚📖 💰

👉 Tafseer:

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Hazrat Yusuf (as) hudood e mamlekat Misr se Yemen tak phaili hui thi. Aap (as) ne bhooki Khalqe Khuda (creature) ko Ghalla (Food grains) faraham kiya tha. Aap (as) Hukmaran ho kar bhi Jadae Haq se kabhi munharif nahi hue the. Aap (as) hamesha sach kehte the aur Haq par amal karte the. Hamne to kisi ko un par tanqeed karte hue nahi dekha."

(Al Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)

🌾🎋🌿🌱

Imam Reza (as): (Cont'd)

"Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne Shahe Misr se kaha: "Aap ne mulaheza farmaya mujhe Khuda ne Misr mein Hukumat ata ki hai aur aaj mein is Mulk ke siya o safed ka Malik ban chuka hun, lekin mein apni Tadbeer (Plan) ko inke liye wabal banana nahi chahta. Ye Khuda ka Ehsaan hai ke Usne inhe mere haathon Qahet Saali (Famine) se Najat ata ki hai. Ab aap farmayen ke hame kiya karna chahiye?" Badshah ne kaha: "Aap (as) ki jo bhi Raye hogi us par amal karen."

Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne kaha:

"Badshah Salamat! Mein Khuda ko aur Uske baad aapko gawah bana kar ailaan karta hun ke tamam Ahle Mamlakat ko Azaad karta hun aur inki Zameenen, Maveshi, Ghulam aur tamam deegar ashiya unhe wapas karta hun aur aapka ata kardah Takht o Taj bhi aapko wapas karta hun, lekin aap bhi mujh se wada karen ke ainda aap meri hi Seerat par amal karenge aur Umoor e Mamlakat mein mujh se mashwara karte rahenge."

Badshah ne kaha: "Mere liye Sharaf o Fakhr hai. Mein hamesha Aap (as) ki Seerat par hi amal karunga aur Aap (as) ke mashware ke baghair koi faisla nahi karunga. Agar Aap (as) na hote to mein is Qahet Saali se Ohda baraa nahi ho sakta tha. Aap (as) ki wajah se to meri Hukumat mazboot hui aur aaj mein bhi Khudaye Wahdahu Lasharik ki Tauheed aur Aap (as) ki Risalat ka iqraar karta hun. Aap (as) apne mansab par qaem rahen aur Aap (as) hamesha hamari nazar mein bawaqar rahenge aur hamen Aap (as) ki Amanat par etemad hai."

(Majmaul Bayan, Noorus Saqlain)

(To be Cont'd....)

🤲🏻

"Aye Aziz e Misr! Ham aur hamare Ahlo Ayaal Musibat mein giraftar ho chuke hain aur ham kuchh mamooli si poonji laye hain. Aap (as) hame bhar poor Ghalla enayat karen aur hame Khairat karen. Beshak Allah Khairat karne walon ko Jaza deta hai." (12:88)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

    10th January 2021, Sunday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

     ♦ HAZRAT YUSUF (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1619)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَكَذَ ٰ⁠لِكَ مَكَّنَّا لِیُوسُفَ فِی ٱلۡأَرۡضِ یَتَبَوَّأُ مِنۡهَا حَیۡثُ یَشَاۤءُۚ نُصِیبُ بِرَحۡمَتِنَا مَن نَّشَاۤءُۖ وَلَا نُضِیعُ أَجۡرَ ٱلۡمُحۡسِنِینَ *  وَلَأَجۡرُ ٱلۡـَٔاخِرَةِ خَیۡرࣱ لِّلَّذِینَ ءَامَنُوا۟ وَكَانُوا۟ یَتَّقُونَ.

"Is tarah se Hamne Yusuf (as) ke liye is Sarzameen ke Iqtedar ki rah hamwar ki, woh Mukhtar tha, jahan chahe apni jagah banaye. Ham Apni Rehmat se jise chahen nawaz dete hain aur Ham Nekokaron ke Ajr ko zaye nahi karte. Aur Yaqeenan Akherat ka Ajr un logon ke liye zyada behtar hai jo Imaan laye aur Parhezgari ke taqazon par amal paira rahe."

(Surah Yusuf: 56 - 57)

https://youtu.be/rpymJzfL6x4

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 📚📖 💰

👉 Tafseer:

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Ek Azad Insaan apne tamam halaat mein azad hi rehta hai us par khwah kitne hi Masaeb kyon na aayen. Phir bhi woh Sabr o Isteqamat ka muzahera karta hai. Masaeb uski Shakhsiyyat ko khatm nahi kar sakte, khwah Zindaan mein kyon na chala jaye. Khwah kisi ki ghulami mein bhi kyon na chala jaye phir bhi woh apne aala atwar ko nahi chhodta. Allah Ta'ala akhirkar uske dukhon ka khatema karta hai aur use Sukh aur Izzat ata karta hai. Uske liye Yusuf Siddiq (as) ki Zindagi ki Misaal dekho. Unhe Ghulam banaya gaya, forokht kiya gaya (sold), un par Zulm o Sitam dhaye gaye aur woh Qaid mein gaye, magar unhone har jagah par apni Azadi aur Bartari ko qaem rakha. Kuwen ki tareeki aur tanhai bhi unhe nuqsan na de saki. Akhirkar Allah Ta'ala ne unhe Izzat di aur jo uska Malik tha woh unka Mamlook (Subject - Parja) bana aur Khuda ne unhe Nabuwwat o Risalat ata ki aur unke zariye se poori Mamlakat ko Qahet Saali (Famine) se Najaat ata ki. Hamesha Sabr ka Phal mitha hota hai. Lehaza logon! Tum bhi Sabr karo aur apne aap ko Sabr ka khugar (aadi) banao. Khuda tumhe iska Ajr dega."

(Usoole Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)

👑

Imam Baqir (as):

"Hazrat Yusuf (as) ki Hudood e Mamlekat (Ruling boundaries) Misr aur uske Sehra tak mehdood thi. Isse zyada ilaaqe par unki Hukumat nahi thi."

(Tafseer Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)

(To be Cont'd....)

🤲🏻

"Aye Aziz e Misr! Ham aur hamare Ahlo Ayaal Musibat mein giraftar ho chuke hain aur ham kuchh mamooli si poonji laye hain. Aap (as) hame bhar poor Ghalla enayat karen aur hame Khairat karen. Beshak Allah Khairat karne walon ko Jaza deta hai." (12:88)

    26th Jamadi ul Awwal 1442

    11th January 2021, Monday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

     ♦ HAZRAT YUSUF (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1620)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَجَاۤءَ إِخۡوَةُ یُوسُفَ فَدَخَلُوا۟ عَلَیۡهِ فَعَرَفَهُمۡ وَهُمۡ لَهُۥ مُنكِرُونَ.

"Yusuf (as) ke bhai uske paas aaye. Yusuf (as) ne unhe pehchan liya, magar unhone Yusuf (as) ko na pehchana."

(Surah Yusuf: 58)

https://youtu.be/rpymJzfL6x4

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 📚📖 🙈

👉

Is Ayat mein Allah Ta'ala ne bayan kiya ke Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne pehli bar hi apne Bhaiyon ko pehchan liya tha, lekin jab tak unhone na chaha us waqt tak Bhai unhe nahi pehchan sake the. Isse sabit hota hai ke Hujjat e Khuda ki ek Alamat (Sign) ye bhi hai ke jab tak woh khud na chahe tab tak use koi pehchan nahi sakta. Yehi wajah hai ke Riwayat e Masoomeen (as) mein mazkoor hai ke ja Qaim e Aale Muhammad (atfs) Zahoor farmayenge to har shakhs unhe dekh kar pehchan lega aur log kahenge ke meine to inhe falan falan maqam par dekha tha. Baaz log kahenge ke unhone to falan Mushkil ghadi mein meri madad ki thi. Isi tarah ka ek waqea pesh e khidmat hai:

👉🏻

*Shahadat Imam Musa Kazim (as):*

Imam Musa Kazim (as) ko jab Sindi bin Shahak Darogha ne Haroon ke hukm se Zeher diya to us waqt Aap (as) ne Qaidkhane ke Darban Musayyab se kaha:

"Musayyab! Ye Najis Sindi bin Shahak ye samajhta hai ke mere marne ke baad mujhe Ghusl o Kafan dega aur mujhe Dafn karega. Aisa kabhi nahi hoga. Jab tum log mera Janaza le kar Maqabire Quraish (Kazmain) pahuncho to wahan meri Lehed (Grave) banana aur meri Qabr ko 4 Ungliyon se zyada buland na banana aur khayal rakhna Barkat ke husool ke liye meri Qabr ki Mitti na uthana. Yaad rakho! Mere Dada Hazrat Imam Husain (as) ki Turbat ke alawa baqi har Turbat ka khana Haraam hai, albatta Syedus Shohada Imam Husain (as) ki Turbat ko Allah ne hamare Shiyon aur Doston ke liye Waseela e Shifa banaya hai."

Musayyab ka bayan hai ke itne mein Zindaan mein ek shakhs ko dekha jo mere Aaqa o Maula Hazrat Imam Musa Kazim (as) ki mukammal shabeeh tha. Meine Imam Ali Reza (as) ko bachpane mein dekha tha. Meine chaha ke aane wale se kuchh sawal karun to Imam Musa Kazim (as) ne cheekh ka mujh se farmaya ke meine tujhe mana nahi kiya tha?

Musayyab kehte hain ke mein khamosh ho kar baith gaya. Kuchh der baad aanewali Shakhsiyyat bhi meri nigahon se ghayab ho gayi. Itne mein Imam (as) ki Shahadat waqe ho gayi. Meine Imam (as) ki Shahadat ki ittela Sindi bin Shahak ko di. Woh apne saathiyon samit aaya aur unhone Imam (as) ko Ghusl dena shuru kiya. Mein khuli Aankhon se dekhta raha ke unke Haath Imam tak nahi pahunch rahe the aur phir meine pehle aanewali Shakhsiyyat ko dekha jo aa kar unke saath Ghusl Kafan mein sharik ho gaya. Imam (as) ko wohi Ghusl o Kafan dete rahe jabke Sindi bin Shahak aur uske saathi ye samajhte rahe ke ye shakhs unki madad kar raha hai. Woh use nahi pehchante the. Jab Ghusl o Kafan ki takmeel ho gayi to us Shakhsiyyat ne mujhe mukhatab karke kaha:

"Musayyab! Har cheez mein shak kar lena lekin mere mutalliq kabhi shak na karna. Mein tera Imam aur tera Maula hun aur apne Waalid ke baad Khuda ki taraf se tujh par Hujjat hun. *Meri misaal Hazrat Yusuf (as) ki si hai. Unhone apne Bhaiyyon ko pehchan liya tha jabke Bhai use nahi pehchan sake the."*

Musayyab kehte hain ke uske baad Hazrat Musa Kazim (as) ka Janaza uthaya gaya aur unhe Maqabir e Quraish (Kazmain) mein Dafn kiya gaya. Aap (as) ki Qabr ko Zameen se 4 ungal buland kiya gaya. Baad mein Aqeedatmandon ne Aap (as) ki Qabr ko ooncha kiya aur Rauza (Shrine) tameer kiya.

(Uyoonul Akhbar, Noorus Saqlain)

----------------------------------------------

🤲🏻

"Aye Aziz e Misr! Ham aur hamare Ahlo Ayaal Musibat mein giraftar ho chuke hain aur ham kuchh mamooli si poonji laye hain. Aap (as) hame bhar poor Ghalla enayat karen aur hame Khairat karen. Beshak Allah Khairat karne walon ko Jaza deta hai." (12:88)

Imam Baqir (as):

"Hazrat Yusuf (as) ki judai Hazrat Yaqoob (as) ke liye badi shaaq, sakht sabit hui. Aap (as) Yusuf (as) ki judai ke gham mein itna roye ke Aankhe Safed ho gayin. Phir Khushk Saali ka Saal shuru hua to Aap (as) ke ghar ka Ghalla khatm ho gaya aur Kan'an mein shohrat hui ke Misr ka Badshah logon ko Ghalla faraham kar raha hai. Us waqt Hazrat Yusuf (as) Misr ke iqtedar par fayez ho chuke the.

Hazrat Yaqoob (as) ne apne Beton ko kuchh Raqam de kar farmaya: 'Tum Misr chale jao aur wahan se Khandan ke liye Ghalla le aao. Hazrat Yusuf (as) ke Bhaiyyon ne safar kiya aur Misr pahunch gaye aur Hazrat Yusuf (as) ke saamne gaye. Aap (as) ne pehchan liya lekin Aap (as) ke Rob e Shahi ki wajah se Aap (as) ko na pehchan sake.

     ♦ HAZRAT YUSUF (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1622)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَلَمَّا جَهَّزَهُم بِجَهَازِهِمۡ قَالَ ٱئۡتُونِی بِأَخࣲ لَّكُم مِّنۡ أَبِیكُمۡۚ أَلَا تَرَوۡنَ أَنِّیۤ أُوفِی ٱلۡكَیۡلَ وَأَنَا۠ خَیۡرُ ٱلۡمُنزِلِینَ *  فَإِن لَّمۡ تَأۡتُونِی بِهِۦ فَلَا كَیۡلَ لَكُمۡ عِندِی وَلَا تَقۡرَبُونِ *  قَالُوا۟ سَنُرَ ٰ⁠وِدُ عَنۡهُ أَبَاهُ وَإِنَّا لَفَـٰعِلُونَ * وَقَالَ لِفِتۡیَـٰنِهِ ٱجۡعَلُوا۟ بِضَـٰعَتَهُمۡ فِی رِحَالِهِمۡ لَعَلَّهُمۡ یَعۡرِفُونَهَاۤ إِذَا ٱنقَلَبُوۤا۟ إِلَىٰۤ أَهۡلِهِمۡ لَعَلَّهُمۡ یَرۡجِعُونَ.

"Aur jab Yusuf (as) ne unka Samaan tayyar karaya to kaha ke apne Pidari Bhai ko mere paas laana. Kya tum nahi dekhte ke mein kis tarah Paimana (Measure) bhar kar deta hun aur mein bahut achha Mehman Nawaz hun. Aur agar tum use mere paas le kar na aaye to phir tumhare liye mere paas koi Ghalla (Grain) nahi hai aur na hi mere qareeb aana. Unhone kaha ke ham uske mutalliq uske Waalid ko qael karne ki koshish karenge aur poori koshish karenge. Aur Yusuf (as) ne apne Ghulamon se kaha ke unki Raqam bhi unke Samaan mein rakh do, taake ghar pahunch kar apna wapas kiya hua Maal pehchan len aur is tarah se wapas aa jayen."

(Surah Yusuf: 59 - 62)

https://youtu.be/rpymJzfL6x4

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 📚📖 🙈

👉 Tafseer:

Imam Baqir (as): (Cont'd)

".....Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne un se Raqam li aur apne Naukaron se farmaya ke in logon ko sab se pehle Ghalla de do aur jab Ghalla bhar kar farigh ho jao to unki Poonji bhi unki Bori mein rakh do, lekin ek baat ka khayal rakhna inhe ye na batana ke inki Raqam inhe wapas ki gayi hai.

Naukaron ne Hazrat (as) ke farman par amal kiya. Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne apne Bhaiyyon se kaha ke meine suna hai ke tumhare do Bhai aur bhi hain. Batao ab woh kaha hain?' Unhone kaha: 'Badshah Salamat! *Pehle hamare do Bhai the lekin hamare ek Bhai ko Bhaidya kha gaya tha* , jabke hamara doosra Bhai is waqt apne Waalid ke paas hai aur hamare Waalid use apne se juda nahi hone dete.'

Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne farmaya: 'Achha suno! Jab agli martaba Ghalla lene aao to apne Bhai ko bhi apne saath le aao. Agar tumne aisa na kiya to meri taraf se tumhe Ghalla nahi milega aur mere qareeb phatakne ki bhi zehmat na karna.' Yusuf (as) ke Bhaiyyon ne kaha: 'Agarche ye kaam khasa mushkil hai, phir bhi ham poori koshish kar ke Waalid ko qael karenge aur apne Bhai ko yahan le aayenge.'......"

(Tafseer Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)

(To be Cont'd......)

   14th January 2021, Thursday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

     ♦ HAZRAT YUSUF (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1623)

*فَلَمَّا رَجَعُوۤا۟ إِلَىٰۤ أَبِیهِمۡ قَالُوا۟ یَـٰۤأَبَانَا مُنِعَ مِنَّا ٱلۡكَیۡلُ فَأَرۡسِلۡ مَعَنَاۤ أَخَانَا نَكۡتَلۡ وَإِنَّا لَهُۥ لَحَـٰفِظُونَ *  قَالَ هَلۡ ءَامَنُكُمۡ عَلَیۡهِ إِلَّا كَمَاۤ أَمِنتُكُمۡ عَلَىٰۤ أَخِیهِ مِن قَبۡلُ فَٱللَّهُ خَیۡرٌ حَـٰفِظࣰاۖ وَهُوَ أَرۡحَمُ ٱلرَّ ٰ⁠حِمِینَ *  وَلَمَّا فَتَحُوا۟ مَتَـٰعَهُمۡ وَجَدُوا۟ بِضَـٰعَتَهُمۡ رُدَّتۡ إِلَیۡهِمۡۖ قَالُوا۟ یَـٰۤأَبَانَا مَا نَبۡغِیۖ هَـٰذِهِۦ بِضَـٰعَتُنَا رُدَّتۡ إِلَیۡنَاۖ وَنَمِیرُ أَهۡلَنَا وَنَحۡفَظُ أَخَانَا وَنَزۡدَادُ كَیۡلَ بَعِیرࣲۖ ذَ ٰ⁠لِكَ كَیۡلࣱ یَسِیرࣱ

"Jab woh apne Waalid ke paas waapas gaye to unhone kaha: 'Abba Jaan! Ainda hame Ghalle se rok diya gaya hai, lehaza Aap (as) hamare saath hamare Bhai ko bhejen, taake ham Ghalla hasil karen aur uski hifazat ke zimmedar hain.' Yaqoob (as) ne kaha: 'Kya mein iske mutalliq tum par usi tarah se bharosa kar lun jaisa ke isse pehle uske Bhai ke mutalliq tum par etemad kiya tha? Allah hi Behtareen Muhafiz hai aur Wohi sab se Zyada Rehem Karnewala hai.'

"Aur jab unhone apna Samaan khola to dekha ke unka Maal bhi unhe wapas kar diya gaya hai, ye dekh kar woh pukar uthe: 'Abba Jaan! Aur hame kya chahiye, dekhiye ye hamari Raqam bhi hame wapas de di gayi hai. Bas ab ham jayenge aur apne Ahlo Ayaal ke liye Ghalla le aayenge, apne Bhai ki Hifazat bhi karenge. Aur ek Oont ke bojh ka Ghalla bhi zyada layenge. Itne Ghalle ka izaafa asaani ke saath ho jayega."

(Surah Yusuf: 63 - 65)

https://youtu.be/rpymJzfL6x4

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 📚📖 🙈

👉 Tafseer:

Imam Baqir (as): (Cont'd)

".....Algharz Bradran e Yusuf (as) Misr se Ghalla le kar ghar pahunche. Jab unhone apni Boriyon ko khola to ye dekh kar hairan reh gaye ke unki Raqam lautai ja chuki thi. Unhone apne Waalid se kaha: 'Abba Jaan! Hame aur kiya chahiye hamari Raqam hame lauta di gayi hai. Ab Badshahe Misr ne dobara Ghalla lene ke liye ham par ye shart aaed ki thi ke tumhe Ghalla tab hi milega jab tum apne Bhai ko le kar aaoge. Aap (as) meherbani karen, Ghalle ke dobara husool ke liye hamare Bhai ko hamare saath rawana karen. Bhai ki wajah se ham ek Oont ke bojh barabar zyada Ghalla hasil karenge aur hamare Bhai ki hifazat ki Aap koi fikr na karen. Ham apne Bhai ki hifazat karenge.'......"

(Tafseer Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)

(To be Cont'd......)

👑

Imam Baqir (as) se poochha gaya ke Hazrat Ali (as) ko Ameerul Mo'meneen (as) kyon kaha jata hai?

Aap (as) ne farmaya:

"Ye lafz وَنَمِیرُ أَهۡلَنَا se Mushtaq hai. Aap (as) ko Ameerul Mo'meneen kehne ki wajah ye hai ke Aap (as) Mo'meneen ko Rizq e Ilm faraham karte hain."

(Kitab Ilalush Sharaye, Ma'anil Akhbar)

👉🏻

Arabic Loghat (Dictionary) mein ُ بَاعَ يَبِيع ke wazan par ُ مَارَ يَمِير ka bhi ek Baab hai. مَارَ يَمِير ka meaning hai Ghalla faraham karna. Isi liye Braderane Yusuf (as) ne apne Waalid se kaha tha: وَنَمِیرُ أَهۡلَنَا ( "Aur ham apne Khandan ke liye Ghalla layenge.")

Mazkoora Riwayat mein lafz " أمير المؤمنين - Ameerul Mo'meneen" mein "Ameer" ko "Fe'l e Muzare -  فعل مضارع واحدمتكلم (Present & Future Tense, Singular, 1st Person) bataya gaya hai. Jiska مفعول به (Object form) أمير المؤمنين hai. Is surat mein" Ameerul Mo'meneen" ka Lafzi Tarjuma (Literal Translation) ye hoga ke: "Mein Ahle Imaan ko Rozi faraham karta hun." Mazkoora Riwayat mein Rizq e Ilm ka hawala diya gaya hai.

👉

Qare'een tawajja farmayen:

Aaj ki Riwayat ye sabit karti hai ke Hazrat Ali Ibne Talib (as) wahid hamare liye zariye Rizq hain. Chahe Rizq e Ghaza ya Rizq e Ilm ya........ etc. Isliye Ameerul Mo'meneen sirf or sirf Ali (as) ki sifat o Khushiyat hai. Ye Ghulu nahi hai kyonki aisa Imam (as) khud farma rahe hain.

اَللّٰهُمَّ الرزُقنِى تَوفّيقَ الطـَّاعَة و بُعد المَعصِيـَة

----------------------------------------------

🤲🏻

"Aye Aziz e Misr! Ham aur hamare Ahlo Ayaal Musibat mein giraftar ho chuke hain aur ham kuchh mamooli si poonji laye hain. Aap (as) hame bhar poor Ghalla enayat karen aur hame Khairat karen. Beshak Allah Khairat karne walon ko Jaza deta hai." (12:88)

     ♦ HAZRAT YUSUF (as) ♦

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1624)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

قَالَ لَنۡ أُرۡسِلَهُۥ مَعَكُمۡ حَتَّىٰ تُؤۡتُونِ مَوۡثِقࣰا مِّنَ ٱللَّهِ لَتَأۡتُنَّنِی بِهِۦۤ إِلَّاۤ أَن یُحَاطَ بِكُمۡۖ فَلَمَّاۤ ءَاتَوۡهُ مَوۡثِقَهُمۡ قَالَ ٱللَّهُ عَلَىٰ مَا نَقُولُ وَكِیلࣱ.

"Yaqoob (as) ne kaha: "Mein ise tumhare saath hargiz na bhejunga, jab tak tum mujhe Khuda ki taraf se Ahd o Paiman (promise) na do ke tum zaroor is mere paas laoge. Haan, agar tum gher liye jao to ye aur baat hai. Jab unhone Paiman de diya to kaha ke Allah hamare Qaul o Qarar ka Nigran aur Zamin hai."

(Surah Yusuf: 66)

https://youtu.be/rpymJzfL6x4

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 📚📖 🙈

👉 Tafseer:

Imam Baqir (as): (Cont'd)

".....Hazrat Yaqoob (as) ne farmaya: "Mujhe tum par etemad nahi hai. Pehle bhi tum log Yusuf (as) ko le kar gaye the, magar tumne Yusuf (as) ki hifazat nahi ki thi, ab mein tum par kis tarah bharosa kar sakta hun? Albatta agar tum mujhe Khuda ki Zamanat do to phir mein apne Bete ko tumhare saath rawana karunga, lekin iske liye tumhe Khuda ki Qasam khaana hogi ke tum use mere paas wapas laoge, haan agar gher liye jao to ye alehda baat hogi. Beton ne Baap ko Khuda ki Zamanat di aur yun Hazrat Yaqoob (as) ne apne Bete ko unke saath jaane ki ijazat de di.'......"

(Tafseer Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)

(To be Cont'd......)

🤲🏻

"Aye Aziz e Misr! Ham aur hamare Ahlo Ayaal Musibat mein giraftar ho chuke hain aur ham kuchh mamooli si poonji laye hain. Aap (as) hame bhar poor Ghalla enayat karen aur hame Khairat karen. Beshak Allah Khairat karne walon ko Jaza deta hai." (12:88)

      2nd Jamadi us Sani 1442

  16th January 2021, Saturday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

            ♦ NAZAR E BAD ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1625)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَقَالَ یَـٰبَنِیَّ لَا تَدۡخُلُوا۟ مِنۢ بَابࣲ وَ ٰ⁠حِدࣲ وَٱدۡخُلُوا۟ مِنۡ أَبۡوَ ٰ⁠بࣲ مُّتَفَرِّقَةࣲۖ وَمَاۤ أُغۡنِی عَنكُم مِّنَ ٱللَّهِ مِن شَیۡءٍۖ إِنِ ٱلۡحُكۡمُ إِلَّا لِلَّهِۖ عَلَیۡهِ تَوَكَّلۡتُۖ وَعَلَیۡهِ فَلۡیَتَوَكَّلِ ٱلۡمُتَوَكِّلُونَ.

"Aur Yaqoob (as) ne kaha: 'Aye mere Farzando! Tum ek Darwaze se dakhil na hona iske bajaye mukhtalif Darwazon se Shaher mein dakhil hona. Mein tumhe Khuda ki Mashiyyat se bacha to nahi sakta, Hukm to bas Usi ka hi chalta hai. Meine Usi par Bharosa kiya hai aur Bharosa karnewalon ko Usi par hi Bharosa karna chahiye."

(Surah Yusuf: 67)

https://youtu.be/rpymJzfL6x4

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Mufasserin ka is Ayat ke bare mein bayan hai ke Hazrat Yaqoob (as) ne apne Beton ko Nazar e Bad se mehfooz rakhne ke liye ye tadbeer ki thi.

👁️

Majmaul Bayan mein hai ke 'Jubai' Nazar e Bad ki taseer ka inkaar karte the. Jabke Muhaqqeqin iske qael hain aur iske saboot mein Rasoole Khuda (saww) ki ye hadis pesh karte hain:

اِنَّ العَينَ حَقٌّ وَ العَينُ تَنْتَزِلُ الْحَالِق.

 "Nigahe Bad Haq (Moassir) hai aur Nigahe Bad mein itni taseer hai ke wo Buland Pahad ko bhi gira sakti hai."

👀

Hazrat Ali (as):

AanHazrat (saww) Imam Hasan (as) aur Imam Husain (as) ko Nazar e Bad se bachane ke liye ye Dua padhte the:

اُعِيذُكُمَا بِكَلِمَاتِ اللُّٰهِ التَّامَّةِ مِن كُلِّ شَيْطَانٍ وَ هَامَّةٍ وَ مِنْ كُلِّ عَيْنٍ لَامَّةٍ وَ مِنْ شَرِّ حَاسِدٍ اِذَا حَسَد.

Aap (saww) farmaya Hazrat Ibrahim (as) ne bhi apne Beton ko Nazar e Bad se bachane ke liye un par yehi Azeemat (Dua) dam ki thi.

(Usoole Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)

👀

Riwayat mein mazkoor hai ke Hazrat Musa (as) ne bhi Farzandan e Haroon (as) ko Nazar e Bad se bachane ke liye Dua e Azimat padhi thi.

Hazrat Jafar e Tayyar (as) ke Bete bhi bade haseen o Jameel the. Unki waleda Asma binte Umais ne AanHazrat (saww) se Dua e Azimat padhwai.

🦚

Rasoole Khuda (saww):

"Jab koi cheez logon ke Seeno mein badi mehsoos hoti hai to Allah uski Qadr ko gira deta hai aur use chhota kar deta hai."

🤲🏻

Riwayat mein hai ke Hazrat Jibrael (as) aaye aur Rasoole Khuda (saww) ko Nazar e Bad se bachane ke liye ye Dua taleem di:

بِسْمِ اللّٰهِ اَرقِيكَ مِنْ كُلِّ عَيْنِ حَاسِدٍ اللّٰهُ يَشْفِيْكَ.

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

     ♦ HAZRAT YUSUF (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1626)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

 وَلَمَّا دَخَلُوا۟ مِنۡ حَیۡثُ أَمَرَهُمۡ أَبُوهُم مَّا كَانَ یُغۡنِی عَنۡهُم مِّنَ ٱللَّهِ مِن شَیۡءٍ إِلَّا حَاجَةࣰ فِی نَفۡسِ یَعۡقُوبَ قَضَىٰهَاۚ وَإِنَّهُۥ لَذُو عِلۡمࣲ لِّمَا عَلَّمۡنَـٰهُ وَلَـٰكِنَّ أَكۡثَرَ ٱلنَّاسِ لَا یَعۡلَمُونَ.

"Aur aisa hi hua ke jab woh Baap ki hidayat ke mutabiq Shaher mein dakhil hue to uski ye ehtiyati tadbeer Khuda ki Mashiyyat ke muqabile mein kuchh kaam na aa saki, haan bas Yaqoob (as) ke Dil mein jo ek khatak thi use door karne ke liye usne apni se koshish kar li. Beshak woh hamari di hui Taleem se Sahibe Ilm tha magar aksar log maamle ki haqiqat ko jaante nahi."

(Surah Yusuf: 68)

https://youtu.be/rpymJzfL6x4

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 📚📖 🙈

👉 Tafseer:

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Jab Farzandan e Yaqoob (as) Bin Yameen ko apne saath le kar Darbar e Yusuf (as) mein gaye to Aap (as) ne unki Ziyafat (Mehman Nawazi) ka intezam kiya aur jab Dastarkhwan bichh gaya to Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne farmaya ke ek hi Maa ke Bete ikatthe ho kar baith jayen. Us hukm ke baad 10 Bhai baith gaye, lekin Bin Yameen akela khada raha.

Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne farmaya: 'Tum kyon akele khade ho?' Bin Yameen ne kaha: 'Aap (as) ne hi to kaha tha ke Maa Jae Bhai saath baith jayen. In mein mera koi Maajaya Bhai nahi hai.'

Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne kaha:

'To kya tera koi Saga Bhai nahi tha?'

Bin Yameen ne kaha: 'Kyon nahi, mera Saga Bhai tha.' Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne kaha: 'To tumhare Bhai ko kya hua?' Bin Yameen ne kaha: 'Ye guman karte hain ke use Bhediya kha gaya tha.' Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne kaha: 'Tumhe tumhare Bhai ke kho jaane ka kitna sadma hua tha?' Bin Tameen ne kaha: 'Khuda ne mujhe 11 Auladen ata ki hai meine sabke naam uske naam se mushtaq karke rakhe hain.'

Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne kaha:

'Ajeeb baat hai, itne pyare Bhai ki judai ke baad bhi tu Biwiyon se ham aghosh hota raha aur Bachche paida karta raha.'

Bin Yameen ne kaha: 'Asl baat ye hai ke mera ek Nek Seerat Waalid hai, usne mujh se kaha ke Beta Shaadi karna ke Khuda tujhe itni Aulad paida kare jo poori Zameen ko Khuda ki Tasbeeh se bhar den.'

Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne farmaya: 'Phir aao tum mere saath mil kar Dastarkhwan par baitho aur mere saath khaana khao.'

Bradaran e Yusuf (as) ne jab Bin Yameen ki is Izzat Afzai ko dekha to kehne kage:

"Allah ne Yusuf (as) aur uske Bhai ko Fazilat di hai aur naubat yahan tak ja pahunchi hai ke aaj Yusuf (as) ka Bhai Badshah ke saath mil kar khaana kha raha hai."

(Tafseer Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)

👉🏻

Yehi riwayat mein is Kitab is tarah izafa hai:

Jab Farzandan e Yaqoob (as) ghar se nikle to Bin Yameen un se alag alag rehte. Phir Hazrat Yusuf (as) is tarah baten hui:

..... Aap (as) ne poochha kya tumne Shaadi ki? Bin Yameen ne kaha: Haan, 3 Bete hain unke Naam hain: Bhediye, Qameez, Khoon. Ye Naam isliye intekhab kiye taake mera Bhai hamesha yaad rahe.

(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi, Noorus Saqlain)

(To be Cont'd......)

----------------------------------------------

🤲🏻

"Aye Aziz e Misr! Ham aur hamare Ahlo Ayaal Musibat mein giraftar ho chuke hain aur ham kuchh mamooli si poonji laye hain. Aap (as) hame bhar poor Ghalla enayat karen aur hame Khairat karen. Beshak Allah Khairat karne walon ko Jaza deta hai." (12:88)

وَلَمَّا دَخَلُوا۟ عَلَىٰ یُوسُفَ ءَاوَىٰۤ إِلَیۡهِ أَخَاهُۖ قَالَ إِنِّیۤ أَنَا۠ أَخُوكَ فَلَا تَبۡتَىِٕسۡ بِمَا كَانُوا۟ یَعۡمَلُونَ

"Ye log Yusuf (as) ke huzoor mein pahunche to usne apne Bhai ko apne paas alag bula liya aur use bata diya ke "mein tera wohi Bhai hun (jo khoya gaya tha), ab tu un baton ka gham na kar jo ye log karte rahe hain."

(Surah Yusuf: 69)

https://youtu.be/rpymJzfL6x4

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Imam Baqir (as): (Cont'd)

"Beher haal 6 Mahine ke baad Pisarane Yaqoob (as) ka Qafila ghar se chala. Is baar is Qafile mein Ibne Yameel (Binyamin) bhi shamil tha. Qafila safar karta hua Yusuf (as) ke paas pahuncha. Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne Bhaiyyon se kaha: 'Ibne Yameel bhi tumhare saath aaya hai?' Bhaiyyon ne kaha: 'Ji haan, ham use saath laaye hain aur woh ye hai.' Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne use uthaya aur apne saath tanhai mein le gaye aur usse farmaya ke mujhe pehchano, mein tumhara khoya hua Bhai Yusuf hun, ab mein jo kuchh karun tumhe us par ghamgeen hone ki koi zaroorat nahi hai aur filhal Bhaiyyon ko bhi mere mutalliq kuchh na batana...."

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

     ♦ HAZRAT YUSUF (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1628)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

فَلَمَّا جَهَّزَهُم بِجَهَازِهِمۡ جَعَلَ ٱلسِّقَایَةَ فِی رَحۡلِ أَخِیهِ ثُمَّ أَذَّنَ مُؤَذِّنٌ أَیَّتُهَا ٱلۡعِیرُ إِنَّكُمۡ لَسَـٰرِقُونَ *  قَالُوا۟ وَأَقۡبَلُوا۟ عَلَیۡهِم مَّاذَا تَفۡقِدُونَ *  قَالُوا۟ نَفۡقِدُ صُوَاعَ ٱلۡمَلِكِ وَلِمَن جَاۤءَ بِهِۦ حِمۡلُ بَعِیرࣲ وَأَنَا۠ بِهِۦ زَعِیمࣱ.

"Jab Yusuf (as) un Bhaiyyon ka Samaan ladwane lage to usne apne Bhaiyyon ke samaan mein apna Pyala rakh diya phir ek Munadi ne pukar kar kaha: 'Aye Qafile walo, tum log Chor ho." Unhone palat kar poochha: 'Tumhari kya cheez khoyi gayi?' Sarkari Mulizemon ne kaha:" Badshah ka peene ka Pyala hamko nahi mil raha.' (Aur unke Jamadar ne kaha:) "Jo shakhs la kar dega uske liye ek Oont barabar Ghalla Inaam milega, iska mein zimma leta hun."

(Surah Yusuf: 70 - 72)

https://youtu.be/rpymJzfL6x4

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Imam Baqir (as): (Cont'd)

"....Iske Baad Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne apne Naukaron ko hukm diya ke woh unki Boriyon mein Ghalla bharen aur jab Ghalla bhar lo to khamoshi se Binyamin ki Bori mein mere Peene ka Pyala rakh dena aur Bori ko band kar dena. Naukaron ne Aapke farman par amal kiya. Ghalla lene ke baad Farzandane Yaqoob (as) Qafile ke saath rawana hue. Abhi woh thodi hi door gaye the ke Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne apne Ghulamon ko saath le kar unke taqqub (follow) mein rawana hue aur ek Munadi ne Ahle Qafile ko sada di aur kaha: "Qafile walo! Tum to Chor ho."

Ye awaaz sun kar Qafila ruk gaya aur unhone ne kaha: "Tumhari kya cheez Chori hui hai? Naukaron ne kaha: "Hamare Badshah ka Pyala kho gaya hai aur jo use baramad karega use Inaam mein Baare Shutar (Oont barabar) Ghalla diya jayega....."

(Tafseer Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)

(To be Cont'd......)

"Aye Aziz e Misr! Ham aur hamare Ahlo Ayaal Musibat mein giraftar ho chuke hain aur ham kuchh mamooli si poonji laye hain. Aap (as) hame bhar poor Ghalla enayat karen aur hame Khairat karen. Beshak Allah Khairat karne walon ko Jaza deta hai." (12:88)

           ♦ TAQAYYAH ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1629)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

فَلَمَّا جَهَّزَهُم بِجَهَازِهِمۡ جَعَلَ ٱلسِّقَایَةَ فِی رَحۡلِ أَخِیهِ ثُمَّ أَذَّنَ مُؤَذِّنٌ أَیَّتُهَا ٱلۡعِیرُ إِنَّكُمۡ لَسَـٰرِقُونَ

"Jab Yusuf (as) un Bhaiyyon ka Samaan ladwane lage to usne apne Bhaiyyon ke samaan mein apna Pyala rakh diya phir ek Munadi ne pukar kar kaha: 'Aye Qafile walo, tum log Chor ho."

(Surah Yusuf: 70)

https://youtu.be/rpymJzfL6x4

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Taqiyya Deen e Khuda Wandi mein shamil hai."

Raavi ne sawal kiya: "Kiya??"

Imam (as) ne iski wazahat ki:

"Ji haan, Khuda ki Qasam! Taqayya Deen mein shamil hai. Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne Bhaiyyon se kaha tha: "Qafile walo! Tum Chor ho jabke unhone koi cheez Chori nahi ki thi"

"Hazrat Ibrahim (as) ne kaha tha: "Mein Bimaar hun." Khuda ki Qasam, Ibrahim (as) Bimaar nahi the."

Means ye sab Taqayya tha.

(Usoole Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)

🤔

Raavi ne Imam Sadiq (as) se sawal kiya ke Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne Bhaiyyon ko Chor kaha jabke woh Chor nahi the. Hazrat Ibrahim (as) ne Buton ko toda aur kaha ke sab se bade But ne chhote Buton ko toda.

Aap (as) ne wazahat ki:

"Allah ko do cheezen Pasand hain aur do cheezen Na-Pasand hain. Allah ko Jihad ki Safon ke darmiyan Kuffar ke saamne akad akad kar chalna Pasand hai aur Islaah ki alawa Jhoot bolna Khuda ko Na-Pasand hai. Hazrat Ibrahim (as) ka jumla Islaah ki gharz se tha aur unhe maloom tha ke ye log Goonge Khud-Sakhta Khudaon se kuchh nahi poochh sakte aur na hi unke But unko jawab dene ke layeq hain. Isi tarah se Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne bhi Islaah ki gharz se kaha tha: "Tum Chor ho."

Isi mafhoom ki Rasoole Khuda (saww) se bhi riwayat hai.

(Usoole Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)

🗣️

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Kalaam ki 3 qismen hain: (1) Ya tobSach hota hai, (2) ya Jhoot, (3) ya logon mein Islaah ka zariya hota hai."

(Noorus Saqlain)

🗣️

Imam Baqir (as) se bataya gaya ke kuchh log Aap (as) ke mutalliq ye kehte hain ke Aap (as) ki guftugu 70 70 mafahim ki haamil hoti hai.

Aap (as) ne farmaya:

"Woh mujh se kya chahta hai, kya mein Malaika ko uske saamne le aaon jabke ye kaam to Anbiya ne bhi nahi kiya tha. Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne bhi Qafile walon ko Chor kaha tha, jabke woh hargiz Chor nahi the aur Yusuf (as) ne bhi Jhoot nahi bola tha."

(Rauza e Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)

----------------------------------------------

🤲🏻

"Aye Aziz e Misr! Ham aur hamare Ahlo Ayaal Musibat mein giraftar ho chuke hain aur ham kuchh mamooli si poonji laye hain. Aap (as) hame bhar poor Ghalla enayat karen aur hame Khairat karen. Beshak Allah Khairat karne walon ko Jaza deta hai." (12:88)

     ♦ HAZRAT YUSUF (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1630)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

قَالُوا۟ تَٱللَّهِ لَقَدۡ عَلِمۡتُم مَّا جِئۡنَا لِنُفۡسِدَ فِی ٱلۡأَرۡضِ وَمَا كُنَّا سَـٰرِقِینَ *  قَالُوا۟ فَمَا جَزَ ٰ⁠ۤؤُهُۥۤ إِن كُنتُمۡ كَـٰذِبِینَ *  قَالُوا۟ جَزَ ٰ⁠ۤؤُهُۥ مَن وُجِدَ فِی رَحۡلِهِۦ فَهُوَ جَزَ ٰ⁠ۤؤُهُۥۚ كَذَ ٰ⁠لِكَ نَجۡزِی ٱلظَّـٰلِمِینَ *  فَبَدَأَ بِأَوۡعِیَتِهِمۡ قَبۡلَ وِعَاۤءِ أَخِیهِ ثُمَّ ٱسۡتَخۡرَجَهَا مِن وِعَاۤءِ أَخِیهِۚ كَذَ ٰ⁠لِكَ كِدۡنَا لِیُوسُفَۖ مَا كَانَ لِیَأۡخُذَ أَخَاهُ فِی دِینِ ٱلۡمَلِكِ إِلَّاۤ أَن یَشَاۤءَ ٱللَّهُۚ نَرۡفَعُ دَرَجَـٰتࣲ مَّن نَّشَاۤءُۗ وَفَوۡقَ كُلِّ ذِی عِلۡمٍ عَلِیمࣱ.

"Un Bhaiyyon ne kaha: "Khuda ki Qasam! Tum log khub jaante ho ke ham is Mulk mein Fasaad karne nahi aayen hain aur ham Chor nahi hain." Shahi Mulazemin ne kaha: "Achha, agar tumhari baat jhooti nikli to Chor ki Saza kya hogi?" Unhone kaha: "Uski Saza? Jiske Samaan mein se cheez nikle woh aap hi apni saza mein rakh liya jaye. Hamare haan to aise Zalimon ko Saza dene ka yahi tariqa hai."

"Tab Yusuf (as) ne apne Bhaiyyon ke Samaan se pehle unke Samaan ki talashi li, phir apne Bhai ke Samaan se Gumshuda Pyala baramad kar liya. Is tarah Hamne Yusuf (as) ke liye ye Tadbeer ki thi warna Badshah ke Qanoon ke tahet apne Bhai ko pakadne ka majaaz nahi tha. Siwai iske ke Allah aisa chaahe. Ham jise Chahte hain uske darajat buland kar dete hain aur ek Ilm Rakhnewala aisa hai jo har Sahibe Ilm se Bartar hai."

(Surah Yusuf: 73 - 76)

https://youtu.be/rpymJzfL6x4

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Imam Baqir (as): (Cont'd)

".....Ye awaaz sun kar Qafila ruk gaya aur unhone kaha: 'Tumhari kya cheez chori hui hai? Naukaron ne kaha: 'Hamare Badshah ka Pyala kho gaya hai aur jo use baramad karega use Inaam mein Bare Shutar (Oont barabar wazan) Ghalla diya jayega.'

Farzandan e Yaqoob (as) ne kaha: 'Tum log jaante ho ke ham yahan Fasaad karne ke liye nahi aaye aur ham log Chor nahi hain.'

Hazrat (as) ke Naukaron ne kaha: 'Achha, agar tum Jhoote sabit hue to batao Chor ki kya Saza hogi?'

Unhone ne kaha: 'Jiske paas tumhara Samaan baramad ho, tum use apne paas thehra len. Ham isi tarah se Choron ko Saza diya karte hain.'

Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne sab se pehle Sautele Bhaiyyon ki Boriyon ki talashi li. Un mein se kuchh baramad na hua. Phir jab Aap (as) ne apne Sage Bhai ki talashi li to us mein se wo Pyala baramad ho gaya......"

(Tafseer Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)

(To be Cont'd......)

----------------------------------------------

🤲🏻

"Aye Aziz e Misr! Ham aur hamare Ahlo Ayaal Musibat mein giraftar ho chuke hain aur ham kuchh mamooli si poonji laye hain. Aap (as) hame bhar poor Ghalla enayat karen aur hame Khairat karen. Beshak Allah Khairat karne walon ko Jaza deta hai." (12:88)

     ♦ HAZRAT YUSUF (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1631)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

قَالُوۤا۟ إِن یَسۡرِقۡ فَقَدۡ سَرَقَ أَخࣱ لَّهُۥ مِن قَبۡلُۚ فَأَسَرَّهَا یُوسُفُ فِی نَفۡسِهِۦ وَلَمۡ یُبۡدِهَا لَهُمۡۚ قَالَ أَنتُمۡ شَرࣱّ مَّكَانࣰاۖ وَٱللَّهُ أَعۡلَمُ بِمَا تَصِفُونَ.

"Un Bhaiyyon ne kaha: "Ye Chori kare to kuchh tajjub ki baat bhi nahi, isse pehle iska Bhai (Yusuf) bhi Chori kar chuka hai. Yusuf (as) unki ye baat sun kar pi gaya, Haqeeqat un par na kholi, bas (zere lab) itna keh kar reh gaya ke: "Bade hi bure ho tum log, (mere munh dar munh mujh par) jo Ilzaam tum laga rahe ho uski Haqeeqat Khuda khoob jaanta hai."

(Surah Yusuf: 77)

https://youtu.be/rpymJzfL6x4

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Hazrat Imam Hasan Askari (as):

"Hazrat Yaqoob (as) ke paas Hazrat Ibrahim (as) ka ek Kamarband maujood tha aur jo bhi use Chori karta tha woh Ghulam bana liya jata tha. Hazrat Yusuf (as) apne Baap ko bahut pyaare the aur Aap (as) ki Phoophi bhi Aap (as) se behad pyaar karti thi. Ek martaba Phoophi Aapko apne haan le gayi. Hazrat Yaqoob (as) ne unhe paigham bheja ke mein Yusuf (as) ke liye udaas hun use mere paas bhej do. Bibi ne Yusuf (as) ki tayyari karayi aur khamoshi se woh Kamarband uski Kamar se bandha aur unhe Waalid ke paas le gayin aur phir Bibi ne apne Bhai Hazrat Yaqoob (as) se kaha ke Ibrahimi Kamarband kahin kho gaya hai. Jibrael (as) nazil hue aur unhone kaha ke Kamarband Yusuf (as) ne pehna hua hai."

"Bibi ne az rahe pyaar Bhai se kaha ke: 'Aapne dekha Yusuf (as) ne meri Chori ki hai aur Ibrahimi Qanoon ke tahet Aap (as) use mere sipurd kar den. Beherhaal wo ek Masoomana harkat thi aur woh pyaar ka ek andaaz tha, lekin jab Binyamin ki Bori se Yusuf (as) ke Paani ka Pyala baramad hua to Braderane Yusuf (as) ne kaha: 'Agar usne aaj Chori ki hai to us mein tajjub ki koi baat nahi hai. Uske Bhai (Yusuf) ne bhi isse pehle Chori ki thi."

Imam (as) ne phir farmaya:

"Yusuf (as) aur Yaqoob (as) ke darmiyan kuchh faasla hael nahi tha. Agar Khuda Hijaab utha kar Yaqoob (as) ko Yusuf (as) dikhana chahta to woh Dikhaane par  Qadir tha, lekin Allah ne har baat ke kiye waqt muqarrar kiya hai aur har kaam apne muqarrar waqt par hi zahoor pazeer hota hai."

(Kitab Al Kharaij wal Jaraeh, Tafseer Ayyashi, Uyoonul Akhbar, Noorus Saqlain)

(To be Cont'd......)

----------------------------------------------

🤲🏻

"Aye Aziz e Misr! Ham aur hamare Ahlo Ayaal Musibat mein giraftar ho chuke hain aur ham kuchh mamooli si poonji laye hain. Aap (as) hame bhar poor Ghalla enayat karen aur hame Khairat karen. Beshak Allah Khairat karne walon ko Jaza deta hai." (12:88)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

     ♦ HAZRAT YUSUF (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1632)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

قَالُوا۟ یَـٰۤأَیُّهَا ٱلۡعَزِیزُ إِنَّ لَهُۥۤ أَبࣰا شَیۡخࣰا كَبِیرࣰا فَخُذۡ أَحَدَنَا مَكَانَهُۥۤۖ إِنَّا نَرَىٰكَ مِنَ ٱلۡمُحۡسِنِینَ * قَالَ مَعَاذَ ٱللَّهِ أَن نَّأۡخُذَ إِلَّا مَن وَجَدۡنَا مَتَـٰعَنَا عِندَهُۥۤ إِنَّاۤ إِذࣰا لَّظَـٰلِمُونَ. * فَلَمَّا ٱسۡتَیۡـَٔسُوا۟ مِنۡهُ خَلَصُوا۟ نَجِیࣰّاۖ قَالَ كَبِیرُهُمۡ أَلَمۡ تَعۡلَمُوۤا۟ أَنَّ أَبَاكُمۡ قَدۡ أَخَذَ عَلَیۡكُم مَّوۡثِقࣰا مِّنَ ٱللَّهِ وَمِن قَبۡلُ مَا فَرَّطتُمۡ فِی یُوسُفَۖ فَلَنۡ أَبۡرَحَ ٱلۡأَرۡضَ حَتَّىٰ یَأۡذَنَ لِیۤ أَبِیۤ أَوۡ یَحۡكُمَ ٱللَّهُ لِیۖ وَهُوَ خَیۡرُ ٱلۡحَـٰكِمِینَ.

"Unhone kaha: 'Aye Azize Misr! Iske Waalid intihai Zaeeful Umr hain, Aap iske bajai ham mein se kisi ek ko pakad len ham Aapko Nekokaron mein se samajhte hain. Yusuf (as) ne kaha: Khuda ki panah! Jiske paas hamne apna Samaan paya hai use chhod kar kisi aur ko pakad len, agar hamne aisa kiya to phir ham Zalim qarar payenge."_

"Jab woh Yusuf (as) se mayus ho gaye to ek goshe mein ja kar aapas mein mashwara karne lage. Un mein jo sab se bada tha woh bola: 'Tum jaante nahi ho ke tumhare Waalid tum se Khuda ke Naam par kya Ahd o Paiman le chuke hain aur isse pehle Yusuf (as) ke maamle mein jo zyadtiyan tum kar chuke ho wo bhi tum ko maloom hai, ab mein to yahan se hargiz na jaonga jab tak ke mere Waalid mujhe ijazat na den, ya phir Allah hi mere haq mein koi Faisla farma de ke Woh sab se Behtar Faisla Karnewala hai."

(Surah Yusuf: 78 - 80)

https://youtu.be/rpymJzfL6x4

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 📚📖

Jab Binyamin ke Samaan se Pyala baramad hua aur Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne uske mutalliq hukm sadir kiya ke use yahan rok liya jaye to Aulad e Yaqoob (as) ko sakht Gussa aaya aur jab unhe gussa aata tha to Kapde ke neeche unke Baal khade ho jate the aur unke Saron se Zard (Yellow) rang ka Khoon nikalta tha aur is mauqe par bhi unhe bada gussa aaya aur unhone aisa kaha (Ayat ke jumle).

Qabil tawajjo baat ye hai ke Yusuf (as) ne unse ye alfaaz nahi kahe the ke ham to bas ise hi pakdenge jisne hamara Saman chori kiya hai. Phir jab Farzandan e Yaqoob (as) Binyamin ki wapsi se mayus ho gaye to woh door ja kar baith gaye aur aapas mein mashwara karne lage. Unke bade Bhai ne kaha: 'Mein ab is Sar Zameen par hi rahunga, yaha tak ke mere Waalid mujhe yahan se wapas na bulayen ya Khuda mere liye koi Faisla na kar de. Waalid e Mohtaram ne ham se waada liya tha ke ham Binyamin ko apne saath wapas le kar aayenge aur isse pehle Yusuf (as) ke mutalliq bhi hamse kotahi hui thi. Lehaza mein kaunsa Munh le kar Waalid e Mohtaram ke paas jaunga. Bade bhai ke mutalliq Kitabon nein ikhtilaf hai, ek qaul hai ke iske naam Laavi tha ya Yahooda tha.

(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi, Noorus Saqlain)

📖

Is tarah ki Riwayat Imam Sadiq (as) se bhi hai.

Jab Braderane Yusuf (as) ki darkhwast mustard ho gayi yo Yahuda ko gussa aaya, tab Yusuf (as) ka nanha Beta Sone ki Ball se khel raha tha. Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne uska Ball Yahooda ki taraf pheka, bachcha Ball lene dauda aur uska haath Yahuda se touch hua to uska gussa thanda ho gaya. Dobara gussa aaya to Aap (as) phir waisa hi kiya.

(Tafseer Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)

Algharz Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne ek haseen bahane se apne Bhai ko apne haan rok liya. Aap (as) ke baqi das Bhaiyyon mein se 9 Bhai wapas Hazrat Yaqoob (as) ke paas gaye.

(To be Cont'd......)

----------------------------------------------

🤲🏻

"Aye Aziz e Misr! Ham aur hamare Ahlo Ayaal Musibat mein giraftar ho chuke hain aur ham kuchh mamooli si poonji laye hain. Aap (as) hame bhar poor Ghalla enayat karen aur hame Khairat karen. Beshak Allah Khairat karne walon ko Jaza deta hai." (12:88)

     ♦ HAZRAT YUSUF (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1633)

*ٱرۡجِعُوۤا۟ إِلَىٰۤ أَبِیكُمۡ فَقُولُوا۟ یَـٰۤأَبَانَاۤ إِنَّ ٱبۡنَكَ سَرَقَ وَمَا شَهِدۡنَاۤ إِلا بِمَا عَلِمۡنَا وَمَا كُنَّا لِلۡغَیۡبِ حَـٰفِظِینَ * وَسۡـَٔلِ ٱلۡقَرۡیَةَ ٱلَّتِی كُنَّا فِیهَا وَٱلۡعِیرَ ٱلَّتِیۤ أَقۡبَلۡنَا فِیهَاۖ وَإِنَّا لَصَـٰدِقُونَ * قَالَ بَلۡ سَوَّلَتۡ لَكُمۡ أَنفُسُكُمۡ أَمۡرࣰاۖ فَصَبۡرࣱ جَمِیلٌۖ عَسَى ٱللَّهُ أَن یَأۡتِیَنِی بِهِمۡ جَمِیعًاۚ إِنَّهُۥ هُوَ ٱلۡعَلِیمُ ٱلۡحَكِیمُ.*

"Tum ja kar apne Waalid se kaho ke "Abba Jaan, Aapke Sahebzade ne Chori ki hai. Hamne use Chori karte hue nahi dekha, jo kuchh hame maloom hua bas wohi bayan kar rahe hain, aur Ghaib ki Nigehbani to ham na kar sakte the. Aap is Basti ke logon se poochh lijiye, jahan ham the us Qafile se daryaft kar lijiye jiske saath ham aayen hain, ham apne bayan mein Sachche hain. Baap ne ye Dastaan sun kar kaha: "Darasl tumhare Nafs ne tumhare liye ek aur badi baat ko asaan bana diya. Achha is par bhi Sabr karunga aur bakhoobi karunga, kya baeed hai ke Allah un sab ko mujh se la milaye. Woh sab kuchh Jaanta hai, aur Uske sab kaam Hikmat par mabni hain."

(Surah Yusuf: 81 - 83)

https://youtu.be/rpymJzfL6x4

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Imam Sadiq (as):

Jab Farzandan e Yaqoob (as) ghar pahunche to unse pehla Sawal yehi hua ke tum mere Bete Binyamin ko le kar gaye the, batao woh kaha hai? Unhone kaha: 'Abba Jaan! Binyamin ne Chori ki thi. Use Shahe Misr ne apne haan rok liya hai aur hame wapasi ki ijazat di hai. Ham Aapke paas aa gaye hain. Agar Aap (as) ne mazeed tasalli karni ho to phir us Shaher walon se poochhen jahan ye waqea pesh aaya tha aur Aap(as) us Qafile se bhi tasalli kar sakte hain jinke saath hamne safar kiya tha, to Aap (as) ko hamari sachchai ka yaqeen ho jayega. Hazrat Yaqoob (as) ne farmaya: "Tumne apni taraf se ye baat bana li hai, ab mein 'Sabr e Jameel' hi kar sakta hun."

(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi, Noorus Saqlain)

👉🏻

Sheikhut Taifa likhte hain: 'Sabr e Jameel us Sabr ko kaha jata hai jis mein Khaliq ka Shikwa na ho.'

😔

Imam Baqir (as):

" *Sabr e Jameel'* aise Sabr ko kehte hain jis mein apni Takleef ka logon ke saamne shikwa na kiya jaye."

(Tafseer Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)

(To be Cont'd......) ----------------------------------------------

"Aye Aziz e Misr! Ham aur hamare Ahlo Ayaal Musibat mein giraftar ho chuke hain aur ham kuchh mamooli si poonji laye hain. Aap (as) hame bhar poor Ghalla enayat karen aur hame Khairat karen. Beshak Allah Khairat karne walon ko Jaza deta hai." (12:88)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

       ♦ GIRYA O ZARI ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1634)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَتَوَلَّىٰ عَنۡهُمۡ وَقَالَ یَـٰۤأَسَفَىٰ عَلَىٰ یُوسُفَ وَٱبۡیَضَّتۡ عَیۡنَاهُ مِنَ ٱلۡحُزۡنِ فَهُوَ كَظِیمࣱ *  قَالُوا۟ تَٱللَّهِ تَفۡتَؤُا۟ تَذۡكُرُ یُوسُفَ حَتَّىٰ تَكُونَ حَرَضًا أَوۡ تَكُونَ مِنَ ٱلۡهَـٰلِكِینَ *  قَالَ إِنَّمَاۤ أَشۡكُوا۟ بَثِّی وَحُزۡنِیۤ إِلَى ٱللَّهِ وَأَعۡلَمُ مِنَ ٱللَّهِ مَا لَا تَعۡلَمُونَ.

"Phir (Yaqoob (as)) ne unse Munh pher liya aur kaha: 'Haye Yusuf! Aur Ranj o Gham ki wajah se Unki Aankhe Safed ho gayin aur woh Gham ke ghoont peete rahe."

"Beton ne kaha:' Khudara! Aap to bas Yusuf ko hi yaad kiye jaate hain. Nobat ye aa gayi hai ke uske Gham mein apne Aapko ghula denge ya apni Jaan halaak kar dalenge."

"Aap (as) ne kaha: 'Mein apni pareshani aur apne Gham ki Faryaad Allah ke siwa kisi se nahi karta, aur Allah se jaisa mein waqif hun tum nahi ho."

(Surah Yusuf: 84 - 86)

https://youtu.be/rpymJzfL6x4

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Imam Sadiq (as) se poochha gaya ke Hazrat Yaqoob (as) ko Yusuf (as) ki judai ka Gham kitna tha?

Aap (as) ne farmaya:

"Agar 70 Pisar apni murda Maon ka Gham karen..."

(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim, Noorus Saqlain)

😢😪😩😭

Imam Baqir (as):

"Mere Waalid Imam Sajjad (as) Waqea e Karbala ke baad poore 20 Baras tak rote rahe aur Aap (as) ki haalat ye thi ke jab bhi Aap (as) ke saamne khaana rakha jata to Aap (as) Waqeat e Karbala ko yaad kar ke rone lag jate the."

"Ek dafa Aap (as) ke ek Ghulam ne Aap (as) se kaha: 'Kya abhi Aap (as) ka Gham poora nahi hua? Aap (as) ne farmaya: 'Tujh par afsos! Hazrat Yaqoob (as) ke 12 Farzand the. 12 mein se ek Farzand juda hua tha to rote rote unki Ankhen Safed ho gayi thi aur unki Kamar jhuk gayi thi, jabke unka Farzand bhi Zinda. Meine to Karbala mein apne Waalid, Bhai aur Chacha aur Khandan ke 17 afraad ko Qatl hote hue dekha hai. Ab tum khud hi batao mera Gham kaise khatm ho sakta hai?"

(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi, Noorus Saqlain)

😢😪😩😭

Hazrat Imam Sadiq (as):

"Duniya mein sab se zyada 5 afraad roye:"

1. Hazrat Adam (as) (2) Hazrat Yaqoob (as) (3) Hazrat Yusuf (as) (4) Hazrat Fatema Zehra (sa) (5) Hazrat Imam Zainul Abedin (as)

Hazrat Adam (as) firaaq e Jannat mein itna roye ke Aapke Rukhsaron par Nehren se ban gayi thin. Yaqoob (as) firaaq e Yusuf (as) mein itna roye ke unki Nigah khatm ho gayi thi aur unke Bete unse kaha karte the ke Khudara ab bas bhi karen. Musalsal Gham ki wajah se Aap (as) Bimaar ho jayenge ya Aap (as) halaak ho jayenge."

"Hazrat Yusuf (as) apne Waalid ki judai mein itna roye ke Ahle Zindaan tang aa gaye the aur unhone kaha: 'Agar Aap (as) Din ko royen to ham Raat ko araam karen aur agar Aap (as) Raat ko royen to ham Din ko araam karen."

"Hazrat Fatema Zehra (sa) apne Waalid Majid Rasoole Khuda (saww) ke Gham mein itna royin ke Ahle Medina tang aa gaye. Hazrat Ali (as) ne unke rone ke liye Medina se bahar ek "Baitul Huzn" tameer kiya, jahan Aap (as) apne Shahzadon ko le ja kar Waalid e Maajid ke Gham mein roti thi."

"Hazrat Imam Zainul Abedin (as) Waqea e Karbala ke baad musalsal 20 Baras tak rote rahe. Aap (as) jab bhi Paani ko dekhte to Karbala walon ki Pyaas ko yaad kar ke rote the aur jab bhi Aap (as) ke saamne khana rakha jata to Aap (as) Karbala walon ki bhook ko yaad kar ke rone lag jate the."

(Kitabul Khisaal, Noorus Saqlain)

(To be Cont'd......)

----------------------------------------------

🤲🏻

"Aye Aziz e Misr! Ham aur hamare Ahlo Ayaal Musibat mein giraftar ho chuke hain aur ham kuchh mamooli si poonji laye hain. Aap (as) hame bhar poor Ghalla enayat karen aur hame Khairat karen. Beshak Allah Khairat karne walon ko Jaza deta hai." (12:88)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

    13th Jamadi us Sani 1442

27th January 2021, Wednesday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

            ♦ GIRYA O ZARI ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1635)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَتَوَلَّىٰ عَنۡهُمۡ وَقَالَ یَـٰۤأَسَفَىٰ عَلَىٰ یُوسُفَ وَٱبۡیَضَّتۡ عَیۡنَاهُ مِنَ ٱلۡحُزۡنِ فَهُوَ كَظِیمࣱ *  قَالُوا۟ تَٱللَّهِ تَفۡتَؤُا۟ تَذۡكُرُ یُوسُفَ حَتَّىٰ تَكُونَ حَرَضًا أَوۡ تَكُونَ مِنَ ٱلۡهَـٰلِكِینَ *  قَالَ إِنَّمَاۤ أَشۡكُوا۟ بَثِّی وَحُزۡنِیۤ إِلَى ٱللَّهِ وَأَعۡلَمُ مِنَ ٱللَّهِ مَا لَا تَعۡلَمُونَ.

"Phir (Yaqoob (as)) ne unse Munh pher liya aur kaha: 'Haye Yusuf! Aur Ranj o Gham ki wajah se Unki Aankhe Safed ho gayin aur woh Gham ke ghoont peete rahe."

"Beton ne kaha:' Khudara! Aap to bas Yusuf ko hi yaad kiye jaate hain. Nobat ye aa gayi hai ke uske Gham mein apne Aapko ghula denge ya apni Jaan halaak kar dalenge."

"Aap (as) ne kaha: 'Mein apni pareshani aur apne Gham ki Faryaad Allah ke siwa kisi se nahi karta, aur Allah se jaisa mein waqif hun tum nahi ho."

(Surah Yusuf: 84 - 86)

https://youtu.be/rpymJzfL6x4

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

😢😪😩😭

Ek Yahoodi ne Hazrat Ali (as) se Rasoole Khuda (saww) ke Girya ke bare mein sawal kiya, to Aap (as) ne farmaya:

"Hazrat Yaqoob (as) ne Firaaqe Yusuf (as) par Sabr kiya aur is Sabr ke bawajood unhone itna Girya kiya ke unki Aankhen safed ho gayi thi, jabke hamare Rasoole Karim (saww) ka Jigar Gosha Ibrahim Aapki zindagi mein faut hua, Aap (saww) ne is Maut par ye Jumle farmaye: 'Nafs Gham mehsoos kar raha hai aur Dil jaza (ghabrahat) kar raha hai. Ibrahim, ham teri Maut par Ghamgin hain, lekin ham Zabaan se aisa koi baat nahi nikalenge jo Khuda ko Naraaz kar de.' Hamare Nabi (saww) ne is azeem Musibat par Allah ki Raza ke Taqazon ko madde nazar rakha."

(Kitab Ehtejaje Tabarsi, Noorus Saqlain)

😢😪😩😭

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Makhzoon *محزون* (Udaasi) aur hai aur 'Mutafakkir' متفكر (Fikrmand, Pareshan) aur hai, kyonki Tafakhur mein Takalluf aur Tasanno ki milawat hoti hai (man-made), jabke "Huzn - *حزن* ' Fitri Jazba hai. Huzn ka aghaz Baatin se hota hai aur Fikr o Pareshani ki ibteda hawadis ko dekhne se hoti hai aur in dono kaifiyaton mein bada farq hai. Allah Ta'ala ne Qissa e Yaqoob (as) mein farmaya ke: 'Mein apni Pareshani aur Gham ki shikayat Khuda ke haan karta hun......." 'Huzn' ke jhelni ki wajah se Khuda ne unhe us Ilm se makhsoos kiya jise baqi log nahi jaante the."

(Misbahus Shariyah, Noorus Saqlain)

(To be Cont'd......)

----------------------------------------------

🤲🏻

"Aye Aziz e Misr! Ham aur hamare Ahlo Ayaal Musibat mein giraftar ho chuke hain aur ham kuchh mamooli si poonji laye hain. Aap (as) hame bhar poor Ghalla enayat karen aur hame Khairat karen. Beshak Allah Khairat karne walon ko Jaza deta hai." (12:88)

      ♦ HAZRAT YUSUF (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1636)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَتَوَلَّىٰ عَنۡهُمۡ وَقَالَ یَـٰۤأَسَفَىٰ عَلَىٰ یُوسُفَ وَٱبۡیَضَّتۡ عَیۡنَاهُ مِنَ ٱلۡحُزۡنِ فَهُوَ كَظِیمࣱ *  قَالُوا۟ تَٱللَّهِ تَفۡتَؤُا۟ تَذۡكُرُ یُوسُفَ حَتَّىٰ تَكُونَ حَرَضًا أَوۡ تَكُونَ مِنَ ٱلۡهَـٰلِكِینَ *  قَالَ إِنَّمَاۤ أَشۡكُوا۟ بَثِّی وَحُزۡنِیۤ إِلَى ٱللَّهِ وَأَعۡلَمُ مِنَ ٱللَّهِ مَا لَا تَعۡلَمُونَ.

"Phir (Yaqoob (as)) ne unse Munh pher liya aur kaha: 'Haye Yusuf! Aur Ranj o Gham ki wajah se Unki Aankhe Safed ho gayin aur woh Gham ke ghoont peete rahe."

"Beton ne kaha:' Khudara! Aap to bas Yusuf ko hi yaad kiye jaate hain. Nobat ye aa gayi hai ke uske Gham mein apne Aapko ghula denge ya apni Jaan halaak kar dalenge."

"Aap (as) ne kaha: 'Mein apni pareshani aur apne Gham ki Faryaad Allah ke siwa kisi se nahi karta, aur Allah se jaisa mein waqif hun tum nahi ho."

(Surah Yusuf: 84 - 86)

https://youtu.be/rpymJzfL6x4

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

😩

Rasoole Khuda (saww) & Hazrat Ali (as):

"Jo apni Musibat ka logon ke saamne Shikwa karta hai woh darasl apne Rab ka Shikwa karta hai."

(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim, Nahjul Balagha, Noorus Saqlain)

🤝🏻🤲🏻

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Qahet Saali ki ibtedai ayyam mein ek Eraabi ne Hazrat Yusuf (as) se Ghalla khareeda tha. Ittefaq se uska ghar Kan'an se kuchh aage tha. Aap (as) ki usse farmaya: 'Jab tum falan waadi se guzro to wahan Yaqoob ke naam se awaaz dena. Is awaaz ko sun kar ek Khoobsurat Buzurg tere paas aayenge, unse kehna ke Misr mein mujhe ek shakhs mila tha jisne Aapko 'Salam' kaha hai aur woh keh raha tha Aapki Amanat Khuda ke haan bilkul mehfooz hai. Khuda use hargiz zaye bahi karega.'

Jab Eraabi ne Hazrat Yaqoob (as) ko ye Paigham pahunchaya to Aap (as) behosh ho gaye. Jab kuchh der baad hosh mein aaye to Aapne usse farmaya: 'Tumhari koi Haajat ho to bayan karo. Mein Khuda se tumhari Haajat poori karaunga.'

Eraabi ne kaha: 'Mein Aulaad se mehroom hun.'

Aap (as) ne uske haq mein Dua farmayi. Eraabi ki Biwi Chaar bar Bachche jane aur har janam mein judwan Bachche paida hue."

(Kitab Al-Kharaij Wal-Jaraeh)

(To be Cont'd......)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

      ♦ HAZRAT YUSUF (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1637)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

یَـٰبَنِیَّ ٱذۡهَبُوا۟ فَتَحَسَّسُوا۟ مِن یُوسُفَ وَأَخِیهِ وَلَا تَا۟یۡـَٔسُوا۟ مِن رَّوۡحِ ٱللَّهِۖ إِنَّهُۥ لَا یَا۟یۡـَٔسُ مِن رَّوۡحِ ٱللَّهِ إِلَّا ٱلۡقَوۡمُ ٱلۡكَـٰفِرُونَ.

"Mere Bachcho! Ja kar Yusuf (as) aur uske Bhai ki kuchh toh lagao (search), Allah ki Rehmat se mayoos na ho, Uski Rehmat se to bas Kafir hi mayoos hua karte hain."

(Surah Yusuf: 87)

https://youtu.be/rpymJzfL6x4

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Hazrat Imam Baqir (as):

"Jab Hazrat Yaqoob (as) par azmayishon ka Badal khoob khul kar barse aur Yusuf (as) ke baad Binyamin bhi unse juda ho gaya aur ghar mein Ghalla khatm ho gaya. In sadmaat ki wajah se Aap (as) ki Binaayi khatm ho gayi aur Kamar khameeda ho gayi. Aap (as) ne ghar mein maujood Oon ki kuchh miqdaar Beton ke hawaale ki aur unse farmaya: 'Jao aur Yusuf (as) aur uske Bhai ko talash karo aur Allah ki Rehmat se mayoos na ho..."

"Phir Aap (as) ne Aziz e Misr ke naam ek Khat tehreer kiya aur Aap (as) ne apni Aulad se kaha ke jab Misr pahuncho to mera ye Khat Aziz e Misr ke hawale karo aur iske baad Ghalla farahmi ka zikr karo."

Khat min janib Yaqoob bin Ishaaq bin Ibrahim (as) Aziz e Misr ke naam.....phir poora majra bayan kiya... Ghalla dene ki request ki.....

Jaise hi Khat pahuncha Jibrael (as) Aap (as) par nazil hue aur Khuda ka Paigham sunaya ke Aye Yaqoob tujhe is Masaeb mein Kisne dala, tu apne Masaeb ka Shikwa Aziz e Misr se karta hai? Kya tu Mujh se Shikwa nahi kar sakta tha, tu ne ek Bande se madad talab ki?

Hazrat Yaqoob (as) ne arz kiya: "Khudaya! mein Isteghfar karta hun, Teri hi Bargah mein Tauba karta hun, apne tamam dukhon ka shikwa Tere Huzoor mein pesh karta hun."

Allah Ta'ala ne Wahy farmayi: Meine Adab sikhane ke liye jo Saza tujhe aur teri Aulad ko dena thi ab wo Saza Ikhtetam ko pahunchi. Agar tu ibteda hi se meri Bargah mein rujoo' karta to Mein Apni Taqdeer ko tujh se pher deta. Asl baat ye hai ke Shaitan ne tujh se Mera Zikr faramosh kara diya tha aur tu Meri Rehmat se mayoos ho gaya tha jabke Mein Karim aur Bakhshnewala hun. Mujhe apne Isteghfar karnewale Bande bade pasand hain aur Mein un logon se Muhabbat karta hun jo Tauba karke Meri Bargah mein Rujoo' karen. Ab Mein Yusuf (as) aur uske Bhai se teri mulaqat karaunga aur teri sahet ke nuqsaan ki talafi karunga aur teri Binaayi tujhe wapas karuga aur tera Maali Nuqsaan poora karunga aur teri khameeda Kamar ko seedha karunga aur teri Aankhon ko thandak ata karunga."

(Majmaul Bayan, Amali Shaikhut Taifa, Tafseer e Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)

(To be Cont'd......)

🤲🏻

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Jab Aap (as) ke Farzand Khat le kar rawana hue, us waqt Hazrat Yaqoob (as) ne Aasmaan ki janib haath uthaye aur Bargah e Waahediyat mein ye Darkhwast ki:

يا حسن الصحبة، يا كريم المعونة و يا خير كله، ايتنى بروح منك و فرج من عندك.

"Aye Achhe Masaheb (Saathi)! Aye Ba Izzat Madad karnewale! Aye Khair e Mutlaq Zaat! Apni taraf se mujhe Khushi ata kar aur Ghamon se Najaat ata farma."

Us waqt Jibrael Amin (as) nazil hue aur ye Dua taleem farmayi:

يَا مَنْ لَا يَعْلَمُ اَحَدٌ كَيْفَ هُو وَ قُدْرَتُهٗ اِلَّا هُو، يَا مَنْ سَدـَ الْهَوَاء بِالسـَمَآءِ وَ يَا مَنْ كَبَسَ الأرْضَ عَلَى الْمَآءِ وَ اخْتَارَ لِنَفْسِهِ اَحْسَنَ الْأسْمَاءِ، اِيتنِى بِرُوحٍ مِنْكَ وَ فَرَجٍ مِنْ عِنْدِكَ.

(Aap (as) ki ye Dua se mustajab hui.)

(Tafseer e Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)

 *30th January 2021, Saturday*

     ♦ HAZRAT YUSUF (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1638)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*فَلَمَّا دَخَلُوا۟ عَلَیۡهِ قَالُوا۟ یَـٰۤأَیُّهَا ٱلۡعَزِیزُ مَسَّنَا وَأَهۡلَنَا ٱلضُّرُّ وَجِئۡنَا بِبِضَـٰعَةࣲ مُّزۡجَىٰةࣲ فَأَوۡفِ لَنَا ٱلۡكَیۡلَ وَتَصَدَّقۡ عَلَیۡنَاۤۖ إِنَّ ٱللَّهَ یَجۡزِی ٱلۡمُتَصَدِّقِینَ *  قَالَ هَلۡ عَلِمۡتُم مَّا فَعَلۡتُم بِیُوسُفَ وَأَخِیهِ إِذۡ أَنتُمۡ جَـٰهِلُونَ.*

"Jab ye log Misr ja kar Yusuf (as) ki peshi mein dakhil hue to unhone arz kiya ke: "Aye Aziz e Misr! Ham aur hamare Ahlo Ayaal sakht Musibat mein mubtila hain aur ham kuchh haqeer si Poonji le kar aaye hain, Aap (as) hame bharpoor Ghalla enayat farmayen, aur hamko Khairat den, Allah Khairat karnewalon ko Jaza deta hai."

"(Ye sun kar Yusuf (as) se na raha gaya) Usne kaha: "Kya Tumhe maloom hai ke tumne nadaani mein Yusuf (as) aur uske Bhai ke saath kya kiya tha? Woh chonk kar bole: "Kya tum Yusuf ho?...."

(Surah Yusuf: 88 - 89)

https://youtu.be/rpymJzfL6x4

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 📚📖

👉 Tafseer: 

Hazrat Imam Baqir (as):

".... Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne wo Khat liya aur use choom kar Aankhon se lagaya aur Aap (as) be tahasha roye yahan tak ke Aap (as) ki cheekhen nikal gayin aur Aap (as) ki Qameez Aansuon se tar ho gayi.

Iske baad Farzand e Yaqoob (as) ne Aap (as) se kaha: "Ham thodi se Raqam laye hain.....(Ayat)

Waalid ka Dard Angez Khat padh kar aur Bhaiyyon ka iltijaiyya lehja sun kar Yusuf (as) se raha na gaya aur zabt ke bandhan toot gaye. Aap (as) ne unke sa kaha: "Kya tumhe maloom hai tumne Yusuf (as) aur uske Bhai ke saath kiya sulook kiya?.....(Ayat)

(Majmaul Bayan, Noorus Saqlain)

🤷‍♂ 📖

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Jab koi shakhs Gunah karta hai agarche woh Aalim bhi kyon na ho, Gunah ke waqt woh Jahil ho jata hai. Kya tumne Hazrat Yusuf (as) ka ye farman nahi suna jo unhone apne Bhaiyyon se kaha tha: (12:89) Braderane Yusuf (as) agarche Aalim the magar Hazrat ne unhe Jahil kaha tha aur isse ye saboot milta hai ke Gunah karte waqt Aalim bhi Jahil ban jata hai."

(Majmaul Bayan, Noorus Saqlain)

🤷‍♂

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Aulad e Fatema (sa) (Sadaat) mein se har shakhs marne se pehle Imam e Zamana (as) ka iqraar karke hi marega jaisa ke Braderane Yusuf (as) kafi arse tak Gunahon ki daldal mein phanse rahe lekin akhirkar unhone Yusuf (as) ki Fazilat ka iqraar kiya tha: "Khuda ki Qasam! Khuda ne Aapko Fazilat Bakhshi hai."

(Tafseer e Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)

(To be Cont'd......)

🤲🏻

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Jab Aap (as) ke Farzand Khat le kar rawana hue, us waqt Hazrat Yaqoob (as) ne Aasmaan ki janib haath uthaye aur Bargah e Waahediyat mein ye Darkhwast ki:

*يا حسن الصحبة، يا كريم المعونة و يا خير كله، ايتنى بروح منك و فرج من عندك.*

"Aye Achhe Masaheb (Saathi)! Aye Ba Izzat Madad karnewale! Aye Khair e Mutlaq Zaat! Apni taraf se mujhe Khushi ata kar aur Ghamon se Najaat ata farma."

*يَا مَنْ لَا يَعْلَمُ اَحَدٌ كَيْفَ هُو وَ قُدْرَتُهٗ اِلَّا هُو، يَا مَنْ سَدـَ الْهَوَاء بِالسـَمَآءِ وَ يَا مَنْ كَبَسَ الأرْضَ عَلَى الْمَآءِ وَ اخْتَارَ لِنَفْسِهِ اَحْسَنَ الْأسْمَاءِ، اِيتنِى بِرُوحٍ مِنْكَ وَ فَرَجٍ مِنْ عِنْدِكَ.*

(Aap (as) ki ye Dua se mustajab hui.)

     ♦ HAZRAT YUSUF (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1639)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*قَالُوۤا۟ أَءِنَّكَ لَأَنتَ یُوسُفُۖ قَالَ أَنَا۠ یُوسُفُ وَهَـٰذَاۤ أَخِیۖ قَدۡ مَنَّ ٱللَّهُ عَلَیۡنَاۤۖ إِنَّهُۥ مَن یَتَّقِ وَیَصۡبِرۡ فَإِنَّ ٱللَّهَ لَا یُضِیعُ أَجۡرَ ٱلۡمُحۡسِنِینَ *  قَالُوا۟ تَٱللَّهِ لَقَدۡ ءَاثَرَكَ ٱللَّهُ عَلَیۡنَا وَإِن كُنَّا لَخَـٰطِـِٔینَ *  قَالَ لَا تَثۡرِیبَ عَلَیۡكُمُ ٱلۡیَوۡمَۖ یَغۡفِرُ ٱللَّهُ لَكُمۡۖ وَهُوَ أَرۡحَمُ ٱلرَّ ٰ⁠حِمِینَ.*

"Woh chonk kar bole, "Kya tum Yusuf (as) ho?" Aap (as) ne kaha: "Haan mein Yusuf (as) hun aur ye mera Bhai hai. Allah ne ham par Ehsaan farmaya. Haqeeqat ye hai ke agar koi Taqwa aur Sabr se kaam le to Allah haan aise Nek logon ka Ajr mara nahi jata."

"Unhone ke kaha: "Ba-Khuda ke tumko Allah ne ham par Fazilat Bakhshi aur waqai ham Khatakar the."

"Aap (as) ne jawab diya: "Aaj tum par koi giraft nahi, Allah tumhe Ma'af kare, Woh sab se badh kar Rahem Farmanewala hai."

(Surah Yusuf: 90 - 92)

https://youtu.be/rpymJzfL6x4

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Jab Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne Makkah fatah kiya to Aap (saww) ne Ka'abe ka Darwaza khola. Ka'aba mein But the, Aap (as) ne wo tudwaye aur jo tasweeren thin unhe saaf karaya aur Baitullah ke Darwaze ko pakad kar Aap (saww) ne farmaya:

"Allah ke alawa koi Ma'bood nahi hai, Woh Wahdahu La-Sharik hai. Usne Apna Waada sach kar dikhaya aur apne Bande ki madad ki aur usne tan o tanha tamam girohon ko shikast di."

"Us waqt Makkah ke tamam Zaalim afraad Sar jhukai apni Sarnawisht (Fate) ke intezar mein khade the. Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne un Khoon ke pyason ko khitab karte hue farmaya: "Bolo tum kya kehna chahte ho aur tum kya guman karte ho?"

Unhone kaha: "Ham Aap (saww) se Bhalai ki tawaqqo rakhte hain, Aap (saww) Karim ibne Karim hain."

Us waqt Rehmatul lil Aalameen (saww) ne farmaya:

"Aaj mein tum se wohi jumle kehta hun jo mere Bhai Yusuf (as) ne apne Khatakar Bhaiyyon se kahe the: (12:92) *اذْهَبُوْا فَاَنْتُمِ الطُلُقَاء* Jao Aaj tum hamare Azad kardah ho."

(Al Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)

(To be Cont'd......)

🤲🏻

Imam Sajjad (as):

"Mere Ma'bood! Agar Tu Ma'af kar de to kaun Tujh se zyada Ma'af karnewala hai? Agar Tu Azaab de to kaun Faisla karne mein zyada Aadil hai? Rahem farma is Duniya mein meri bekasi par, maut ke waqt meri takleef par aur qabr mein meri Tanhaai par aur pehlu e qabr mein meri khaufzadgi par rahem farma. Jab main Hisaab ke liye uthaya jaau'n to Apne Huzoor mere bayaan ko narm farma."

(Dua e Abu Hamza Shimaali)

🤲🏻

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Jab Aap (as) ke Farzand Khat le kar rawana hue, us waqt Hazrat Yaqoob (as) ne Aasmaan ki janib haath uthaye aur Bargah e Waahediyat mein ye Darkhwast ki:

*يا حسن الصحبة، يا كريم المعونة و يا خير كله، ايتنى بروح منك و فرج من عندك.*

"Aye Achhe Masaheb (Saathi)! Aye Ba Izzat Madad karnewale! Aye Khair e Mutlaq Zaat! Apni taraf se mujhe Khushi ata kar aur Ghamon se Najaat ata farma."

Us waqt Jibrael Amin (as) nazil hue aur ye Dua taleem farmayi:

*يَا مَنْ لَا يَعْلَمُ اَحَدٌ كَيْفَ هُو وَ قُدْرَتُهٗ اِلَّا هُو، يَا مَنْ سَدـَ الْهَوَاء بِالسـَمَآءِ وَ يَا مَنْ كَبَسَ الأرْضَ عَلَى الْمَآءِ وَ اخْتَارَ لِنَفْسِهِ اَحْسَنَ الْأسْمَاءِ، اِيتنِى بِرُوحٍ مِنْكَ وَ فَرَجٍ مِنْ عِنْدِكَ.*

(Aap (as) ki ye Dua se mustajab hui.)

(Tafseer e Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

   1st February 2021, Monday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

♦ QAMEEZ HAZRAT YUSUF (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1640)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

ٱذۡهَبُوا۟ بِقَمِیصِی هَـٰذَا فَأَلۡقُوهُ عَلَىٰ وَجۡهِ أَبِی یَأۡتِ بَصِیرࣰا وَأۡتُونِی بِأَهۡلِكُمۡ أَجۡمَعِینَ

"Jao aur apne saath meri ye Qameez le jao aur ise mere Waalid ke Chehre par dal do, woh dobara Beena ho jayenge aur apne tamam  Ahlo Ayaal ko le kar mere paas aa jao."

(Surah Yusuf: 93)

https://youtu.be/rpymJzfL6x4

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 📚📖

👉 Tafsir:

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Hazrat Yusuf (as) jab Bhaiyyon ko apna tarruf kara chuke to Asp (as) ne unse farmaya: "Tum meri Aansuon se bhari hui ye Qameez le jao aur ise ja kar mere Waalid ke Chehre par dalo. Unki khoyi hui Beenayi laut aayegi aur tum tamam afraad e Khandan ko yahan mere paas le aao."

Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne apne Waalid ke paas apni Dastaar o Aba nahi bheji thi. Aapne apni Qameez bheji shayad is mein unki Hikmat ye thi ke jab Bhaiyyon ne un par Zulm kiya tha to woh bhi unki Qameez par Jhoota Khoon laga kar Waalid ke paas le gaye the. Us Qameez se unke Waalid ko Aziyyat pahunchi thi. Isiliye Aap (as) ne apne Waalid ko Khushi faraham karne ke liye Aba o Dastaar ke bajaye Qameez hi rawana ki thi.

(Tafseer Ayyashi)

🥼

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Qissa e Yusuf (as) ki Jaan Yusuf (as) ki Qameez par hai. Ek martaba Qameez par Khoon laga. Zulekha ke haathon Qameez phati. Isi Qameez se Hazrat Yaqoob (as) ko binayi mili."

(Kitabul Khisaal, Noorus Saqlain)

🥼

Ek riwayat ye bhi hai:

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Jab Namrud ne Hazrat Ibrahim (as) ko Aag mein dala tha to us waqt Hazrat Jibrael (as) Jannat se ye Qameez le kar aaye the aur unhone wo Qameez Hazrat Ibrahim (as) ko pehnayi thi jiski wajah se Aag thandak aur Salamti mein badal gayi thi. Jab Hazrat Ibrahim (as) ki Wafat ka waqt aaya to Aap (as) ne us Qameez ko samet kar ek Taweez ki tarah se banaya aur use H. Ishaaq ke gale mein bandh diya. Hazrat Ishaaq (as) ne use Taweez bana kar Hazrat Yaqoob (as) ke gale mein bandha tha. Hazrat Yaqoob (as) ne use Taweez bana kar Hazrat Yusuf (as) ke Bazu mein bandha tha.

Jab Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne apne tarruf ke baad apne Bazu se us Qameez ko khola aur farmaya: "Ye Qameez le jao......"

Raavi ne sawal kiya ke iske baad woh Qameez kahan gayi? Aap (as) ne farmaya:

"Woh Qameez unke Ahle Afraad ke haathon mein rahi aur jab Qaem e Aale Muhammad (atfs) Zahoor karenge to wo Qameez unke paas hogi. Anbiya Karam (as) ne jo bhi Ilm aur jitne Tabarrukat chhode hain wo akhir mein Muhammad o Aale Muhammad (as) ke paas jama hain."

(Kamaluddin, Noorus Saqlain)

(To be Cont'd......)

🤲🏻

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Jab Aap (as) ke Farzand Khat le kar rawana hue, us waqt Hazrat Yaqoob (as) ne Aasmaan ki janib haath uthaye aur Bargah e Waahediyat mein ye Darkhwast ki:

يا حسن الصحبة، يا كريم المعونة و يا خير كله، ايتنى بروح منك و فرج من عندك.

"Aye Achhe Masaheb (Saathi)! Aye Ba Izzat Madad karnewale! Aye Khair e Mutlaq Zaat! Apni taraf se mujhe Khushi ata kar aur Ghamon se Najaat ata farma."

Us waqt Jibrael Amin (as) nazil hue aur ye Dua taleem farmayi:

يَا مَنْ لَا يَعْلَمُ اَحَدٌ كَيْفَ هُو وَ قُدْرَتُهٗ اِلَّا هُو، يَا مَنْ سَدـَ الْهَوَاء بِالسـَمَآءِ وَ يَا مَنْ كَبَسَ الأرْضَ عَلَى الْمَآءِ وَ اخْتَارَ لِنَفْسِهِ اَحْسَنَ الْأسْمَاءِ، اِيتنِى بِرُوحٍ مِنْكَ وَ فَرَجٍ مِنْ عِنْدِكَ.

(Aap (as) ki ye Dua se mustajab hui.)

(Tafseer e Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

    19th Jamadi us Sani 1442

   2nd February 2021, Tuesday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

      ♦ HAZRAT YUSUF (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1641)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَلَمَّا فَصَلَتِ ٱلۡعِیرُ قَالَ أَبُوهُمۡ إِنِّی لَأَجِدُ رِیحَ یُوسُفَۖ لَوۡلَاۤ أَن تُفَنِّدُونِ *  قَالُوا۟ تَٱللَّهِ إِنَّكَ لَفِی ضَلَـٰلِكَ ٱلۡقَدِیمِ.

"Jab ye Qafila (Misr se) rawana hua to unke Baap ne (Kan'an mein) kaha: "Mein Yusuf (as) ki Khushbu mehsoos kar raha hun, tum log kahin ye na kahne lago ke mein Budhape mein Satya gaya hun."

"Ghar ke log bole: "Khuda ki Qasam! Aap abhi tak apne usi purane Khabt mein pade hain."

(Surah Yusuf: 94 - 95)

https://youtu.be/rpymJzfL6x4

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 📚📖 🥼

👉 Tafseer:

Qafila Misr se chala. Hazrat Yaqoob (as) us waqt Falisteen (Palestine) mein the. Aap (as) ne uski Khushbu ko mehsoos kar liya tha. Ye Qameez Jannat se laayi gayi thi aur ham uske Waaris hain.

(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi, Noorus Saqlain)

🥼

Egypt aur Palestine mein (us waqt) 10 Raaton ki Masaafat (distance) thi, magar Yaqoob (as) ne uski Khushbu ko mehsoos kar liya tha.

(Tafseer e Ayyashi, Ilalush Sharaye, Noorus Saqlain)

🥼

Algharz Yusuf (as) ki Qameez laayi gayi aur use Hazrat Yaqoob (as) ke Chehre par dala gaya to Aap (as) ki Binaayi laut aayi aur Aap (as) ne apne Bachchon se kaha: "Kya mein tum se ye na kehta tha ke mein Khuda ki taraf se wo kuchh jaanta hun jo tum nahi jaante?

(Noorus Saqlain)

🥼

Khush khabri laane wala Yahooda Bin Yaqoob tha aur usi ne Hazrat Yusuf (as) ki Qameez Hazrat Yaqoob (as) ke Chehre par dali thi jisse unki Beenayi laut aayi thi.

(Kamaluddin, Noorus Saqlain)

⁉️

Raavi ne Imam Sadiq (as) se arz: Kya Farzandan e Yaqoob (as) Nabi the?

Aap (as) farmaya: "Nahi."

Phir poochha: "Kya Khuda ke Saleh Bande tha?"

Aap (as) ne farmaya:

"Jo apne Baap ko ( قَالُوا۟ تَٱللَّهِ إِنَّكَ لَفِی ضَلَـٰلِكَ ٱلۡقَدِیمِ ) Khabti (purani Gumrahi mein pade hain.) kahte hon, woh Saleh kaise ho sakte hain?"

Phir poochha:" Kya haalate Imaan mein Duniya se rukhsat hue?"

Aap (as) ne farmaya: "Ji haan."

(Tafseer e Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)

📖

Hadise Qirtaas: 👉🏻

قَالَ لَمَّا اشْتَدَّ بِالنَّبِيِّ صلى الله عليه وسلم وَجَعُهُ قَالَ ‏"‏ ائْتُونِي بِكِتَابٍ أَكْتُبُ لَكُمْ كِتَابًا لاَ تَضِلُّوا بَعْدَهُ ‏"‏‏.‏ قَالَ عُمَرُ إِنَّ النَّبِيَّ صلى الله عليه وسلم "غَلَبَهُ الْوَجَعُ" وَعِنْدَنَا كِتَابُ اللَّهِ حَسْبُنَا فَاخْتَلَفُوا وَكَثُرَ اللَّغَطُ‏.‏ قَالَ ‏"‏ قُومُوا عَنِّي، وَلاَ يَنْبَغِي عِنْدِي التَّنَازُعُ ‏"‏‏.‏ فَخَرَجَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ يَقُولُ إِنَّ الرَّزِيَّةَ كُلَّ الرَّزِيَّةِ مَا حَالَ بَيْنَ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ صلى الله عليه وسلم وَبَيْنَ كِتَابِهِ‏.‏

Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne farmaya: "Mere paas Samaane Kitabat lao taake tumhare liye ek Tehreer likh dun, taake baad mein tum Gumrah na ho sako", us par Umar (ra) ne logon se kaha ke "is waqt Aap (saww) par *takleef ka ghalba* hai. hamare paas Allah ki Kitab Qur'an kafi hai." (kuchh kitabon mein doosre gair zaroori alfaaz se nawaza gaya hai jaise: Hizyaan etc)  Is par logon ki raye mukhtalif ho gayi aur shor o ghul zyada ho gaya. Aap (saww) ne farmaya: "Chalo niklo mere saamne jaghadna theek nahi." Is par Ibne Abbas ye kehte hue nikle' Beshak Musibat, badi sakht Musibat hai. Wo cheez jo hamare aur Rasool (saww) ke aur Aapki Tehreer ke darmiyan haael ho gayi."

(Ref :Sahih al-Bukhari, Book 3, Hadith 56, or Vol. 1, Book 3, Hadith 114)

👆🏻

Hazrat Yaqoob (as) ke ghar walon ka bayan aur is Riwayat mein Rasool (saww) ko kis tarah se khitab hua, iska mila ke dekhen, Haq zahir ho jayega.

(To be Cont'd......)

----------------------------------------------

🤲🏻

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Jab Aap (as) ke Farzand Khat le kar rawana hue, us waqt Hazrat Yaqoob (as) ne Aasmaan ki janib haath uthaye aur Bargah e Waahediyat mein ye Darkhwast ki:

يا حسن الصحبة، يا كريم المعونة و يا خير كله، ايتنى بروح منك و فرج من عندك.

"Aye Achhe Masaheb (Saathi)! Aye Ba Izzat Madad karnewale! Aye Khair e Mutlaq Zaat! Apni taraf se mujhe Khushi ata kar aur Ghamon se Najaat ata farma."

Us waqt Jibrael Amin (as) nazil hue aur ye Dua taleem farmayi:

يَا مَنْ لَا يَعْلَمُ اَحَدٌ كَيْفَ هُو وَ قُدْرَتُهٗ اِلَّا هُو، يَا مَنْ سَدـَ الْهَوَاء بِالسـَمَآءِ وَ يَا مَنْ كَبَسَ الأرْضَ عَلَى الْمَآءِ وَ اخْتَارَ لِنَفْسِهِ اَحْسَنَ الْأسْمَاءِ، اِيتنِى بِرُوحٍ مِنْكَ وَ فَرَجٍ مِنْ عِنْدِكَ.

(Aap (as) ki ye Dua se mustajab hui.)

(Tafseer e Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)

وہ اتنی دور ہو گیا جتنا قریب تھا
