   4th February 2021, Thursday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

      ♦ HAZRAT YUSUF (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1642)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

فَلَمَّاۤ أَن جَاۤءَ ٱلۡبَشِیرُ أَلۡقَىٰهُ عَلَىٰ وَجۡهِهِۦ فَٱرۡتَدَّ بَصِیرࣰاۖ قَالَ أَلَمۡ أَقُل لَّكُمۡ إِنِّیۤ أَعۡلَمُ مِنَ ٱللَّهِ مَا لَا تَعۡلَمُونَ *  قَالُوا۟ یَـٰۤأَبَانَا ٱسۡتَغۡفِرۡ لَنَا ذُنُوبَنَاۤ إِنَّا كُنَّا خَـٰطِـِٔینَ *  قَالَ سَوۡفَ أَسۡتَغۡفِرُ لَكُمۡ رَبِّیۤۖ إِنَّهُۥ هُوَ ٱلۡغَفُورُ ٱلرَّحِیمُ.

"Phir jab Khush Khabari laanewala aaya to usne Yusuf (as) ki Qameez Yaqoob (as) ke Munh par dal di. Yakayak uski Beenayi laut aayi, tab usne kaha: 'Mein tumse kehta na tha? Mein Allah ki taraf se wo kuchh jaanta hun jo tum nahi jaante."

"Sab bol uthe: 'Abbajan, Aap hamare Gunahon ki Bakhshish ke liye Dua karen, waqai ham Khatakar the."

"Yaqoob (as) ne kaha: 'Mein apne Rab se tumhare liye Ma'afi ki darkhwast karunga, Woh Bada Ma'af Karnewala, aur Rahim hai."

(Surah Yusuf: 96 - 98)

https://youtu.be/rpymJzfL6x4

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 📚📖

👉 Tafseer:  Isteghfar:

Imam Sadiq (as) se sawal hua ke Hazrat Yusuf (as) aur Yaqoob (as) ke tarz e amal mein farq kyon, Yusuf (as) ne Ma'af kar diya jabke Hazrat Yaqoob (as) ne kaha ke Allah se Dua karunga.

Imam (as) ne farmaya:

"Iski wajah ye hai ke Jawan Aadmi ek Buzurg se zyada Rahem Dil hota hai. Braderane Yusuf (as) ne Yusuf (as) par direct zyadti ki thi aur Hazrat Yaqoob (as) par bilwasta zyadti ki thi. Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne unhe unki Khata Ma'af kar di thi jabke Yaqoob (as) ne ma'afi ko uske liye moakhkhr kiya tha ke zyadti barahe raast kisi aur par hui thi. Aap (as) ne Roze Juma ke waqt Seher tak Isteghfar ko Moakhkhar kiya tha."

(Kitab Ilalush Sharaye, Noorus Saqlain)

🤲🏻

Rasoole Khuda (saww):

"Seher ke waqt Qubooliyat e Dua ke liye behtareen hai. Hazrat Yaqoob (as) ne bhi waqt e Seher ke liye Dua ko delay kiya tha."

(Usoole Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)

(To be Cont'd......)

----------------------------------------------

🤲🏻

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Jab Aap (as) ke Farzand Khat le kar rawana hue, us waqt Hazrat Yaqoob (as) ne Aasmaan ki janib haath uthaye aur Bargah e Waahediyat mein ye Darkhwast ki:

يا حسن الصحبة، يا كريم المعونة و يا خير كله، ايتنى بروح منك و فرج من عندك.

"Aye Achhe Masaheb (Saathi)! Aye Ba Izzat Madad karnewale! Aye Khair e Mutlaq Zaat! Apni taraf se mujhe Khushi ata kar aur Ghamon se Najaat ata farma."

Us waqt Jibrael Amin (as) nazil hue aur ye Dua taleem farmayi:

يَا مَنْ لَا يَعْلَمُ اَحَدٌ كَيْفَ هُو وَ قُدْرَتُهٗ اِلَّا هُو، يَا مَنْ سَدـَ الْهَوَاء بِالسـَمَآءِ وَ يَا مَنْ كَبَسَ الأرْضَ عَلَى الْمَآءِ وَ اخْتَارَ لِنَفْسِهِ اَحْسَنَ الْأسْمَاءِ، اِيتنِى بِرُوحٍ مِنْكَ وَ فَرَجٍ مِنْ عِنْدِكَ.

(Aap (as) ki ye Dua se mustajab hui.)

(Tafseer e Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

      ♦ HAZRAT YUSUF (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1643)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

فَلَمَّا دَخَلُوا۟ عَلَىٰ یُوسُفَ ءَاوَىٰۤ إِلَیۡهِ أَبَوَیۡهِ وَقَالَ ٱدۡخُلُوا۟ مِصۡرَ إِن شَاۤءَ ٱللَّهُ ءَامِنِینَ.

"Phir jab ye log Yusuf (as) ke pahunche to usne apne Waaledain ko apne saath betha liya aur (apne sab Kunbe walon se) kaha: "Chalo, ab Shaher mein chalo, Inshallah Aman chain se rahoge."

(Surah Yusuf: 99)

https://youtu.be/rpymJzfL6x4

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Khandan e Hazrat Yaqoob (as) Misr pahunche aur Hazrat Yusuf (as) se mulaqat ki. (tafseel ayinda)

🍂🍃

Imam Musa Kazim (as):

"Hazrat Yaqoob (as) 11 Bete le kar aaye the, unhe hi ' اسباط - Asbaat' kaha jata hai. Binyamin ki Maa Yusuf (as) ki Khala thin."

(Tafseer e Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)

(To be Cont'd....)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

🍲 EVENT OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!! 🍪

🙇

Aaj ghar ghar Niyaz o Dastarkhwan e Imam Hasan (as) ka ehtamam hai. Khushi ka mahaul hai kyonki aaj Munafiq e Ghasib e Haqqe Awwal, Qatil e Zehra (sa) wasil e Jahannum hua. Tarikh e Marg mein ikhtelaf hai lekin English date mein ittefaq hai yani 23rd Aug jise convert karne par urdu ki aaj ki date confirm hai.

Shuru'at to Mannat ki Nazr se hui thi aur kab se hui ye nahi maloom lekin ye buzurgo ki hikmat e amali thi ke hame ek aisa program de diya ke ham Bakre ka Ghosht par Niyaz de kar Mo'meneen ko dawat de kar us Bakre ko yaad karen aur is khushi mein shamil hon. Hare rang ka Dastarkhwan ho, ye rang aam Musalmano mein Islami rang mana jaata hai, Khulafa ka yehi rang hota tha. Tarikh mein Imam Hasan (as) ka Dastarkhwan mashhoor tha aur usi rivayat ko qayem rakha gaya. Ravadari ka lehaz rakhte hue buzurgo ne ye laye amal ikhtiyar kiya. Is mein kitni sachchai hai ye ham nahi kah sakte lekin sahi raasta ikhtiyar kiya.

Kat ti hai apni zindagi aaram-o-chayn se,

Khana Hasan se milta hai paani Husain se.

Maula sab Mo'meneen ki Niyaz qubool farmaye.

----------------------------------------------

🤲🏻

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Jab Aap (as) ke Farzand Khat le kar rawana hue, us waqt Hazrat Yaqoob (as) ne Aasmaan ki janib haath uthaye aur Bargah e Waahediyat mein ye Darkhwast ki:

يا حسن الصحبة، يا كريم المعونة و يا خير كله، ايتنى بروح منك و فرج من عندك.

"Aye Achhe Masaheb (Saathi)! Aye Ba Izzat Madad karnewale! Aye Khair e Mutlaq Zaat! Apni taraf se mujhe Khushi ata kar aur Ghamon se Najaat ata farma."

Us waqt Jibrael Amin (as) nazil hue aur ye Dua taleem farmayi:

يَا مَنْ لَا يَعْلَمُ اَحَدٌ كَيْفَ هُو وَ قُدْرَتُهٗ اِلَّا هُو، يَا مَنْ سَدـَ الْهَوَاء بِالسـَمَآءِ وَ يَا مَنْ كَبَسَ الأرْضَ عَلَى الْمَآءِ وَ اخْتَارَ لِنَفْسِهِ اَحْسَنَ الْأسْمَاءِ، اِيتنِى بِرُوحٍ مِنْكَ وَ فَرَجٍ مِنْ عِنْدِكَ.

(Aap (as) ki ye Dua se mustajab hui.)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

      ♦ HAZRAT YUSUF (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1644)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

 وَرَفَعَ أَبَوَیۡهِ عَلَى ٱلۡعَرۡشِ وَخَرُّوا۟ لَهُۥ سُجَّدࣰاۖ وَقَالَ یَـٰۤأَبَتِ هَـٰذَا تَأۡوِیلُ رُءۡیَـٰیَ مِن قَبۡلُ قَدۡ جَعَلَهَا رَبِّی حَقࣰّاۖ وَقَدۡ أَحۡسَنَ بِیۤ إِذۡ أَخۡرَجَنِی مِنَ ٱلسِّجۡنِ وَجَاۤءَ بِكُم مِّنَ ٱلۡبَدۡوِ مِنۢ بَعۡدِ أَن نَّزَغَ ٱلشَّیۡطَـٰنُ بَیۡنِی وَبَیۡنَ إِخۡوَتِیۤۚ إِنَّ رَبِّی لَطِیفࣱ لِّمَا یَشَاۤءُۚ إِنَّهُۥ هُوَ ٱلۡعَلِیمُ ٱلۡحَكِیمُ.

"(Shaher mein dakhil hone ke baad) Usne apne Waaledain ko utha kar apne paas Takht par baithaya aur sab uske aage be-ikhtiyar Sajde mein jhuk gaye. Yusuf (as) ne kaha: "Abba Jaan! Ye Ta'beer hai mere us Khwab ki jo meine pehle dekha tha, mere Rab ne use Haqeeqat bana diya. Uska Ehsaan hai, Usne mujhe Qaidkhane se nikala, aur aap logon ko Sehra se laa kar mujh se milaya, halanke Shaitan mere aur mere Bhaiyyon ke darmiyan Fasaad dal chuka tha. Waqea ye hai ke mera Rab ghair mehsoos Tadbeeron se Apni Mashiyyat poori karta hai. Beshak Woh Aleem aur Hakeem hai."

(Surah Yusuf: 100)

https://youtu.be/rpymJzfL6x4

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 📚📖 👑🤝🏻

👉 Tafseer:

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Is Ayat mein Arsh se 'Takhte Hukumat' murad hai  aur Hazrat Yaqoob (as) aur unki Aulad ne Khuda ki Ibaadat ka Sajdah kiya tha.

(Noorus Saqlain)

🐪🐫

Hazrat Yaqoob (as) ne apne poore Khandan ko Misr ke liye tayyar kiya aur Palestine chhod kar Misr ki taraf rawana hue aur 9 Din ke qaleel waqt mein Misr pahunche. Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne Waaledain ke isteqbaal ki tayyariyan ki. Isteqbaal e Juloos le kar Shaher se bahar tashreef laaye. Yaqoob (as) apna Khandan le kar Shaher ke qareeb pahunche to Aap (as) Yusuf (as) se milne ke liye sawari se utre. Yusuf (as) ne abhi utrne ka iraada kiya, magar jab unhone apne iqtedar ko dekha to utarne ka iraada tark kiya. Baap bete apas mein mile. Us waqt Jibrael Amin (as) nazil hue aur unse kaha ke Allah Ta'ala tum se keh raha hai ke tum mere Abde Saleh ke liye sawari se kyon na utre? Ab apna haath daraaz karo. Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne haath daraaz kiya to Ungliyon mein se ek Roshni baramad hui. Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne Jibrael (as) se poochha ke ye kaisi Roshni thi? Jibrael (as) ne farmaya: 'Ye Noor e Nabuwwat tha jo tere haatho se nikal gaya. Tumne Yaqoob (as) ka Shayaane Shaan Isteqbaal nahi kiya lehaza ab teri Nasl mein koi Nabi paida nahi hoga.'

(Ilalush Sharaye, Noorus Saqlain)

👑 🙌🏻 🤝🏻

Imam Mohd Baqir (as):

"Jab Hazrat Yaqoob (as) Khandan ke afraad ko le kar Misr aaye to Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne Waalid ko gale lagaya aur girya kiya, unhe aur apni Khaala ko Takht par bithaya aur phir khud apne ghar gaye wahan jaa kar Aap (as) ne Tel lagaya, Surma kiya aur phir Shahana Libaas zebe tan kar ke wapas aaye. Us waqt Hazrat Yaqoob (as) aur unki Zauja aur unke 11 Farzandon ne Allah ka Shukr ada karte hue aur Yusuf (as) ki Tazeem karte hue Sajda kiya.

Jab unhone Sajde se Sar uthaya to Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne kaha: "Abba Jaan! Ye mere us Khwab ki Ta'beer hai jise meine ek arsa qabl dekha tha. Waalid ki mulaqat se qabl poore 20 Saal tak Yusuf (as) ne na to Tel lagaya tha aur na hi Khushbu lagayi thi aur na kabhi hanse the."

(Noorus Saqlain)

🧎🏻‍♂️🙇

Sajdah:

Hazrat Yaqoob (as) aur unke Farzandon ne Hazrat Yusuf (as) ke saamne jo Sajdah kiya tha usse Allah ki Ita'at aur Yusuf (as) ka Salam maqsood tha. Isi tarah se Malaika ne Hazrat Adam (as) ke saamne Sajdah kiya tha usse bhi yahi murad tha.

(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi, Noorus Saqlain)

(To be Cont'd......)

----------------------------------------------

🤲🏻

Jab Hazrat Yaqoob (as) aur unke Farzandon ne Sajdah kiya to us Sajdeh mein Hazrat Yusuf (as) khud bhi shamil the aur unhone Sajdeh mein ye Dua padhi:

رَبِّ قَدۡ ءَاتَیۡتَنِی مِنَ ٱلۡمُلۡكِ وَعَلَّمۡتَنِی مِن تَأۡوِیلِ ٱلۡأَحَادِیثِۚ فَاطِرَ ٱلسَّمَـٰوَ ٰ⁠تِ وَٱلۡأَرۡضِ أَنتَ وَلِیِّۦ فِی ٱلدُّنۡیَا وَٱلۡـَٔاخِرَةِۖ تَوَفَّنِی مُسۡلِمࣰا وَأَلۡحِقۡنِی بِٱلصَّـٰلِحِینَ.

(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi, Noorus Saqlain)

      ♦ HAZRAT YUSUF (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1645)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

 رَبِّ قَدۡ ءَاتَیۡتَنِی مِنَ ٱلۡمُلۡكِ وَعَلَّمۡتَنِی مِن تَأۡوِیلِ ٱلۡأَحَادِیثِۚ فَاطِرَ ٱلسَّمَـٰوَ ٰ⁠تِ وَٱلۡأَرۡضِ أَنتَ وَلِیِّۦ فِی ٱلدُّنۡیَا وَٱلۡـَٔاخِرَةِۖ تَوَفَّنِی مُسۡلِمࣰا وَأَلۡحِقۡنِی بِٱلصَّـٰلِحِینَ.

"Aye mere Rab, Tu ne mujhe Hukumat Bakhshi aur mujhko Khwabon ki Taveel (Baaton ki teh tak pahunchna) sikhayi. Zameen o Aasmaan ko banane wale, Tu hi Duniya o Akherat mein mera Sarparast hai. Mera khaatma Islam par kar aur Anjamkar mujhe Salehin ke saath mila."

(Surah Yusuf: 101)

https://youtu.be/rpymJzfL6x4

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 📚📖 👑🤲🏻

👉 Tafseer:

👆🏻🤲🏻  Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne ye Dua ki.

"Us waqt Jibrael Amin (as) Aap (as) par nazil hue aur unhone kaha: "Aap (as) apna haath phailayin." Jaise hi Aap (as) ne haath phailaya to Aap (as) ki Ungliyon se Roshni baramad hui. Aap (as) ne Jibrael (as) se poochha: 'Ye kya hai?' Jibrael (as) ne kaha: 'Ye Noor e Nabuwwat hai, jise Khuda ne tumhari Sulb se nikal liya hai, kyonki tum apne Waalid ke saamne khade nahi hue. Ab teri Nasl mein se koi Nabi paida na hoga. Allah ne teri bajaye Silsila e Nabuwwat tere Bhai Laavi bin Yaqoob (as) ki Sulb mein rakh diya hai.

Imam Musa Kazim (as):

"Khuda ko Laavi ki do adaayen pasand aayin thi: Jab Braderane Yusuf (as) ne Yusuf (as) ko Qatl karne ka iraada kiya tha to us waqt Laavi ne madakhalat ki thi aur kaha tha Qatl na karo iske bajaye use kisi Andhe Kuwen mein dal do. Jab Yusuf (as) ne Binyamin ko apne paas rok liya tha to Laavi ne hi Bhaiyyon se kaha tha ke tum Abbajan ke paas chale jao, mein yahan hi rahunga."

"Allah Ta'ala ne Laavi ki Nasl mein Silsila e Nabuwwat ko rakh diya aur Bani Israel ke Anbiya usi ki Nasl se hi talluq rakhte the. Hazrat Musa (as) ka talluq bhi isi Khandan se tha. Aapka Nasab Nama ye hai:

Musa bin Imraan bin Yahsir bin wahas bin Laavi bin Yaqoob bin Ishaaq bin Ibrahim (as)."

(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi, Noorus Saqlain)

😢

Hazrat Yaqoob (as) Hazrat Yusuf (as) se jab bhi poochhte ke tere Bhaiyyon ne tujh se kya sulook kiya tha? Uske jawab mein Hazrat Yusuf (as) kehte: "Abbajan! Ye na poochhen ke Bhaiyyon ne mujhse kya Sulook kiya. Iske bajaye ye poochhen ke Khuda ne mujh par kitna Karam kiya."

(Majmaul Bayan, Noorus Saqlain)

🕌

Ameerul Mo'meneen Ali (as) ne Shaami Yahoodi ke sawal ka jawab diya:

"Agar Yusuf (as) Chaahe Kan'an mein Qaid rahe to hamare Rasool (saww) Shebe Abi Talib (as) mein poore 3 Saal mehsoor rahe, Ghaare Thaur mein 3 Din tak qayam kiya. Aur agar Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne Khwab dekha tha to hamare Rasool (saww) ne bhi Khwab dekha tha ke woh aur unke saathi Masjidul Haram mein Sar mundaye ya Taqseer karaye hue dakhil ho rahe hain. Hazrat Yusuf (as) ka Khwab unki Shahi ki alamat bana aur hamare Rasool (saww) ka Khwab Fateh Makkah ki alamat bana."

(Kitab Ehtejaj e Tabarsi, Noorus Saqlain)

(To be Cont'd......)

----------------------------------------------

🤲🏻

Jab Hazrat Yaqoob (as) aur unke Farzandon ne Sajdah kiya to us Sajdeh mein Hazrat Yusuf (as) khud bhi shamil the aur unhone Sajdeh mein ye Dua padhi:

رَبِّ قَدۡ ءَاتَیۡتَنِی مِنَ ٱلۡمُلۡكِ وَعَلَّمۡتَنِی مِن تَأۡوِیلِ ٱلۡأَحَادِیثِۚ فَاطِرَ ٱلسَّمَـٰوَ ٰ⁠تِ وَٱلۡأَرۡضِ أَنتَ وَلِیِّۦ فِی ٱلدُّنۡیَا وَٱلۡـَٔاخِرَةِۖ تَوَفَّنِی مُسۡلِمࣰا وَأَلۡحِقۡنِی بِٱلصَّـٰلِحِینَ.

(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

      ♦ HAZRAT YUSUF (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1646)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

ذَ ٰ⁠لِكَ مِنۡ أَنۢبَاۤءِ ٱلۡغَیۡبِ نُوحِیهِ إِلَیۡكَۖ وَمَا كُنتَ لَدَیۡهِمۡ إِذۡ أَجۡمَعُوۤا۟ أَمۡرَهُمۡ وَهُمۡ یَمۡكُرُونَ * وَمَاۤ أَكۡثَرُ ٱلنَّاسِ وَلَوۡ حَرَصۡتَ بِمُؤۡمِنِینَ.

"Aye Muhammad (saww)! Ye Qissa Ghaib ki Khabron mein se hai jo Ham tum par Wahy kar rahe hain, warna tum us waqt maujood na the jab Yusuf (as) ke Bhaiyyon ne apas mein ittefaq karke Sazish ki thi. Magar Aap (saww) khwah kitna hi kyon na chahen phir bhi logon ki aksariyat Imaan qubool nahi karegi."

(Surah Yusuf: 102 - 103)

https://youtu.be/rpymJzfL6x4

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Tazkara Hazrat Yusuf (as) ab akheri marhale mein hai.

🌜💭

Raavi ne Imam Sadiq (as) se apna Khwab sunaya ke usne apne Murda Damad, jiska naam Husain tha, se gale lagaya. Woh samajha Maut ka waqt qareeb hai.

Imam (as) ne farmaya:

"Insaan ko har waqt Maut ka Intezar karte rahna chahiye lekin tumhare Khwab ki ye Ta'beer nahi hai. Agar Khwab mein koi Murda kisi ke gale mile to ye Tool e Umr ko alamat hoti hai.

"Jo bhi Imam Husain (as) ke kisi ham-naam ko gale lagaye to use Hazrat Imam Husain (as) ki Ziyarat naseeb hoti hai."

(Noorus Saqlain)

⚰️🕌

Imam Baqir (as) ne ek sawal ke jawab mein farmaya:

"Hazrat Yaqoob (as) Hazrat Yusuf (as) ki mulaqat ke baad do Saal zinda rahe the. Hazrat Yaqoob (as) Hujjat e Khuda the aur Iqtedar Hazrat Yusuf (as) ka tha. Jab Hazrat Yaqoob (as) ki wafat hui to Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne unki Lash ko Taboot mein rakha aur unki Lash ko Baitul Muqaddas mein Dafan karayi. Hazrat Yaqoob (as) ke baad Hazrat Yusuf (as) Hujjat e Khuda ke Mansab par faiz hue. Aap (as) bhi Nabi the. Hazrat Yaqoob (as) ki Nabuwwat sar Zameen e Kan'an tak mehdood thi. Phir Aap (as) Kan'an se Misr Tashrif laaye aur wahan Aap (as) ki Wafat hui."

(Majmaul Bayan, Kamaluddin, Noorus Saqlain)

(To be Cont'd......)

----------------------------------------------

🤲🏻

Jab Hazrat Yaqoob (as) aur unke Farzandon ne Sajdah kiya to us Sajdeh mein Hazrat Yusuf (as) khud bhi shamil the aur unhone Sajdeh mein ye Dua padhi:

رَبِّ قَدۡ ءَاتَیۡتَنِی مِنَ ٱلۡمُلۡكِ وَعَلَّمۡتَنِی مِن تَأۡوِیلِ ٱلۡأَحَادِیثِۚ فَاطِرَ ٱلسَّمَـٰوَ ٰ⁠تِ وَٱلۡأَرۡضِ أَنتَ وَلِیِّۦ فِی ٱلدُّنۡیَا وَٱلۡـَٔاخِرَةِۖ تَوَفَّنِی مُسۡلِمࣰا وَأَلۡحِقۡنِی بِٱلصَّـٰلِحِینَ.

(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

♦ H. YUSUF (as) & ZULEKHA ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1647)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

ذَ ٰ⁠لِكَ مِنۡ أَنۢبَاۤءِ ٱلۡغَیۡبِ نُوحِیهِ إِلَیۡكَۖ وَمَا كُنتَ لَدَیۡهِمۡ إِذۡ أَجۡمَعُوۤا۟ أَمۡرَهُمۡ وَهُمۡ یَمۡكُرُونَ * وَمَاۤ أَكۡثَرُ ٱلنَّاسِ وَلَوۡ حَرَصۡتَ بِمُؤۡمِنِینَ. * وَمَا تَسۡـَٔلُهُمۡ عَلَیۡهِ مِنۡ أَجۡرٍۚ إِنۡ هُوَ إِلَّا ذِكۡرࣱ لِّلۡعَـٰلَمِینَ.

"Aye Muhammad (saww)! Ye Qissa Ghaib ki Khabron mein se hai jo Ham tum par Wahy kar rahe hain, warna tum us waqt maujood na the jab Yusuf (as) ke Bhaiyyon ne apas mein ittefaq karke Sazish ki thi. Magar Aap (saww) khwah kitna hi kyon na chahen phir bhi logon ki aksariyat Imaan qubool nahi karegi. Halanke tum unse in Baaton ki koi Ujrat bhi nahi mangte ho, ye to tamam Jahanon ke liye Nasihat hai."

(Surah Yusuf: 102 - 104)

https://youtu.be/rpymJzfL6x4

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Tazkara Hazrat Yusuf (as) ab akheri marhale mein hai.

Jab Yusuf (as) Badshah bane to us waqt Zulekha par zawal chha chuka tha. Shauhar mar chuka tha, khud boodhi ho gayi thi aur Road par logon se Khairat maang kar guzar basar kar rahi thi.

(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi, Noorus Saqlain)

💔

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Zulekha Yusuf (as) se milne ke liye Aap (as) ke Darwaze par aayi aur usne Ijazat talab ki. Kisi ne kaha: 'Tu ne un par zulm kiya tha ho sakta hai ke woh tujhe Saza den isliye behtar hai ke unse mulaqat hi na karo.'

Zulekha ne kaha: 'Darna usse chahiye jo Khuda se na darta ho. Yusuf (as) to Khuda se darne wala hai, lehaza mujhe uska koi kauf nahi hai. Algharz Zulekha ko ijazat mili to Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne farmaya:

"Zulekha! Ye kya hua, tumhara to Rang tak badal chuka hai?"

Zulekha:

"Us Zaat ki Hamd hai Jisne Nafarmani ki wajah se Badshahon ko Ghulam aur Ita'at ki wajah se Ghulamon ko Badshah bana diya."

Yusuf (as):

"Tumne mujh se ye kya sulook kiya tha?"

Zulekha:

"Mein Aapki Khoobsurati se majboor ho gayi thi."

Yusuf (as):

"Agar tu akheri Zamane mein mab'oos hone wale Nabi ko dekh leti jiska Naam Muhammad (saww) hoga jo mujh se zyada Haseen o Jameel aur mujh se zyada sakht hoga tab na jaane teri kaifiyat kya hoti?"

Zulekha:

"Aap (as) ne bilkul sach farmaya."

Yusuf (as):

"Tujhe kaise pata chala ke meine sach kaha hai?"

Zulekha:

"Aap (as) ne jaise hi unka naam liya to unki Muhabbat mere Dil mein ghar kar gayi. Isse maloom hua ke Aap (as) sach keh rahe hain."

Us waqt Allah Ta'ala ne Yusuf (as) ko Wahy ki ke: "Ye sach keh rahi hai. Usne Mere Muhammad (saww) se Muhabbat ki hai to Mujhe usse Muhabbat ho gayi hai."

Phir Allah Ta'ala ne Hazrat Yusuf (as) ko usse Shaadi karne ka Hukm diya."

(Kitab Ilalush Sharaye, Noorus Saqlain)

🗒️📈

Rasoole Khuda (saww):

"Hazrat Yaqoob (as) ne 140 Saal ki Umr payi thi aur Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne 120 Saal ki Umr payi thi."

(Kamaluddin, Noorus Saqlain)

Hazrat Yusuf (as) jab Zindan mein gaye to Aap (as) 12 Baras ke the aur 18 Baras Zindan mein rahe aur Zindan ki rihai ke baas 80 Saal tak zinda rahe.

(Majmaul Bayan, Noorus Saqlain)

(To be Cont'd......)

----------------------------------------------

🤲🏻

Jab Hazrat Yaqoob (as) aur unke Farzandon ne Sajdah kiya to us Sajdeh mein Hazrat Yusuf (as) khud bhi shamil the aur unhone Sajdeh mein ye Dua padhi:

رَبِّ قَدۡ ءَاتَیۡتَنِی مِنَ ٱلۡمُلۡكِ وَعَلَّمۡتَنِی مِن تَأۡوِیلِ ٱلۡأَحَادِیثِۚ فَاطِرَ ٱلسَّمَـٰوَ ٰ⁠تِ وَٱلۡأَرۡضِ أَنتَ وَلِیِّۦ فِی ٱلدُّنۡیَا وَٱلۡـَٔاخِرَةِۖ تَوَفَّنِی مُسۡلِمࣰا وَأَلۡحِقۡنِی بِٱلصَّـٰلِحِینَ.

(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

♦ H. YUSUF (as) KI WAFAT ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1647)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

ذَ ٰ⁠لِكَ مِنۡ أَنۢبَاۤءِ ٱلۡغَیۡبِ نُوحِیهِ إِلَیۡكَۖ وَمَا كُنتَ لَدَیۡهِمۡ إِذۡ أَجۡمَعُوۤا۟ أَمۡرَهُمۡ وَهُمۡ یَمۡكُرُونَ * وَمَاۤ أَكۡثَرُ ٱلنَّاسِ وَلَوۡ حَرَصۡتَ بِمُؤۡمِنِینَ. * وَمَا تَسۡـَٔلُهُمۡ عَلَیۡهِ مِنۡ أَجۡرٍۚ إِنۡ هُوَ إِلَّا ذِكۡرࣱ لِّلۡعَـٰلَمِینَ.

"Aye Muhammad (saww)! Ye Qissa Ghaib ki Khabron mein se hai jo Ham tum par Wahy kar rahe hain, warna tum us waqt maujood na the jab Yusuf (as) ke Bhaiyyon ne apas mein ittefaq karke Sazish ki thi. Magar Aap (saww) khwah kitna hi kyon na chahen phir bhi logon ki aksariyat Imaan qubool nahi karegi. Halanke tum unse in Baaton ki koi Ujrat bhi nahi mangte ho, ye to tamam Jahanon ke liye Nasihat hai."

(Surah Yusuf: 102 - 104)

https://youtu.be/rpymJzfL6x4

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Tazkara Hazrat Yusuf (as) ab akheri marhale mein aa gaya hai.

Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne Jame Sawaal ki wazahat karte hue bayan farmaya:

"Jab Hazrat Yusuf (as) ki Wafat hui to Mulke Misr ke har Shaher ke logon ne is khwahish ka izhaar kiya ke unki Laash unke hawale ki jaye taake woh apne Shaher mein le ja kar unhe dafan karen aur unke wujood se barkat haasil karen. Jab logon ka israar badha to aakhir mein ye faisla kiya gaya ke Aap (as) ki Laash ko ek Taboot mein rakh kar darya mein dafan kar diya jaye taake darya ka Paani Aap (as) ki Qabr se mas (touch) ho kar poore Misr ko seraab kare aur yun poora Mulk Aap (as) ki Barkat se istefada kar sake."

Udhar Hazrat Yusuf (as) ne aakhiri waqt mein ye Wasiyyat ki thi ke jab Bani Israel Misr ko kairbad kahe to unke Jasad e khaaki ko bhi yahan se nikal kar apne saath Palestine mein le jayen. Chunanche Yusuf (as) ko Darya mein Dafan kiya gaya aur ek taveel arse baad Hazrat Musa (as) mab'oos hue aur Allah ne unhe Hukm diya ke Firaun doob chuka hai, lehaza tum apni Qaum ko Arz e Falisteen mein wapas le jao aur jab tak tum Yusuf (as) ke Jasad e Khaaki (body) ko yahan se nahi nikaloge us waqt tak Chaand tulu na hoga."

Hazrat Musa (as) ne logon se kaha ke kya is waqt poore Misr mein aisa shakhs maujood hai jise Yusuf (as) ki Qabr ka sahih pata ho?"

Aap (as) ko bataya gaya ke ek Budhiya ko sahih maloom hai.

Hazrat Musa (as) ke kehne par log usko unke paas laye.

Hazrat Musa (as) ne usse Qabr ka pata poochha.

Us Aurat ne kaha: "Mein hargiz na bataongi jab tak meri Sharten poori na ho jayen."

Sharten ye hain:

1. Mein chalne phirne se mazoor hun Dua karen ke meri Taagen sahi ho jayen aur mein chal sakun.

2. Mein Aankho se Nabeena hun Khuda meri Beenayi ata farmaye.

3. Allah mujhe dubara Shabab (Jawani) ata kare.

4. Mein Jannat mein bhi Aap (as) ki Rafeeqa banun."

Hazrat Musa (as) ko uske sawal garan mehsoos hue. Allah Ta'ala ne Wahy farmayi:

"Aya Musa! Use sab kuchh milna to Meri jaanib se hai tum kyon pareshan ho rahe ho."

Algharz uske sari sharte manzoor kar li gayin aur usne Hazrat Yusuf (as) ki Qabr ki Nishandahi ki.

Jab us jagah ko khoda gaya to wahan se marmar Sandooq baramad hui. Us mein Hazrat Yusuf (as) ka Jasad e Khaaki tha. Iske baad Chaand tulu hone laga. Hazrat Musa (as) unka Taboot apne saath le gaye. Yehi wajah hai ke Ahle Kitab apne Murdon ko Shaam (Syria) (including Palestine of today) le ja kar Dafan karte hain."

(Rauza e Kaafi, Man La Yahzarahul Faqih, Noorus Saqlain)

(To be Cont'd......)

----------------------------------------------

🤲🏻

Jab Hazrat Yaqoob (as) aur unke Farzandon ne Sajdah kiya to us Sajdeh mein Hazrat Yusuf (as) khud bhi shamil the aur unhone Sajdeh mein ye Dua padhi:

رَبِّ قَدۡ ءَاتَیۡتَنِی مِنَ ٱلۡمُلۡكِ وَعَلَّمۡتَنِی مِن تَأۡوِیلِ ٱلۡأَحَادِیثِۚ فَاطِرَ ٱلسَّمَـٰوَ ٰ⁠تِ وَٱلۡأَرۡضِ أَنتَ وَلِیِّۦ فِی ٱلدُّنۡیَا وَٱلۡـَٔاخِرَةِۖ تَوَفَّنِی مُسۡلِمࣰا وَأَلۡحِقۡنِی بِٱلصَّـٰلِحِینَ.

(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi, Noorus Saqlain)

 11th February 2021, Thursday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

     ♦ NADANASTA SHIRK ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1648)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَكَأَیِّن مِّنۡ ءَایَةࣲ فِی ٱلسَّمَـٰوَ ٰ⁠تِ وَٱلۡأَرۡضِ یَمُرُّونَ عَلَیۡهَا وَهُمۡ عَنۡهَا مُعۡرِضُونَ * وَمَا یُؤۡمِنُ أَكۡثَرُهُم بِٱللَّهِ إِلَّا وَهُم مُّشۡرِكُونَ.

"Zameen aur Aasmaano mein kitni hi Nishaniyan hain jin par se ye log guzarte rehte hain aur zara Tawajjoh nahi karte."

"In mein se aksar Allah ko maante bhi hain to bhi Uske saath doosron ko sharik karte hain."

(Surah Yusuf: 105 - 106)

https://youtu.be/rpymJzfL6x4

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Ayat (12:105) mein Suraj Girhan, Chaand Girhan, Zalzala aur Bijli girne jaisi Asmaani Nishaniyan murad hain.

(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi, Noorus Saqlain)

🕌

Imam Baqir (as) Ayat (12:106) ke silsile mein farmaya:

"Isse Shirke Ita'at murad hai, Shirke Ibaadat nahi. Jab log Ma'asi (Gunah) ka irtekab karte hain to us waqt woh Amali taur par Shaitan ki ita'at kar rahe hote hain, jabke Ita'at sirf Khuda ki karni chahiye. Log Shaitan ki ita'at karke Shirk fil Ita'at ka muzahera karte hain, jabke woh us ma'ani mein sharik nahi karte ke Khuda ko chhod kar Ghairullah ki Ibaadat karne lag jayen."

(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi, Noorus Saqlain)

🕌

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Asmaa e Husna Khuda ke liye makhsoos hain aur in Asmaa ka itlaaq Ghairullah ke liye durust nahi hai aur Asmaa e Husna wo Asmaa hain jinka Zikr Allah ne apni Kitab mein kiya hai aur farmaya: "Aur Allah ke liye Asmaaul Husna hain, inko achhe Naamo se pukaro aur un logon ko chod do jo Uske Naamo mein Haqeeqat se iheraaf karte hain."

"Jo shakhs Ilm ke baghair Khuda ke Naamo mein Haqeeqat se inheraaf karta hai to woh ghair-danista (unintentionally) taur par Shirk karta hai aur woh apne guman ke mutabiq achha kar raha hota hai, jabke woh dar haqeeqat Kufr mein mubtila ho raha hota hai. Aise hi logon ke liye Allah ne farmaya (12:106) Chunanche ye woh log hain jo Khuda ke Asmaa mein Ilm ke baghair inheraaf karte hain aur use ghair munasib maqamat par rakhte hain."

(Kitabut Tauheed, Noorus Saqlain)

🕌

Imam baqir (as):

"Jo shakhs kisi se ye kahe mujhe teri Zindagi ki Qasam hai to is Ayat ke zimn mein woh bhi shamil hai."

(Tafseer e Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)

(To be Cont'd......)

🤲🏻

Imam Sajjad (as):

"Pus, Hamd Tere liye hai ke Tu ne mere Dil ko Shirk se Paak kiya. Tere hi liye Hamd hai ke Tu ne meri Zabaan ko goya kiya. Aaya main is teddi-meddi Zabaan se Tera Shukr ada kar sakta hun? Ya Amal mein koshish kar ke Tujhe Raazi kar sakta hun? Aye Parwardigar! Teri Hamd ke muqabil meri Zabaan ki kya haisiyat hai aur Ne'mato'n aur Ehsaano'n ke saamne mere Amal ka kya wazn hai? Mere Ma'bood! Teri sakhawat ne meri Aarzu ko badhaya aur Teri Qadr-daani ne mere Amal ko qubool farmaya hai."

(Dua-e-Abu Hamza Sumali)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

◼️ WAFAT UMME KULSUM BINTE ALI (as) ◼️

     29th Jamadi us Sani 1442

    12th February 2021, Friday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

     ♦ NADANASTA SHIRK ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1649)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَمَا یُؤۡمِنُ أَكۡثَرُهُم بِٱللَّهِ إِلَّا وَهُم مُّشۡرِكُونَ.

"In mein se aksar Allah ko maante bhi hain to bhi Uske saath doosron ko sharik karte hain."

(Surah Yusuf: 106)

https://youtu.be/rpymJzfL6x4

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 📚📖

👉 Tafseer:  (Cont'd)

Imam Sadiq ( as) is Ayat ke bare mein daryaft kiya to Aap (as) ne farmaya:

"Isse woh shakhs murad hai jo kisi se ye kahe: "Agar falan na hota to mein halak ho jata" ya "Agar Falan na hota to mein Falan Falan cheez hasil kar leta" ya "Falan na hota to mera Maal zaye ho jata." (Umar ne yehi to kaha tha: Agar Ali (as) na hote to mein halaak ho jata.)

"Kya tum in misaalon mein nahi dekhte ke aise Kalam karne walon ne Khuda ke Sharik muqarrar kiye hain jo inhe Rizq de sakta hain aur unse Masaib door kar sakte hain."

Raavi ne kaha ke agar is tarah kaha jaye to:

"Agar Khuda Falan shakhs ke zariye se meri Madad na karata to mein halaak ho jata"?

Imam (as) ne farmaya ke is mein koi qabahat nahi hai." (This is ok)

(Tafseer e Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)

🕌

Imam Reza (as) se is Ayat ke zel mein 3 mafhoom hain:

1. Isse Mushrekin e Quresh murad hain, jo Khuda ke Khaliq (Creator) aur Mohyee o Momeet (Zindagi o Maaut Denewala) hone ka iqraar karte the, magar Buton ki Ma'bood samajh kar unki Pooja bhi karte the aur Zabaan se kehte the Allah hamara Rab hai aur hamara Ma'bood hame Rizq ata karta hai.

2. Ye Ayat Mushrekin e Arab ke mutalliq nazil hui, jab un se poochha jata tha ke Asmaan o Zameen ka Khaliq kaun hai aur Baadlon se Paani kaun barsata hai to iske jawab mein woh Allah ka Naam lete the, lekin woh apne iqraar par qaem nahi rehte the aur apne Talbiya mein kehte the:

   الا شريك هو لك تملكه و ما ملك

( "Tera bas ek hi Sharik hai jiska Tu Malik hai aur Woh Tera Malik nahi hai.")

3. Isse Mushrekin e Ahle Kitab murad hain. Woh log zahiri taur par Allah, Roz e Akherat aur Taurat o Injeel par Imaan rakhte the, lekin Qur'an e Karim aur Hazrat Muhammad Mustafa (saww) ka inkaar karte the."

(Majmaul Bayan, Noorus Saqlain)

🕌

Imam Sadiq (as):

الشرک اخفی من دبیب النمل

"Insaani Amaal Shirk Chiunti (Ant) ki chal se bhi zyada makhfi (hidden) hai."

(Safinatul Bihar, Vol 1, P-1697)

🕌

Rasoole Khuda (saww):

"Khatarnak cheez ke jiska mujhe tum se khauf hai 'Shirk e Asghar' hai."

"Riyakari (Showoff), Qayamat ke Din jab log apne Amal ke saath Bargahe Khuda mein hazir honge to Parwardigar unhe jo Duniya mein Riyakari karte the, Farmayega: 'Unke paas jao, ke jinke liye tum Riya karte the aur dekho ke unke haan se tumhe koi Ajr milta hai?"

(Tafseer fi Zalal, Vol 5, P-53)

🤲🏻

Imam Sajjad (as):

"Pus, Hamd Tere liye hai ke Tu ne mere Dil ko Shirk se Paak kiya. Tere hi liye Hamd hai ke Tu ne meri Zabaan ko goya kiya. Aaya main is teddi-meddi Zabaan se Tera Shukr ada kar sakta hun? Ya Amal mein koshish kar ke Tujhe Raazi kar sakta hun? Aye Parwardigar! Teri Hamd ke muqabil meri Zabaan ki kya haisiyat hai aur Ne'mato'n aur Ehsaano'n ke saamne mere Amal ka kya wazn hai? Mere Ma'bood! Teri sakhawat ne meri Aarzu ko badhaya aur Teri Qadr-daani ne mere Amal ko qubool farmaya hai."

(Dua-e-Abu Hamza Sumali)

          ♦ MAUT O BALAA ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1650)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

أَفَأَمِنُوۤا۟ أَن تَأۡتِیَهُمۡ غَـٰشِیَةࣱ مِّنۡ عَذَابِ ٱللَّهِ أَوۡ تَأۡتِیَهُمُ ٱلسَّاعَةُ بَغۡتَةࣰ وَهُمۡ لَا یَشۡعُرُونَ.

"Kya ye Mutmain hain ke Khuda ke Azaab ki koi Bala inhe daboch na legi ya bekhabari mein Qayamat ki ghadi achanak un par na aa jayegi?

(Surah Yusuf: 106)

https://youtu.be/rpymJzfL6x4

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Insaan is Duniya mein aise rehta hai jaise use yahan hamesha rehna hai. Har shakhs ki khwahish hoti hai ke mein din ba din is Duniya mein taraqqi karta jaon. Uski Arzuen Aasmaan chhune lagti hain. Duniya ki tez raftar Zindagi mein woh ye bhool jata hai ke woh Gunah kar raha hai ya Neki. Woh apne Khaliq ko bhool jata hai. Allah ke Azaab ki talwar har waqt uske Sar par latakti rehti hai. Thokre khata rehta hai sanbhalta rehta hai lekin isse koi sabaq hasil nahi karta. Ye bhi dekhta rehta hai ke aaj kisi ko Maut aayi to kal kisi aur ko. Ye nahi samajhta ke ek din iska bhi number aayega. Is sab ke bawajood mutmain baitha rehta hai. Bala ya Maut kab kis ko aa ghere ye kisi ko nahi maloom. Ye achanak aayengi.

Isliye Insaan ko chahiye is Duniya mein Kirayedar ki hasiyat se rahe. Aapka Malik Allah hai. Jisne aapko Hayat di hai Wohi le bhi lega. Khuda ka Banda ban kar rahe. Khauf e Khuda har waqt Dil mein basaye rakhen. Iske baad phir har Mushkil mein Khuda se lao lagayen. Jab aap Uske ho jayenge to Woh bhi Tumhara ho jayega. Ahle Bait (as) ki Muhabbat Qurbe Ilahi ka zariya hai. Kyonki Allah inhi ki shifarish ko qubool karta. Jo inke Raaste par chalega wohi Uska Muhib hoga, usiki Zindagi Mutmain hogi. Phir Allah usko is tarah apne paas bulayega:

یَـٰۤأَیَّتُهَا ٱلنَّفۡسُ ٱلۡمُطۡمَىِٕنَّةُ. ٱرۡجِعِیۤ إِلَىٰ رَبِّكِ رَاضِیَةࣰ مَّرۡضِیَّةࣰ. (28-89:27)

"Aye Nafs e Mutmainna, tu apne Rab ki taraf Raazi Marzi se laut aa."

⚰️

Imam Baqir (as):

"Momin ki Nishaani ye hai ke jab uski Maut ka waqt aata hai to uske chehre ka rang jitna safed tha usse zyada safed aur raushan ho jaata hai, Pehsaani par paseena aane lagta hai, uski Aa'nkho’n se Aa'nsuo’n ki tarah rutubat behne lagti hai; to yehi uski Rooh nikalne ki nishaani hai…"

(Man La Yahzarahul Faqih, v1, p100)

⚰️

 Rasule Khuda (saww):

"Aye Abuzar! Kya Jannat mein daakhil hona chahte ho?" Farmaya, "Haa'n. Aap par mere maa baap qurbaan". Aap (saww) ne farmaya, "(3 kaam karo) (1) Aarzu kam karo, (2) Maut ko har waqt Aa'nkho'n ke saamne rakho, (3) Khuda se is tarah sharm o hayaa karo jis tarah sharm o hayaa karne ka haq hai."

(Wasaail ush Shia, v1, p197)

🤲🏻

Imam Ali (as):

"Khudaya! Meine apne Nafs par Zulm kiya hai. Apni Jihalat se Jasarat ki hai aur mein is baat par Mutmain baitha hun ke Tu ne mujhe hamesha Yaad rakha aur hamesha Ehsaan farmaya hai. Khudaya! Mere kitne hi Aib hain jinhe Tu ne chhupaya hai, kitni hi Azeem Balayen hain jinse Tu ne bachaya hai, kitni hi thokre hain jin se Tu ne sanbhala hai, kitni hi Buraiyan hain jinhe Tu ne taala hai...."

(Dua-e-Kumail)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

     ♦ RAAH-E-BASEERAT ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1651)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

قُلۡ هَـٰذِهِۦ سَبِیلِیۤ أَدۡعُوۤا۟ إِلَى ٱللَّهِۚ عَلَىٰ بَصِیرَةٍ أَنَا۠ وَمَنِ ٱتَّبَعَنِیۖ وَسُبۡحَـٰنَ ٱللَّهِ وَمَاۤ أَنَا۠ مِنَ ٱلۡمُشۡرِكِینَ.

"Tum unse saaf keh do, ke mera Raasta to ye hai, mein Allah ki taraf Dawat deta hun, mein khud bhi Baseerat par hun aur jin logon ne meri Pairavi ki hai woh bhi Baseerat par hain aur Allah (Wahm o Khayalat se) Paak hai aur mera Mushrekin se waasta nahi hai."

(Surah Yusuf: 108)

https://youtu.be/rpymJzfL6x4

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Imam Mohd Baqir (as):

"Ayat عَلَىٰ بَصِیرَةٍ أَنَا۠ وَمَنِ ٱتَّبَعَنِی se Hazrat Rasoole Akram (saww), Hazrat Ali (as) aur doosre Ausiya murad hai."

(Usoole Kaafi, Rauzatul Waezeen, Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim, Noorus Saqlain)

👶

Imam Ali Naqi (as) se Raavi ne kaha: 'Mere Aaqa! Log Aapki kam sini ki wajah se Aap (as) par aitraz karte hain?'

Aap (as) ne farmaya:

"Is mein aitraz aur tajjub ki kya baat hai. Hazrat Ali (as) ne 9 Baras ki Umr mein Rasoole Khuda (saww) ki pairavi ki thi aur is waqt meri Umr bhi 9 Saal ki hai. Jab Hazrat Ali (as) ne AanHazrat (saww) ki pairavi ki to Allah ko unki pairavi ka andaz itna pasand aaya ke Allah ne farmaya: "Mein Khud bh Baseerat par hun aur meri Pairavi karnewala bhi Baseerat par hai."

(Usoole Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)

🙌🏻

Subhallah سُبحَانَ اللّٰه:

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Subhallah' ka matlab hai 'Khuda har Nuqs o Aib se Paak hai."

"Isse Khuda ki Tanzeeh murad hai."

(Usoole Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)

Means jo bhi ham Khuda ke bare mein soch sakte hain, har Sifaat se Munazzah hai. Yaani agar ham Allaho Akbar kehte hai to ham jaisa bhi bada sochte hai, Allah waisa Bada nahi, balke itna bada hai ke ham soch bhi nahi sakte.

🤲🏻

Imam Sadiq (as) se Roze Ghadeer ek Namaz manqool hai, iske baad ki Dua ye hai:

اَلدّاعِى اِلَيْكَ عَلَى بَصِيْرَةٍ وَ مَنِ اتَّبَعَهٗ.......

"Tu ne Rasool ko Apni Dawat Denewala bana kar bheja, woh khud bhi Baseerat par the aur unki pairavi karnewale bhi Baseerat par the."

(Tehzeeb ul Ahkam, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

  15th February 2021, Monday

♦ ZAMEEN PAR HUJJATE KHUDA ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1652)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَمَاۤ أَرۡسَلۡنَا مِن قَبۡلِكَ إِلَّا رِجَالࣰا نُّوحِیۤ إِلَیۡهِم مِّنۡ أَهۡلِ ٱلۡقُرَىٰۤۗ أَفَلَمۡ یَسِیرُوا۟ فِی ٱلۡأَرۡضِ فَیَنظُرُوا۟ كَیۡفَ كَانَ عَـٰقِبَةُ ٱلَّذِینَ مِن قَبۡلِهِمۡۗ وَلَدَارُ ٱلۡـَٔاخِرَةِ خَیۡرࣱ لِّلَّذِینَ ٱتَّقَوۡا۟ۚ أَفَلَا تَعۡقِلُونَ.

"Aye Muhammad (saww)! Tumse pehle Hamne jo Paighambar bheje the woh sab bhi Insaan hi the, aur unhi Bastiyon ke rehne walon mein se the aur unhi ki taraf Ham Wahy bhejte rahe hain, phir kya ye log Zameen par chale phire nahi hain ke un Qaumon ka Anjaam unhe nazar na aaya jo unse pehle guzar chuki hain? Yaqeenan Akherat ka ghar un logon ke liye aur zyada behtar hai Jinhone (Paighambaron ki baat maan kar) Taqwa ki Ravish ikhtiyar ki. Kya ab bhi tum log na samjhoge?"

(Surah Yusuf: 109)

https://youtu.be/rpymJzfL6x4

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Imam Reza (as):

"Kya tu nahi jaanta ke Allah ne apni Zameen ko Nabi ya Imam se khali nahi chhoda aur Nabi ya Imam ka talluq Insaano ki sinf (type) se hi hota hai jaisa ke Allah Ta'ala ne Farmaya: (12:109) Allah Ta'ala ne Zameen par Malaika ko kabhi Imam aur Haakim bana kar nahi bheja. Malaika ki duty ye hai ke woh Khuda ka Paigham Anbiya tak pahunchayen."

(Uyoonul Akhbar, Noorus Saqlain)

🕌

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

"Main hi Mahdi hun, main hi Qaim uz Zamaan hun, main hi zameen ko is tarah Adl o Insaaf se bhar dunga jis tarah wo Zulm o Jaur se bhar chuki hogi. Zameen Hujjat e Khuda se khaali nahi rehti."

(Guftaar e Dil Nasheen, p255)

🕌

Imam Kazim (as):

"Kul (tamaam) aadmiyo'n par Allah ki 2 Hujjaten hain, ek Hujjat e Zaahiri aur ek Hujjat e Baatini. Hujjat e Zaahiri to Rasool aur Anbiya aur Aimma e Masumeen (as) hain aur Hujjat e Baatini (inner) khud unki (aadmiyo'n) ki Aql hai."

(Irshadaat e Masumeen (as), p74)

🕌

Riwayat

Abu Ismail Sindhi ka bayaan hai ke "maine apne watan Hind mein suna ke Arab mein koi Hujjat e Khuda hai. Main unki talaash mein rawana ho gaya aur Imam Reza (as) ki khidmat mein haazir ho kar mulaqaat ka sharaf haasil kiya. Magar main Arabi (Arabic) zabaan se na-waaqif tha, is liye aap ko Sindhi zabaan mein Salaam kiya. Aap ne Sindhi zabaan hi mein jawaab diya. To maine aap se apni zabaan mein guftagu shuru ki aur Imam (as) barabar meri zabaan mein jawaab dete rahe. Maine arz kiya ke maine apne watan mein suna tha ke Arab mein koi Hujjat e Khuda hai, isliye main unki talaash mein nikla hun. Imam (as) ne farmaya, "Tum Hujjat e Khuda ke paas pahunch gaye, ab jo chaaho daryaft karo". Chunanche, maine bahut se Masail daryaft kiye aur mutmain ho gaya. Phir jab Aapki khidmat se rukhsat hone laga to arz kiya, "Huzoor! Main Arabi zabaan se na-waqif hun. Aap Allah se Dua farmaiye ke main Arabi bolne aur samajhne lagun taaki Ahle Arab se guftagu ke dauran sahulat ho jaaye". Ye sun kar Aapne mere Labon (lips) par haath phera, main usi waqt Arabi zabaan mein guftagu karne laga."

(Bihaar ul Anwaar, v5, p43)

🤲🏻

اَلسَّلَامُ عَلَيْكَ يَا حَجَّةَ اللّٰهِ فى الأرْضِهِ.

"Salam ho Aap par, aye Uski Zameen par Hujjat e Khuda (Imam Mahdi (atfs)."

(Ziyarat Roze Juma)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

          ♦ ILAAHI TA'EED ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1653)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

حَتَّىٰۤ إِذَا ٱسۡتَیۡـَٔسَ ٱلرُّسُلُ وَظَنُّوۤا۟ أَنَّهُمۡ قَدۡ كُذِبُوا۟ جَاۤءَهُمۡ نَصۡرُنَا فَنُجِّیَ مَن نَّشَاۤءُۖ وَلَا یُرَدُّ بَأۡسُنَا عَنِ ٱلۡقَوۡمِ ٱلۡمُجۡرِمِینَ.

"(Pehle Paighambaron ke saath bhi yehi hota raha hai ke woh muddaton Nasihat karte rahe aur logon ne na suna) yahan tak ke jab Paighambar logon se mayoos ho gaye aur logon ne bhi samajh liya ke unse Jhoot bola gaya tha, to yakayak hamari madad Paighambaron ko pahunch gayi phir jab aisa mauqa aa jata hai to Hamara qaeda ye hai ke jise ham chahte hain bacha lete hain aur Mujrimon par se Hamara Azaab taala hi nahi ja sakta."

(Surah Yusuf: 110)

https://youtu.be/rpymJzfL6x4

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Mamoom Al Rasheed ne Imam Reza (as) se kaha: 'Is Ayat mein Anbiya ki Ismat kahan hai? Is mein to aisa likha hai ke Anbiya ne samajh liya ke unse Jhoot kaha gaya?'

Imam (as) ne farmaya:

"Tumhe ghalat fehmi hui hai. وَظَنُّوۤا۟ Fe'l فعل (Verb) ke Fa'el فاعل (Subject) Anbiya nahi hain, isse unki Qaumen murad hain. Maqsade Ayat ya hai ke Anbiya (as) ki Qaumen ye guman karne lagi ke Anbiya ki Zabani unse Jhoot kaha gaya hai to us waqt Hamari Madad nazil hui."

(Kitab Uyoonul Akhbar, Noorus Saqlain)

📚

Is Ayat ka tasalsul guzishta Ayaat se wabasta hai. Ye Concluding Verses hain.

Anbiya (as) ne Hidayat ka kaam jari rakha aur kafi musibat o mushaqqat ka saamna karna pada. Anbiya (as) ki itni Tableegh ke bawajood jab Qaum o Ummat par koi asar na hua balke ulta ye soch mein pad gayi ke kya ye Nabi sach bhi keh raha hai ya nahi. Jaise aaj ke Zamane mein bhi log is shak mein hain ke kya Imam Mahdi (atfs) waqai mein Zinda hain? Ya aajkal kuchh log Maulvi par hi shak karne lagte hai ke ye Mimber par se kya keh raha hai (Jab Maulvi ki baat sahih hoti hai). Jab ye nobat aa jaati hai to Allah Khud is masle mein Haq ki madad karta hai.

Qur'an ki ek misal arz hai ke jab Rasoole Khuda (saww) Ghaar (Cave) mein poshida the aur agar awaaz hoti to Kuffar ko pata chal jata aur mushkil badh jati. Rasool (saww) ka Munafiq saathi rone laga. Allah ko is wajah se aur security badhane padi. (Tauba:40) Usko bhi saath mein Allah ke Hukm se isiliye rakha tha taake Munafiq Kafir se mil kar Rasool (saww) ke Plan mein rakhna na dale. Maqsad ye hai ke aise mauqe par Allah ki Taeed (Support) jaari rehti hai.

🤲🏻

وَحُفَّهُ بِمَلَآئِكَتِكَ الْمُقَرَّبِيْنَ، وَاَيِّدْهُ بِرُوْحِ الْقُدُسِ يَا رَبَّ الْعَالَمِيْنَ، اَللّٰهُمَّ اجْعَلْهُ الدَّاعِيَ اِلٰى كِتَابِكَ، وَالْقَاۤئِمَ بِدِيْنِكَ،.......

"Jinse (Imam Mahdi atfs) Ummeeden wabasta hain, jinki aamad ka Intezaar hai, unhe Apne Malaika e Muqarrabin ke halqe mein rakh, Roohul Quds ke zariye unki ta'eed farma, Aye Alameen ka Parwardigar."

(Dua-e-Iftetah)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

🔸🔸🔸🔸🔸🔸🔸🔸🔸🔸

SHIA CHANNEL WELCOMES YOU

**********************************

         4th Mahe Rajab 1442

17th February 2021, Wednesday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

         ♦ IBRAT (LESSON) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1654)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

لَقَدۡ كَانَ فِی قَصَصِهِمۡ عِبۡرَةࣱ لِّأُو۟لِی ٱلۡأَلۡبَـٰبِۗ مَا كَانَ حَدِیثࣰا یُفۡتَرَىٰ وَلَـٰكِن تَصۡدِیقَ ٱلَّذِی بَیۡنَ یَدَیۡهِ وَتَفۡصِیلَ كُلِّ شَیۡءࣲ وَهُدࣰى وَرَحۡمَةࣰ لِّقَوۡمࣲ یُؤۡمِنُونَ.

"Aql o hosh rakhne walon ke liye inke Waqeat mein Ibrat ka Samaan maujood hai. Jo kuchh Qur'an mein bayan kiya ja raha hai ye banaoti baten nahi hain balke jo Kitaben isse pehle aa chuki hain ye unhi ki tasdeeq hai aur Qur'an har cheez ki Tafseel aur Ahle Imaan ke liye saraspa Hidayat o Rehmat hai."

(Surah Yusuf: 111)

https://youtu.be/rpymJzfL6x4

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Ye Ayat is Surah ki Concluding Ayat hai, ek Jame Khulasa hai. Hazrat Yusuf (as) ke saath saath doosre Anbiya (as) ki Sarguzish jo in do Surah Hud wa Surah Yusuf mein bayan hui, ye Sahabane Aql ke liye wo Aeena (Mirror) hai jis mein unki Fatah o Shikst, Kamyabi o Nakaami, Khubakhti wa Badbakhti, Surbulandi wa Zillat sab kuchh dekhi ja sakti hai. Ye wo Aeena hai jis mein guzishta Qaumon aur Azeem Rehbaron ke tamam Tajarbaat ka ma-hasl nazar aata hai. Ye aisa Aeena hai ke jiska Mushaheda kam Umr wale Insaan ko tamam Aalam e Bashariyyat ke Umr ke barabar Tulaani Zindagi wala bana deta hai.

Lekin sirf Sahebane Aql o Fahm o Fikr hi hain jo is Ajeeb o Ghareeb Aeene se in Nuqoose Ibrat ko dekh sakte hain.

Ye koi Story-telling, Kahani, ya Afsana nahi, Haqeeqat par mabni Tarikh (History) hai jisko Allah bayan kar raha hai. Agar tab bhi koi Lesson hasil na kar sake to woh Jahil o Diwana hi ho sakta hai.

(End of Surah e Yusuf) 

📚

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Zalzale (earthquakes) aur oos jaise doosre azaab (jaise toofan, sailaab / floods) insaan ke liye nasihat hain, taaki log ibrat (lesson) haasil karein aur gunaho'n se parhez karein."

(Aasmani Nasihatein, v2, p200)

📚

Rasule Khuda (saww):

"Logo'n mein sabse zyada ghaafil (negligent) wo hai jo Duniya ke badalte haalaat se sabak (lesson) nahi leta."

(Nahjul Fasaha)

📚

Imam Ali (as):

"Momin duniya ko ibrat (lesson) ki nigaah se dekhta hai aur utni hi giza haasil karta hai jiske liye shikam ki zarurat usay majboor karti hai."

(Meezan ul Hikmah, v6, p53)

🤲🏻

اَلسَّلَامُ عَلَيْكَ وَ عَلَى الْاَئِمَّةِ مِنْ ذُرِّيَّتِكَ وَ بَنِيْكَ اَشْهَدُ لَقَدْ طَيَّبَ اللّٰهُ بِكَ التُّرَابَ وَ اَوْضَحَ بِكَ الْكِتَابَ وَ جَعَلَكَ وَ اَبَاكَ وَ جَدَّكَ وَ اَخَاكَ وَ بَنِيْكَ عِبْرَةً لِاُوْلِي الْاَلْبَابِ.......

(Ziyarat-e-Imam Husain (as) - Mafateeh)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

THE END
